### Returning to Septimus

The Oghma Infinium

Upon acquiring different blood samples, you will be prompted to return to Septimus Signus's Outpost. Give the blood samples to Septimus and wait for him to open the cube. Following him inside will reveal, much to the surprise of the delusional quest giver, that it was not the "Heart of a God" that was stored inside the cube, but rather a book. His surprise is cut short as his usefulness to Hermaeus Mora has been outlived and he is promptly disposed of in a flash of light.

It is revealed that the book on a pedestal is actually the *[Oghma Infinium](/wiki/Skyrim:Oghma_Infinium "Skyrim:Oghma Infinium")*. Hermaeus Mora will greet you again, calling you his champion. You can reply with "What now?" or "I am not your champion, monster." Again, there are no consequences to the completion of this quest with either choice. Through conversation with the Daedric prince, you learn that it was sealed here for a reason, so that no more of its dangerous knowledge could be shared with the world of mortals—something that Hermaeus Mora wishes undone.

At this point, the quest is complete. Reading the book will reveal some of the knowledge hidden within. Specifically, you can choose from three different paths: magic, shadow, or might, and receive +5 permanent points in the following skills, depending on the choice:

:   **The Path of Might:** Archery, Block, Heavy Armor, One-handed, Smithing, Two-handed
:   **The Path of Shadow:** Alchemy, Light Armor, Lockpicking, Pickpocket, Sneak, Speech
:   **The Path of Magic:** Alteration, Conjuration, Destruction, Enchanting, Illusion, Restoration

## Notes

- You will automatically start this quest during the course of [Elder Knowledge](/wiki/Skyrim:Elder_Knowledge "Skyrim:Elder Knowledge") or [Scroll Scouting](/wiki/Skyrim:Scroll_Scouting "Skyrim:Scroll Scouting")[DG](/wiki/Skyrim:Dawnguard "Skyrim:Dawnguard") if you have not already started it, as the Elder Scroll is required for both the main questline and for the Dawnguard core questline. This quest does not have to be completed in order to complete either questline, however.
- After opening the cube, leaving [Septimus Signus's Outpost](/wiki/Skyrim:Septimus_Signus%27s_Outpost "Skyrim:Septimus Signus's Outpost") and letting the cell respawn will cause the dwemer puzzle door to close permanently, potentially locking in the Oghma Infinium.
- You don't have to access [Blackreach](/wiki/Skyrim:Blackreach "Skyrim:Blackreach") through [Alftand](/wiki/Skyrim:Alftand "Skyrim:Alftand"), as it's also possible to reach it through the two other linked Dwemer ruins, [Raldbthar](/wiki/Skyrim:Raldbthar "Skyrim:Raldbthar") and  [Mzinchaleft](/wiki/Skyrim:Mzinchaleft "Skyrim:Mzinchaleft"), by using the sphere given by Septimus on the apparatus at the end of these dungeons.
- The "Heart of a God" to which Septimus refers is actually the [Heart of Lorkhan](/wiki/Lore:Heart_of_Lorkhan "Lore:Heart of Lorkhan"). However, there is no Heart inside the chamber.
- The retrieved Elder Scroll can be sold to [Urag gro-Shub](/wiki/Skyrim:Urag_gro-Shub "Skyrim:Urag gro-Shub") in the College of Winterhold's Arcanaeum for 2000 gold. However, do not do so until you have completed [Alduin's Bane](/wiki/Skyrim:Alduin%27s_Bane "Skyrim:Alduin's Bane"), as it is essential to the main quest. If *[Dawnguard](/wiki/Skyrim:Dawnguard "Skyrim:Dawnguard")* is installed, the Elder Scroll is also needed to complete its [main questline](/wiki/Skyrim:Dawnguard_Quests#Main_Quests "Skyrim:Dawnguard Quests"), though you can buy it back from Urag if you have already sold it to him.
- If you give the lexicon to Septimus before reaching level 15, it may be necessary to wait for a [letter](/wiki/Skyrim:Letter_from_Septimus_Signus "Skyrim:Letter from Septimus Signus") from him to arrive via courier. Simply returning to him when you reach that level will not work.
- Corpses fed on while in Beast Form or with the [Ring of Namira](/wiki/Skyrim:Ring_of_Namira "Skyrim:Ring of Namira") cannot be harvested for blood. Avoid feeding on the named elven corpses inside Alftand as you will have to find samples in other, potentially far apart, locations. However, if *Dawnguard* is installed, you may be able to harvest corpses while in Beast Form, as long as you have advanced far enough in the quest to have been given the extractor.
- You can keep the Oghma Infinium after use by dropping it before exiting the inventory upon its initial use, however, it will only be a book, and will not grant the bonuses again. Otherwise it will disappear after you use it.
- If *[Dragonborn](/wiki/Skyrim:Dragonborn "Skyrim:Dragonborn")* is installed, Hermaeus Mora will not be represented as a large purple shape. Instead, he is shown as the tentacled form seen during the quests of the DLC. If you have completed the *Dragonborn* quest line before speaking to Mora in this quest, he will use unique dialogue referring to the events of *Dragonborn*.
- You can't harvest your own blood if your character is elven.
  - You also can't harvest the blood of any of the [Snow Elves](/wiki/Skyrim:Snow_Elf "Skyrim:Snow Elf") encountered in the *Dawnguard* quest line.
- As of version 2.0.1 of the [Unofficial Skyrim Patch](/wiki/Skyrim_Mod:Unofficial_Skyrim_Patch "Skyrim Mod:Unofficial Skyrim Patch"), this quest appears to have lost several properties due to unknown causes, possibly from bad official patches that have since been undone. Not many people seem to have been affected by this so it may have been caused by a Steam beta patch that went bad and was quickly corrected. These properties will now be restored allowing the quest to be completed.

## Bugs

- The [Attunement Sphere](/wiki/Skyrim:Attunement_Sphere "Skyrim:Attunement Sphere") and [Runed Lexicon](/wiki/Skyrim:Runed_Lexicon "Skyrim:Runed Lexicon") are still considered quest items after the quest completion and therefore cannot be removed from inventory. Since the Sphere is not removed during the quest it will stay forever in inventory. The Runed Lexicon is correctly removed during quest and will be stuck only if you pickpocket/loot it back from Septimus Signus.
  -  The [Unofficial Skyrim Patch](/wiki/Skyrim_Mod:Unofficial_Skyrim_Patch "Skyrim Mod:Unofficial Skyrim Patch"), version 1.0, addresses this issue. Both objects will not be quest items anymore upon quest completition
  -  The console commands `player.removeitem 3a3dd 1` and `player.removeitem 3532c 1` can be used to remove both items from inventory.
- Septimus is supposed to be lifted into the air and turned into ashes after approaching the Oghma Infinium book and saying the final line. However, there is a bug where the event is sometimes not triggered due to a bad animation registration event which then makes the quest impossible to complete.
  -  The [Unofficial Skyrim Patch](/wiki/Skyrim_Mod:Unofficial_Skyrim_Patch "Skyrim Mod:Unofficial Skyrim Patch"), version 1.3.2, fixes this bug.
  - The most reliable solution to this problem is to kill Septimus. Once the quest has progressed to where he should be dead, killing him does not count as a crime.
  - Alternatively, reload an earlier save (before giving the blood to Septimus). If inside, exit the cave and wait for an hour while outside before re-entering. This can fix the event to trigger normally.
- If you kill Septimus right after he gives you the stage to harvest blood, you will fail the quest, but the game will still prompt you with the "Harvest blood" option every time you loot the corpses of Orcs or elves.
  -  The [Unofficial Skyrim Patch](/wiki/Skyrim_Mod:Unofficial_Skyrim_Patch "Skyrim Mod:Unofficial Skyrim Patch"), version 2.0.0, fixes this bug.
- You may not have the "Harvest blood" option despite having the Essence Extractor in your inventory.
  -  The [Unofficial Skyrim Patch](/wiki/Skyrim_Mod:Unofficial_Skyrim_Patch "Skyrim Mod:Unofficial Skyrim Patch"), version 2.0.1, fixes this bug.
  -  Use the console command `player.addperk 79af5`.
- If you are finding the Elder Scroll for a [Dawnguard](/wiki/Skyrim:Dawnguard "Skyrim:Dawnguard") quest, the journal entry will still say "Find the Elder Scroll for Paarthurnax" even if you have never met him.
  -  The [Unofficial Dawnguard Patch](/wiki/Skyrim_Mod:Unofficial_Dawnguard_Patch "Skyrim Mod:Unofficial Dawnguard Patch"), version 1.1.2, fixes this bug.
- If you remove the Elder Scroll before the Blank Lexicon is transcribed, you may be unable to proceed with the quest.
  - Also, it is possible that if you remove the scroll without retrieving the lexicon, you will not "discover" the Tower of Mzark, and you will not be able to fast travel there. This can be remedied by fast travel to Fort Dunstad and following the trail SSW. The gates will still be open to the Tower of Mzark, and you can retrieve the lexicon.
- A second [Attunement Sphere](/wiki/Skyrim:Attunement_Sphere "Skyrim:Attunement Sphere") can be found in [Sinderion's Field Laboratory](/wiki/Skyrim:Sinderion%27s_Field_Laboratory "Skyrim:Sinderion's Field Laboratory"); having both spheres at any time in inventory will leave both permanently stuck there.
  - Pick up the non-quest one and remove it from inventory before starting the quest.

:   -  The console command `player.removeitem 3532c 2` can be used to remove both items from inventory, however this is not recommended beacuse you cannot acquire any more Attunement Sphere, blocking potential [Blackreach](/wiki/Skyrim:Blackreach "Skyrim:Blackreach") entrances. See [Mzinchaleft](/wiki/Skyrim:Mzinchaleft "Skyrim:Mzinchaleft") and [Raldbthar](/wiki/Skyrim:Raldbthar "Skyrim:Raldbthar") for more.

- If you run fast enough, you can leave the cube after acquiring the Oghma Infinium before Hermaeus Mora blocks the passage. This will leave the quest unfinished despite all the objectives being completed and you will not be able to get the Oghma Infinium's bonuses.
  - Speak to Hermaeus Mora from behind to resume and correctly end the quest scripts.
- After Septimus is killed, picking up the Oghma Infinium may not trigger the next stage of the quest and Hermaeus Mora may not appear in the passageway. **?**

:   -  The console command `setstage DA04 60` can be used to make Hermaeus Mora appear, if not, continue with next line.
    -  The console command `setstage DA04 100` can be used to advance the quest manually.

- Despite having the blank lexicon in inventory, you might not be able to activate the stand.[[1]](http://www.gamesas.com/transcribe-lexicon-glitch-t344378.html) This blocks progress on this quest and [Elder Knowledge](/wiki/Skyrim:Elder_Knowledge "Skyrim:Elder Knowledge"), and is caused by the game forgetting the reference to the quest item. **?**

:   -  Add the Runed Lexicon to your inventory using the console command `player.additem 3a3dd 1`, and remove the blank with `player.removeitem 3a3d2 1`.

- Even after you finish the quest, the items in Septimus Signus's Outpost may still be marked as owned by him. **?**
- Attempting to leave Septimus Signus's Outpost before speaking to the Wretched Abyss may cause it to persist but not continue the dialogue, making the quest unable to be completed. **?**
  -  The console command `resetquest DA04` can be used to reset your progress in this quest, followed by `setstage DA04 40` which will then advance the quest manually.
- If you don't take the Elder Scroll and eventually go on to end the quest without doing so, it becomes impossible to take the scroll later due to the activator being set for an alias in this quest.
  - The [Unofficial Skyrim Special Edition Patch](/wiki/Skyrim_Mod:Unofficial_Skyrim_Special_Edition_Patch "Skyrim Mod:Unofficial Skyrim Special Edition Patch"), version 4.1.4, addresses this issue. The activator is instead set to use the alias in [Elder Knowledge](/wiki/Skyrim:Elder_Knowledge "Skyrim:Elder Knowledge") to get the scroll since Elder Knowledge is a background quest that is never terminated during the life of the game.

## Quest Stages

| Discerning the Transmundane (DA04) | | |
| --- | --- | --- |
| Stage | Finishes Quest | Journal Entry |
| 5 |  | I've been given a book of bizarre ramblings about Elder Scrolls, written by Septimus Signus. He claims to have spent time at the Winterhold Arcanaeum. *Objective 5:* Ask Urag about the insane book |

He doesn't care about the Scroll itself, but wants me to use some kind of machine there to inscribe a dwarven lexicon with the Scroll's knowledge and bring it to him. *Objective 20:* Transcribe the Lexicon |

| 40 |  | I met Septimus Signus and brought him a dwarven lexicon containing the distilled knowledge of an Elder Scroll. With it, he believes he can open the lockbox he's been studying by creating a mixture of blood that will resemble dwarven. I need to collect blood from several different races if I want to help him. *Objective 41:* Harvest High Elf blood  *Objective 42:* Harvest Wood Elf blood  *Objective 43:* Harvest Dark Elf blood  *Objective 44:* Harvest Falmer blood  *Objective 45:* Harvest Orc blood |

I helped him open it. It did not contain what he had expected, but instead a book of great knowledge, the Oghma Infinium. |
| 105 | ☒ | I met and killed a strange hermit named Septimus Signus, who needed the knowledge of an Elder Scroll and a collection of blood to open a dwarven lockbox he had studied for years. |

Notes

- Any text displayed in angle brackets (e.g., `<Alias=LocationHold>`) is dynamically set by the Radiant Quest system, and will be filled in with the appropriate word(s) when seen in game.
- Not all Journal Entries may appear in your journal; which entries appear and which entries do not depends on the manner in which the quest is done.
- Stages are not always in order of progress. This is usually the case with quests that have multiple possible outcomes or quests where certain tasks may be done in any order. Some stages may therefore repeat objectives seen in other stages.
- If an entry is marked as "Finishes Quest" it means the quest disappears from the Active Quest list, but you may still receive new entries for that quest.
- On the PC, it is possible to use the [console](/wiki/Skyrim:Console "Skyrim:Console") to advance through the quest by entering `setstage DA04 stage`, where `stage` is the number of the stage you wish to complete. It is not possible to un-complete (i.e. go back) quest stages, but it is possible to clear all stages of the quest using `resetquest DA04`.

Dishonored Skald

The **Dishonored Skald** is a [Nord](/wiki/Skyrim:Nord "Skyrim:Nord") [warrior](/wiki/Skyrim:Warrior_(class) "Skyrim:Warrior (class)") who may appear in the [Bards College](/wiki/Skyrim:Bards_College "Skyrim:Bards College") in [Solitude](/wiki/Skyrim:Solitude "Skyrim:Solitude") during the quest [The Dark Brotherhood Forever](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Dark_Brotherhood_Forever "Skyrim:The Dark Brotherhood Forever"). He will only be enabled if the [Night Mother](/wiki/Skyrim:Night_Mother "Skyrim:Night Mother") picks him as the contract giver.

He will be chosen randomly from a list of ten people who performed the Black Sacrament and want someone killed. When approached, he will choose between a total of ten possible targets, hand you a leveled amount of gold and blindly expect you to carry out the task.

He wears a set of [iron armor](/wiki/Skyrim:Iron_Armor "Skyrim:Iron Armor"), including the [gauntlets](/wiki/Skyrim:Iron_Gauntlets "Skyrim:Iron Gauntlets") and [boots](/wiki/Skyrim:Iron_Boots "Skyrim:Iron Boots"). He also wields an [iron warhammer](/wiki/Skyrim:Iron_Warhammer "Skyrim:Iron Warhammer") and carries a copy of [*A Kiss, Sweet Mother*](/wiki/Skyrim:A_Kiss,_Sweet_Mother "Skyrim:A Kiss, Sweet Mother").

He shares his dialogue with the nine other potential quest givers; see [this section](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Dark_Brotherhood_Forever#Detailed_Walkthrough "Skyrim:The Dark Brotherhood Forever") for details.

## Related Quests

- **[The Dark Brotherhood Forever](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Dark_Brotherhood_Forever "Skyrim:The Dark Brotherhood Forever")**: Yet another child has prayed to their [mother](/wiki/Skyrim:Night_Mother "Skyrim:Night Mother").

# Skyrim:Distant Memories

## Overview

|  |
| --- |
| **This page is currently being rewritten as part of the [Skyrim Quest Redesign Project](/wiki/UESPWiki:Skyrim_Quest_Redesign_Project "UESPWiki:Skyrim Quest Redesign Project").** The page is being rewritten and checked in several stages. All users are welcome to make changes to the page. If you make a change that is relevant to the project, please update this template accordingly, and make sure you have observed the [project guidelines](/wiki/UESPWiki:Skyrim_Quest_Redesign_Project#Guidelines "UESPWiki:Skyrim Quest Redesign Project"). The waterlogged chest

## Quick Walkthrough

1. Speak to [Brand-Shei](/wiki/Skyrim:Brand-Shei "Skyrim:Brand-Shei").
2. Find [Lymdrenn Tenvanni's Journal](/wiki/Skyrim:Lymdrenn_Tenvanni%27s_Journal "Skyrim:Lymdrenn Tenvanni's Journal") in [Wreck of The Pride of Tel Vos](/wiki/Skyrim:Wreck_of_The_Pride_of_Tel_Vos "Skyrim:Wreck of The Pride of Tel Vos").
3. Take the journal to Brand-Shei.

## Detailed Walkthrough

[Brand-Shei](/wiki/Skyrim:Brand-Shei "Skyrim:Brand-Shei") is a [Dark Elf](/wiki/Skyrim:Dark_Elf "Skyrim:Dark Elf") trader in [Riften](/wiki/Skyrim:Riften "Skyrim:Riften"). He can usually be found at his stall at the market, or in a cell in the [Riften Jail](/wiki/Skyrim:Riften_Jail "Skyrim:Riften Jail") if you've helped [Brynjolf](/wiki/Skyrim:Brynjolf "Skyrim:Brynjolf") frame him for theft. As a [Dunmer](/wiki/Skyrim:Dark_Elf "Skyrim:Dark Elf"), he has an oddly [Argonian](/wiki/Skyrim:Argonian "Skyrim:Argonian") name (such as [Beem-Ja](/wiki/Skyrim:Beem-Ja "Skyrim:Beem-Ja"), [Gulum-Ei](/wiki/Skyrim:Gulum-Ei "Skyrim:Gulum-Ei"), [Talen-Jei](/wiki/Skyrim:Talen-Jei "Skyrim:Talen-Jei")). In fact, he was raised Argonian. *"I ended up orphaned then taken in by a kindly Argonian family in [Black Marsh](/wiki/Lore:Black_Marsh "Lore:Black Marsh")."* He hopes one day to find out what happened to him and he has got one clue. When he was found by his Argonian father, he was wrapped in a blanket bearing the symbol of [House Telvanni](/wiki/Lore:House_Telvanni "Lore:House Telvanni"), one of the great houses in [Morrowind](/wiki/Lore:Morrowind "Lore:Morrowind") long ago. He'd like you to keep an eye on anything that might provide him with the answers he is looking for in your travels. If you ask him why was he searching in Skyrim, he will tell you something about a matron who had served for House Telvanni and remind you to investigate a ship named "[The Pride of Tel Vos](/wiki/Skyrim:Wreck_of_The_Pride_of_Tel_Vos "Skyrim:Wreck of The Pride of Tel Vos")".

Travel to the northeast coast of Skyrim and you can find the wreck of The Pride of Tel Vos. A group of three [bandits](/wiki/Skyrim:Bandit "Skyrim:Bandit") have a camp here. However, you can hide yourself from them easily. You can also choose to wipe them out and take their treasures. In the northern half of the ship at the waterline, you can find a waterlogged chest containing the item you need: [Lymdrenn Tenvanni's Journal](/wiki/Skyrim:Lymdrenn_Tenvanni%27s_Journal "Skyrim:Lymdrenn Tenvanni's Journal"). This journal would be the key to the answers Brand-Shei is looking for.

Return to Brand-Shei and give the book to him. He will be very excited. *"Yes... yes. This is it! I don't know how you found this stranger, but you've obviously succeeded where I had failed."* Then he will offer you the key to his strongbox under his stand in the marketplace. You are free to take anything inside, including some [gems](/wiki/Skyrim:Gems "Skyrim:Gems"), [potions](/wiki/Skyrim:Potions "Skyrim:Potions"), and a random novice level [Destruction](/wiki/Skyrim:Destruction "Skyrim:Destruction") [spell tome](/wiki/Skyrim:Spell_Tomes "Skyrim:Spell Tomes").

## Notes

- This quest can be completed by finding the journal in the wreck first, then talking to Brand-Shei afterward.
- Since the lockbox's contents are leveled, the [Prowler's Profit](/wiki/Skyrim:Prowler%27s_Profit "Skyrim:Prowler's Profit") perk will give you more value.
- After completion of this quest, some items in Haelga's Bunkhouse will be free to take, as this is Brand-Shei's residence at the start of the game.

## Bugs

- Brand-Shei's journal may not appear in the chest, even when the quest marker points to it. **?**
  - This can be fixed using the console command `setstage FreeFormRiften08 30`.
- If Brand-Shei's still in Jail when player try to give his journal, his dialogue might stuck on "This City is Corrupt, etc. **?**
  - Try to wait until Brand-Shei's get out from Jail, or
  - If you using PC, use console to fix this glitch. (1) Prid 19ddc, then (2) Say e829b
- Brand-Shei's dialogue topic about the mystery of his birth no longer makes sense after you give him his journal during this quest.
  -  The [Unofficial Skyrim Patch](/wiki/Skyrim_Mod:Unofficial_Skyrim_Patch "Skyrim Mod:Unofficial Skyrim Patch"), version 2.1.2, addresses this issue. A condition check has been added to make that topic unavailable when this quest is finished.
- Although unconfirmed, it's likely that the name of the journal's author, Lymdrenn Te**n**vanni, is misspelled and should be Te**l**vanni.
  -  The [Unofficial Skyrim Patch](/wiki/Skyrim_Mod:Unofficial_Skyrim_Patch "Skyrim Mod:Unofficial Skyrim Patch"), version 1.0, fixes this bug.

- Any text displayed in angle brackets (e.g., `<Alias=LocationHold>`) is dynamically set by the Radiant Quest system, and will be filled in with the appropriate word(s) when seen in game.
- Not all Journal Entries may appear in your journal; which entries appear and which entries do not depends on the manner in which the quest is done.
- Stages are not always in order of progress. This is usually the case with quests that have multiple possible outcomes or quests where certain tasks may be done in any order. Some stages may therefore repeat objectives seen in other stages.
- If an entry is marked as "Finishes Quest" it means the quest disappears from the Active Quest list, but you may still receive new entries for that quest.
- On the PC, it is possible to use the [console](/wiki/Skyrim:Console "Skyrim:Console") to advance through the quest by entering `setstage FreeformRiften08 stage`, where `stage` is the number of the stage you wish to complete. It is not possible to un-complete (i.e. go back) quest stages, but it is possible to clear all stages of the quest using `resetquest FreeformRiften08`.

# Skyrim:Divine Quests

## Overview

These **quests** involve the **[Eight Divines](/wiki/Lore:Eight_Divines "Lore:Eight Divines")**.

- **[Kyne's Sacred Trials](/wiki/Skyrim:Kyne%27s_Sacred_Trials "Skyrim:Kyne's Sacred Trials")**: Participate in [Kyne](/wiki/Lore:Kyne "Lore:Kyne")'s Sacred Trials by hunting the guardian beasts of [Skyrim](/wiki/Skyrim:Skyrim "Skyrim:Skyrim").
- **[The Blessings of Nature](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Blessings_of_Nature "Skyrim:The Blessings of Nature")**: Restore the [Gildergreen](/wiki/Lore:Gildergreen "Lore:Gildergreen") for [Danica Pure-Spring](/wiki/Skyrim:Danica_Pure-Spring "Skyrim:Danica Pure-Spring").
- **[The Book of Love](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Book_of_Love "Skyrim:The Book of Love")**: Help the [Temple of Mara](/wiki/Skyrim:Temple_of_Mara "Skyrim:Temple of Mara") spread the cause of love throughout Skyrim.
- **[The Heart of Dibella](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Heart_of_Dibella "Skyrim:The Heart of Dibella")**: Find a new [Sybil](/wiki/Skyrim:Fjotra "Skyrim:Fjotra") for the [Temple of Dibella](/wiki/Skyrim:Temple_of_Dibella "Skyrim:Temple of Dibella").

# Skyrim:Divine Quests

## Overview

These **quests** involve the **[Eight Divines](/wiki/Lore:Eight_Divines "Lore:Eight Divines")**.

- **[Kyne's Sacred Trials](/wiki/Skyrim:Kyne%27s_Sacred_Trials "Skyrim:Kyne's Sacred Trials")**: Participate in [Kyne](/wiki/Lore:Kyne "Lore:Kyne")'s Sacred Trials by hunting the guardian beasts of [Skyrim](/wiki/Skyrim:Skyrim "Skyrim:Skyrim").
- **[The Blessings of Nature](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Blessings_of_Nature "Skyrim:The Blessings of Nature")**: Restore the [Gildergreen](/wiki/Lore:Gildergreen "Lore:Gildergreen") for [Danica Pure-Spring](/wiki/Skyrim:Danica_Pure-Spring "Skyrim:Danica Pure-Spring").
- **[The Book of Love](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Book_of_Love "Skyrim:The Book of Love")**: Help the [Temple of Mara](/wiki/Skyrim:Temple_of_Mara "Skyrim:Temple of Mara") spread the cause of love throughout Skyrim.
- **[The Heart of Dibella](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Heart_of_Dibella "Skyrim:The Heart of Dibella")**: Find a new [Sybil](/wiki/Skyrim:Fjotra "Skyrim:Fjotra") for the [Temple of Dibella](/wiki/Skyrim:Temple_of_Dibella "Skyrim:Temple of Dibella").

Donnel

**Donnel** is an [elderly](/wiki/Skyrim:Elder "Skyrim:Elder") [witchblade](/wiki/Skyrim:Witchblade "Skyrim:Witchblade") who lives and works at [The Treasury House](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Treasury_House "Skyrim:The Treasury House") in [Markarth](/wiki/Skyrim:Markarth "Skyrim:Markarth"). He and [Nana Ildene](/wiki/Skyrim:Nana_Ildene "Skyrim:Nana Ildene") clean the house. They both show their [true selves](/wiki/Skyrim:Forsworn "Skyrim:Forsworn") during the related [quest](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Forsworn_Conspiracy "Skyrim:The Forsworn Conspiracy").

Donnel can always be found sweeping the floor at the foot of the northeastern set of stairs. He never sleeps or eats, and will only leave his spot and reveal his true intentions after you have questioned [Thonar](/wiki/Skyrim:Thonar_Silver-Blood "Skyrim:Thonar Silver-Blood").

He wears a set of farm [clothes](/wiki/Skyrim:Clothing#000209a6 "Skyrim:Clothing") and a pair of [boots](/wiki/Skyrim:Clothing#000209a5 "Skyrim:Clothing"), and is equipped with a [steel dagger](/wiki/Skyrim:Steel_Dagger "Skyrim:Steel Dagger"). He carries a [key](/wiki/Skyrim:Key_to_Markarth_Treasury_House "Skyrim:Key to Markarth Treasury House") to the Treasury House and a selection of [lower-class loot and gold](/wiki/Skyrim:Leveled_Lists#Poor "Skyrim:Leveled Lists"). To aid him in combat, Donnel knows the spells [Oakflesh](/wiki/Skyrim:Oakflesh "Skyrim:Oakflesh"), [Raise Zombie](/wiki/Skyrim:Raise_Zombie "Skyrim:Raise Zombie"), and [Flames](/wiki/Skyrim:Flames "Skyrim:Flames").

## Related Quests

- **[The Forsworn Conspiracy](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Forsworn_Conspiracy "Skyrim:The Forsworn Conspiracy")**: Investigate a murder in [Markarth](/wiki/Skyrim:Markarth "Skyrim:Markarth") to discover a sinister plot surrounding the [Forsworn](/wiki/Skyrim:Forsworn "Skyrim:Forsworn").

### The Forsworn Conspiracy

After questioning Thonar he, along with [Nana](/wiki/Skyrim:Nana_Ildene "Skyrim:Nana Ildene"), will then proceed to attack you and anyone else in the Treasury House.

## Dialogue

When spoken to he will only say:

:   *"I work for the Silver-Bloods. Help clean."*
:   *"Just here to work."*

## Notes

- Donnel's death can be avoided by pickpocketing and reading [Thonar's](/wiki/Skyrim:Thonar%27s_Journal "Skyrim:Thonar's Journal") or [Nepos's journal](/wiki/Skyrim:Nepos%27s_Journal "Skyrim:Nepos's Journal") instead of questioning them, then going directly to [Eltrys](/wiki/Skyrim:Eltrys "Skyrim:Eltrys").
  - Alternatively, it can be avoided by going directly to Eltrys after questioning [Nepos the Nose](/wiki/Skyrim:Nepos_the_Nose "Skyrim:Nepos the Nose").

# Skyrim:Doorman

## Overview

| Doorman (RefID: [xx](/wiki/Skyrim:Form_ID "Skyrim:Form ID")008BF3) | | | |
| --- | --- | --- | --- |
| Added by | [Dawnguard](/wiki/Skyrim:Dawnguard "Skyrim:Dawnguard") | | |
| Location | [Redwater Den](/wiki/Skyrim:Redwater_Den "Skyrim:Redwater Den") | | |

| [Faction(s)](/wiki/Skyrim:Factions "Skyrim:Factions") | [DLC1dunRedwaterDenFaction](/wiki/Skyrim:DLC1dunRedwaterDenFaction "Skyrim:DLC1dunRedwaterDenFaction") | | |

Doorman

The **Doorman** is a [Nord](/wiki/Skyrim:Nord "Skyrim:Nord") [bandit](/wiki/Skyrim:Bandit_(class) "Skyrim:Bandit (class)") found inside [Redwater Den](/wiki/Skyrim:Redwater_Den "Skyrim:Redwater Den"), a drug den for [Redwater skooma](/wiki/Skyrim:Redwater_Skooma "Skyrim:Redwater Skooma"). He wears [studded armor](/wiki/Skyrim:Studded_Armor "Skyrim:Studded Armor"), a pair of [hide boots](/wiki/Skyrim:Hide_Boots "Skyrim:Hide Boots"), a [scaled helmet](/wiki/Skyrim:Scaled_Helmet "Skyrim:Scaled Helmet") and a pair of leveled [heavy gauntlets](/wiki/Skyrim:Armor#Gauntlets_2 "Skyrim:Armor"). He also carries [alto wine](/wiki/Skyrim:Alto_Wine "Skyrim:Alto Wine") and a leveled [mace](/wiki/Skyrim:Mace "Skyrim:Mace").

## Dialogue

When first approached:

:   *"Hold it. If you're going downstairs, you keep your weapons to yourself or we'll be getting better acquainted. Head on in and behave yourself."*

If you talk to him after that, he says:

:   *"Go on downstairs. You're bothering me."*

## Notes

- If still alive, he will be renamed to "[Vampire's Thrall](/wiki/Skyrim:Vampire%27s_Thrall "Skyrim:Vampire's Thrall")" when you leave.

Dorian in the Red Wave

**Dorian** is a [Breton](/wiki/Skyrim:Breton "Skyrim:Breton") [thief](/wiki/Skyrim:CombatThief "Skyrim:CombatThief") and a pirate aboard the [Red Wave](/wiki/Skyrim:Red_Wave "Skyrim:Red Wave"), under the command of [Safia](/wiki/Skyrim:Safia "Skyrim:Safia").

Dorian wears a set of [leather armor](/wiki/Skyrim:Leather_Armor "Skyrim:Leather Armor"), including the [bracers](/wiki/Skyrim:Leather_Bracers "Skyrim:Leather Bracers") and [boots](/wiki/Skyrim:Leather_Boots "Skyrim:Leather Boots"). He carries a [belted tunic](/wiki/Skyrim:Belted_Tunic "Skyrim:Belted Tunic"), a selection of [common loot and gold](/wiki/Skyrim:Leveled_Lists#Common "Skyrim:Leveled Lists"), and an additional small amount of gold. He carries a leveled war axe, bow, and twelve arrows, all of which can be up to [Daedric](/wiki/Skyrim:Daedric "Skyrim:Daedric") in quality.

## Related Quests

- **[Kill Safia](/wiki/Skyrim:Kill_Safia "Skyrim:Kill Safia")**: Kill a [pirate captain](/wiki/Skyrim:Safia "Skyrim:Safia") on her own [ship](/wiki/Skyrim:Red_Wave "Skyrim:Red Wave").

- This NPC is one of many potential quest givers or quest targets for [one or more of the Radiant quests](/wiki/Skyrim:Radiant#Quest_NPCs "Skyrim:Radiant").

## Dialogue

Should you approach him he can say:

:   *"Forget wine, women and wealth - give me a calm sea and a good book, and I'm happy."*
:   *"I hear [Adonato Leotelli](/wiki/Skyrim:Adonato_Leotelli "Skyrim:Adonato Leotelli")'s staying up in [Windhelm](/wiki/Skyrim:Windhelm "Skyrim:Windhelm"). I've read a few of his works. Be good to meet him someday."*
:   *"Don't misunderstand me, friend. I like my quiet, and I like to read. But you trifle with my ship, my crew, or my captain? I will kill you."*
:   *"You've not seen the night sky until you've seen it on the open sea."*

He will also comment on his captain, Safia, as long as she is still alive:

:   *"I've only been a part of the Red Wave's crew for a few weeks, but I've already learned to stay out of Captain Safia's way."*

## Bugs

- While Dorian is technically a leveled NPC, you would need to be level 251 or higher to have any of his stats increase. Since this is highly unlikely, he is effectively unleveled, with Health fixed at 250 and Stamina fixed at 210.
  - The [Unofficial Skyrim Special Edition Patch](/wiki/Skyrim_Mod:Unofficial_Skyrim_Special_Edition_Patch "Skyrim Mod:Unofficial Skyrim Special Edition Patch"), version 4.0.6, addresses this issue. His level is set to PCx1. The fix also includes removing his essential status.
- Dorian does not exit the interior of the ship. This becomes problematic when a radiant quest chooses him as the target, as, once you have entered the ship, all he says is that you aren't supposed to be there.
  -  The [Unofficial Skyrim Patch](/wiki/Skyrim_Mod:Unofficial_Skyrim_Patch "Skyrim Mod:Unofficial Skyrim Patch"), version 1.3.3, addresses this issue. Red Wave crew members can now show up at the Winking Skeever.
  - You can start a fight with him then run outside. Once outside, and away from the entrance, lower your weapons and surrender. Talk to him before he has a chance to go below decks.
    - Having a follower can complicate your efforts to draw him out. The follower will continue to engage in combat and will prevent a surrender.
  -  Using the command `AF525.MoveTo Player` to place him near you.

Dorthe

**Dorthe** is a [Nord](/wiki/Skyrim:Nord "Skyrim:Nord") [child](/wiki/Skyrim:Child "Skyrim:Child") who lives in [Riverwood](/wiki/Skyrim:Riverwood "Skyrim:Riverwood"). [Sigrid](/wiki/Skyrim:Sigrid "Skyrim:Sigrid") and [Alvor](/wiki/Skyrim:Alvor "Skyrim:Alvor") are her mother and father, and she is a cousin of [Hadvar](/wiki/Skyrim:Hadvar "Skyrim:Hadvar"). She is friends with [Frodnar](/wiki/Skyrim:Frodnar "Skyrim:Frodnar"), even though their families support opposing sides in the current civil war. While keeping up appearances, the family is split in two: Her father wanted a son and obviously raises Dorthe like one, while Sigrid is overly concerned about her daughter's upbringing and exaggerates her attempts to make her act like a little girl.

Despite her mother's reservations about her boyish behavior, Dorthe can't be bothered and goes her own ways. After waking up at 6am she takes a quick one-hour breakfast, then leaves the [house](/wiki/Skyrim:Alvor_and_Sigrid%27s_House "Skyrim:Alvor and Sigrid's House") to play with her good friend [Frodnar](/wiki/Skyrim:Frodnar "Skyrim:Frodnar") and his dog [Stump](/wiki/Skyrim:Stump "Skyrim:Stump"). At 4pm she joins her father at his forge and acts as his 'apprentice' until they both go into the house for dinner at 8pm. After listening to her mother's complaints for four hours, she finally goes to bed at midnight. The only exception to this routine occurs when you first enter Riverwood and only if you escaped from [Helgen Keep](/wiki/Skyrim:Helgen_Keep "Skyrim:Helgen Keep") with her cousin Hadvar. She will then stay inside the house until you have spoken with Alvor. At the end of the discussion, she will insistently ask Hadvar: *"Hadvar, did you really see a dragon? What did it look like? Did it have big teeth?"*

She wears a set of [child's clothes](/wiki/Skyrim:Child%27s_Clothes "Skyrim:Child's Clothes") and [shoes](/wiki/Skyrim:Clothing#000e80a8 "Skyrim:Clothing") and carries a copy of the [house key](/wiki/Skyrim:Key_to_Alvor%27s_House "Skyrim:Key to Alvor's House") along with a selection of [food and toys](/wiki/Skyrim:Leveled_Lists#Child "Skyrim:Leveled Lists").

## Related Quests

- **[Before the Storm](/wiki/Skyrim:Before_the_Storm "Skyrim:Before the Storm")**: Inform the [Jarl](/wiki/Skyrim:Balgruuf_the_Greater "Skyrim:Balgruuf the Greater") of [Whiterun](/wiki/Skyrim:Whiterun "Skyrim:Whiterun") about the dragon attack on [Helgen](/wiki/Skyrim:Helgen "Skyrim:Helgen").
- **[Hide and Seek](/wiki/Skyrim:Hide_and_Seek_(game) "Skyrim:Hide and Seek (game)")**: Play a round of Hide and Seek with some [children](/wiki/Skyrim:Children "Skyrim:Children") in town. ([radiant](/wiki/Skyrim:Radiant "Skyrim:Radiant"))
- **[Tag, you're it!](/wiki/Skyrim:Tag,_you%27re_it! "Skyrim:Tag, you're it!")**: Play a round of Tag with the children of a city. ([radiant](/wiki/Skyrim:Radiant "Skyrim:Radiant"))

## Dialogue

When you speak to Dorthe:

:   *"Papa says I'm too friendly with strangers, but you seem all right."*
:   *"My father is Alvor, the blacksmith. I'm his assistant. I mean, apprentice."*
:   *"Some day I'm going to forge my own sword!"*
:   *"Papa says I'm not ready for weapons. So I make lots of horseshoes and hobnails."*
:   *"Mama doesn't think I'm girlish enough. But that's just stupid girl talk."*
:   *"Papa may have wanted a son, but he got me. He's a lucky man."*
:   *"Ain't nothin' a boy can do that I can't do better."*

## Conversations

Her daily life involves fooling around with local prankster [Frodnar](/wiki/Skyrim:Frodnar "Skyrim:Frodnar") although she can be heard telling him off for some really bad suggestions:

**Dorthe**: *"Wait, so... a costume? You're not serious..."*
**Frodnar**: *"Sure I am. We get some furs and tree branches, paint them white, and then tie them to Stump. Instant [Frostbite Spider](/wiki/Skyrim:Frostbite_Spider "Skyrim:Frostbite Spider")!"*
**Dorthe**: *"Frodnar... nobody is going to believe that your dog is a... Frostbite Spider. And if they do... they'll kill him. That's not much of a prank."*
**Frodnar**: *"Oh yeah, and what would you rather do?"*
**Dorthe**: *"How about... we play tag! You're it!"*
**Frodnar**: *"Hey, no fair! Get her, Stump!"*

*"Can I make something now, papa?"*

When Dorthe acts like her father's 'apprentice' near his forge, she will be quite enthusiastic about learning the trade, while Alvor will be more reserved. Dorthe will pick between three random lines and Alvor will do the same:

| Speaker | Conversation |
| --- | --- |
| **Dorthe** | *"Can I make something now, papa?"* |
| *"Is it time yet? Time for me to make my sword? Or maybe... an axe?"* |
| *"I'm bored standing around, papa. I could take over for you..."* |
| **Alvor** | *"Later, little one. I need to finish what I'm working on. But keep watching. Watch, and learn."* |
| *"He he. Not just yet, Dorthe. I need to keep forging, and you need to keep watching."* |
| *"Patience, Dorthe. You'll get some time at the forge, I promise you. But not right now. You need to keep watching me. That's how you'll learn."* |
| **Dorthe** | *"Don't worry, I am."* |
| *"All right. But I am getting a bit tired of waiting."* |
| *"Yes, sir."* |

*"Oh, Dorthe. You're breaking your mother's heart, you know that?"*

Occasionally, Dorthe will ask her father if she is ever going to be a great blacksmith.

**Dorthe**: *"You really think I can be a blacksmith someday, papa? As good as [Eorlund Gray-Mane](/wiki/Skyrim:Eorlund_Gray-Mane "Skyrim:Eorlund Gray-Mane")? Or maybe... even as good as you?"*
**Alvor**: *"Oh, I know it! You keep working hard, like you been doing, and you could be the greatest blacksmith Skyrim has ever seen."*
**Dorthe**: *"He he. Thanks, papa."*

When the family enjoys quality time together, it is quite common to hear Dorthe argue with her concerned mother, at times dragging an innocent Alvor into the conversation:

| Speaker | Conversation |
| --- | --- |
| **Sigrid** | *"Dorthe, dear, I've been growin' some really lovely vegetables. Maybe tomorrow you could help me plant a new patch? What do you say?"* |
| *"Dorthe... I was thinkin' I'd knit a couple of blankets, sell them to Lucan. Would you like to make one? Might be fun, workin' together."* |
| *"You know, Dorthe, with all those vegetables I've been growing lately, I was thinkin' we could make a right lovely stew. Together. How about it?"* |
| **Dorthe** | *"Oh. Um. Well... You see..."* |
| *"Wow. Yeah. That sounds great, mother. Only, um... it's just that..."* |
| *"Oooh. Ahhh... Well... See, the thing is..."* |
| **Sigrid** | *"Shor's crown! There are things ladies like us are supposed to do. We've talked about this..."* |
| *"Let me guess. You'd rather play "Daedra and Battlemages" with Ordnar. Or go fishing, or catch frogs..."* |
| *"Dorthe, listen to me. Your father and your friend may treat you like a boy, but you're not. Do you understand? So please. Be a girl. For me."* |
| **Dorthe** | *"It's just that papa promised I could make something at the forge. So maybe we could do something together, hmmm... next week? Is... that okay?"* |
| *"Just stop trying to change me, mother! I'm not a baby anymore! I'm almost a woman! I... I can't be who I want to be!"* |
| *"I'm sorry, mother. I can't help it. All that stuff you like to do, it's just so... boring."* |
| **Alvor** | *"Ho, now... Keep me out of this..."* |
| **Sigrid** | *"Fine. You play in the mud, or play with your father's forge, or get into sword fights with your little friend. But this is not over."* |
| *"Oh, Dorthe. You're breaking your mother's heart, you know that?"* |
| *"Well. I can see your father and I are going to have to talk about this. And when we do, things are going to change."* |

## Notes

- If you escaped Helgen with Hadvar, he will be flagged as a parent for Dorthe if Alvor and Sigrid are killed.

## Bugs

- Dorthe's bed isn't a child's bed, allowing her to sleep in the parents' bed, causing one of them to stay up all night.
  -  The [Unofficial Skyrim Patch](/wiki/Skyrim_Mod:Unofficial_Skyrim_Patch "Skyrim Mod:Unofficial Skyrim Patch"), version 2.0.0, addresses this issue. Her bed wasn't marked as a child's bed, which forced her AI to pick the nearest one available.

# Skyrim:Double-Edged

## Overview

The dossier and note

## Quick Walkthrough

1. Go to the [Cliffside Retreat](/wiki/Skyrim:Cliffside_Retreat "Skyrim:Cliffside Retreat") and read [Zaharia's note](/wiki/Skyrim:Zaharia%27s_Note "Skyrim:Zaharia's Note").
2. (Optional) Disrupt Zaharia's plan and remove the [Note to Ehlhiel](/wiki/Skyrim:Note_to_Ehlhiel "Skyrim:Note to Ehlhiel") in [Temple of the Divines](/wiki/Skyrim:Temple_of_the_Divines "Skyrim:Temple of the Divines").
3. Go to [Lost Echo Cave](/wiki/Skyrim:Lost_Echo_Cave "Skyrim:Lost Echo Cave") and defeat the person there.

## Detailed Walkthrough

The note sitting on the dresser

Zaharia waiting for Ehlhiel

This quest starts at [Cliffside Retreat](/wiki/Skyrim:Cliffside_Retreat "Skyrim:Cliffside Retreat"), with a barrel that has [Zaharia's Note](/wiki/Skyrim:Zaharia%27s_Note "Skyrim:Zaharia's Note") on top of it alongside [Guard's Dossier: Ehlhiel](/wiki/Skyrim:Guard%27s_Dossier:_Ehlhiel "Skyrim:Guard's Dossier: Ehlhiel"). Read the note to start the quest, you can either help Zaharia, a [Crimson Dirk](/wiki/Skyrim:Crimson_Dirks "Skyrim:Crimson Dirks"), and kill the traitor Ehlhiel, or you can help save Ehlhiel's life.
If you decide to save Ehlhiel, head to the [Temple of the Divines](/wiki/Skyrim:Temple_of_the_Divines "Skyrim:Temple of the Divines") in Solitude, read and take the [note](/wiki/Skyrim:Note_to_Ehlhiel "Skyrim:Note to Ehlhiel") on the dresser upstairs on the right.

Either way go to [Lost Echo Cave](/wiki/Skyrim:Lost_Echo_Cave "Skyrim:Lost Echo Cave"), where you will have to defeat [Zaharia](/wiki/Skyrim:Zaharia "Skyrim:Zaharia") if you took the note from the Temple of the Divines or [Ehlhiel](/wiki/Skyrim:Ehlhiel "Skyrim:Ehlhiel") if you didn't. Afterwards loot your reward from Zaharia.

## Notes

- Although the quest entries read that a Thalmor double agent betrayed a member of the Blades, *[Guard's Dossier: Ehlhiel](/wiki/Skyrim:Guard%27s_Dossier:_Ehlhiel "Skyrim:Guard's Dossier: Ehlhiel")* and *[Zaharia's Note](/wiki/Skyrim:Zaharia%27s_Note "Skyrim:Zaharia's Note")* reads that Ehlhiel betrayed the [Crimson Dirks](/wiki/Skyrim:Crimson_Dirks "Skyrim:Crimson Dirks") for the city guard captains and the [East Empire Company](/wiki/Skyrim:East_Empire_Company "Skyrim:East Empire Company"). This suggests that the storyline of the quest was changed at some point, but the quest objectives were not updated to match.

## Bugs

- [Note to Ehlhiel](/wiki/Skyrim:Note_to_Ehlhiel "Skyrim:Note to Ehlhiel") may still be treated as a quest item despite having completed Double-Edged. **?**
  -  Enter the console command `player.removeitem FExxx81A 1` to remove it from your inventory.

## Quest Stages

| Double-Edged (ccBGSSSE053\_Quest) | | |
| --- | --- | --- |
| Stage | Finishes Quest | Journal Entry |
| 10 |  | Hunters in Skyrim are known to have retreats in the mountains with supplies and food. If I'm ever in the area near Solitude, I should stop by Cliffside Retreat. *Objective 10:* Look for a note at Cliffside Retreat |
| 20 |  | At Cliffside Retreat, I found a dossier that implies a bandit has become an asset of the Thalmor. The accompanying note says that another agent, Zaharia, intends to enact revenge by arranging a meeting at Lost Echo Cave. I can save the Thalmor agent by intercepting her note, or try to help Zaharia by going to the cave. *Objective 20:* Go to Lost Echo Cave  *Objective 30:* (Optional) Disrupt Zaharia's plan and remove the letter |

I decided to save the Thalmor agent by intercepting the note at the Temple of Divines. |

# Skyrim:Dragon Bridge Lumber Camp

## Overview

|  |  |  |
| --- | --- | --- |

| [Dragon Bridge](/wiki/Skyrim:Dragon_Bridge "Skyrim:Dragon Bridge") | |

| # of [Stone Quarries](/wiki/Skyrim:Quarried_Stone "Skyrim:Quarried Stone")[HF](/wiki/Skyrim:Hearthfire "Skyrim:Hearthfire") | 1 |

Dragon Bridge Lumber Camp

**Dragon Bridge Lumber Camp** is a sawmill and lumber camp in the southwestern part of [Dragon Bridge](/wiki/Skyrim:Dragon_Bridge "Skyrim:Dragon Bridge").

It consists of one zone, *[Dragon Bridge Lumber Camp](#Dragon_Bridge_Lumber_Camp).*

### Exterior

| Plants | Other |
| --- | --- |
| 2 [Blue Mountain Flower](/wiki/Skyrim:Blue_Mountain_Flower "Skyrim:Blue Mountain Flower")  2 [Purple Mountain Flower](/wiki/Skyrim:Purple_Mountain_Flower "Skyrim:Purple Mountain Flower")  1 [Red Mountain Flower](/wiki/Skyrim:Red_Mountain_Flower "Skyrim:Red Mountain Flower") | 1 [Stone Quarry](/wiki/Skyrim:Quarried_Stone "Skyrim:Quarried Stone")[HF](/wiki/Skyrim:Hearthfire "Skyrim:Hearthfire")  1 [Wood Chopping Block](/wiki/Skyrim:Chop_Wood "Skyrim:Chop Wood") |

### Dragon Bridge Lumber Camp

Ground floor

The building consists of a ground floor and a basement. On the ground floor, a double bed owned by [Lodvar](/wiki/Skyrim:Lodvar "Skyrim:Lodvar") can be found on the east wall, flanked by a non-respawning unlocked chest containing leveled items on the left and a small table on the right. The table holds two bottles of [alto wine](/wiki/Skyrim:Alto_Wine "Skyrim:Alto Wine") and five loose gold coins. Another bottle of alto wine lies on its side near the foot of the bed. A set of shelves on the north wall holds a bottle of [wine](/wiki/Skyrim:Wine "Skyrim:Wine") and three bottles of alto wine. A respawning food barrel sits in the southwest corner, and at the center of the room is a large dining table holding two [goat cheese wedges](/wiki/Skyrim:Goat_Cheese_Wedge "Skyrim:Goat Cheese Wedge"), one [eidar cheese wedge](/wiki/Skyrim:Eidar_Cheese_Wedge "Skyrim:Eidar Cheese Wedge"), three loaves of [bread](/wiki/Skyrim:Bread "Skyrim:Bread"), a bottle of alto wine, a [pine thrush egg](/wiki/Skyrim:Pine_Thrush_Egg "Skyrim:Pine Thrush Egg"), and two pieces of [salmon meat](/wiki/Skyrim:Salmon_Meat "Skyrim:Salmon Meat"). Beneath the table are two [chicken's eggs](/wiki/Skyrim:Chicken%27s_Egg "Skyrim:Chicken's Egg").

Basement

In the basement, a respawning food barrel can be found beneath the stairs, along with another on the north wall nearby. A small table holds a goat cheese wedge, a loaf of bread, a pine thrush egg, and a bottle of wine. Between the barrel and table, a hanging rack above holds four freshly caught [pheasants](/wiki/Skyrim:Pheasant "Skyrim:Pheasant"). Across from the table, on the south wall, four non-respawning sacks lie on the floor. Next to the sacks is a non-respawning dresser with a [lute](/wiki/Skyrim:Lute "Skyrim:Lute") and an [iron mace](/wiki/Skyrim:Iron_Mace "Skyrim:Iron Mace") sitting on top, a [pickaxe](/wiki/Skyrim:Pickaxe "Skyrim:Pickaxe") on the floor to the right, and a large respawning sack to the left. Another respawning food barrel can be found in the southeast corner, next to a set of shelves holding [miner's clothes](/wiki/Skyrim:Miner%27s_Clothes#00080697 "Skyrim:Miner's Clothes") and an [iron dagger](/wiki/Skyrim:Iron_Dagger "Skyrim:Iron Dagger") on the top shelf, a [common soul gem](/wiki/Skyrim:Common_Soul_Gem "Skyrim:Common Soul Gem"), five gold coins, and a [saw](/wiki/Skyrim:Saw "Skyrim:Saw") on the middle shelf, and two bottles each of wine and alto wine on the bottom shelf. To the left of these shelves is a non-respawning cupboard which holds copies of the books *[The Holds of Skyrim](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Holds_of_Skyrim "Skyrim:The Holds of Skyrim")*, *[Of Crossed Daggers](/wiki/Skyrim:Of_Crossed_Daggers "Skyrim:Of Crossed Daggers")*, *[Herbane's Bestiary: Ice Wraiths](/wiki/Skyrim:Herbane%27s_Bestiary:_Ice_Wraiths "Skyrim:Herbane's Bestiary: Ice Wraiths")*, and *[Alduin is Real](/wiki/Skyrim:Alduin_is_Real "Skyrim:Alduin is Real")*, along with two loaves of bread, a bottle of wine, and a bottle of alto wine. A single bed, also owned by Lodvar, is situated with the head along the north wall. At the foot of the bed is a pair of miner [boots](/wiki/Skyrim:Boots#00080699 "Skyrim:Boots"), and a small non-respawning unlocked chest containing leveled items sits to the left side. Above the bed are some hanging ingredients, including two [garlic](/wiki/Skyrim:Garlic "Skyrim:Garlic") braids, one dried [frost mirriam](/wiki/Skyrim:Frost_Mirriam "Skyrim:Frost Mirriam"), and two portions of dried [elves ear](/wiki/Skyrim:Elves_Ear "Skyrim:Elves Ear"), as well as a hanging rack holding three freshly caught [rabbits](/wiki/Skyrim:Rabbit_(dead) "Skyrim:Rabbit (dead)").

## Notes

- The front door has an apprentice lock, the [key](/wiki/Skyrim:Lumber_Camp_Key "Skyrim:Lumber Camp Key") to which is carried by [Horgeir](/wiki/Skyrim:Horgeir "Skyrim:Horgeir").
- [Sawn logs](/wiki/Skyrim:Sawn_Log "Skyrim:Sawn Log")[HF](/wiki/Skyrim:Hearthfire "Skyrim:Hearthfire") cannot be purchased at the lumber mill here.
- There is a non-respawning pot located at the fire near the wood chopping block.
- All cupboards, end tables, and dressers in the area are non-respawning and safe to store items in.

## Bugs

- The water wheel sounds at the mill here are missing.
  -  The [Unofficial Skyrim Patch](/wiki/Skyrim_Mod:Unofficial_Skyrim_Patch "Skyrim Mod:Unofficial Skyrim Patch"), version 2.0.4, fixes this bug.

# Skyrim:Dragon Bridge Overlook

## Overview

Dragon Bridge Overlook

**Dragon Bridge Overlook** is a small [Forsworn](/wiki/Skyrim:Forsworn "Skyrim:Forsworn") [camp](/wiki/Skyrim:Camps "Skyrim:Camps") south of [Dragon Bridge](/wiki/Skyrim:Dragon_Bridge "Skyrim:Dragon Bridge").

#### Radiant Quests

- **[Bounty: Forsworn](/wiki/Skyrim:Bounty:_Forsworn "Skyrim:Bounty: Forsworn")**: Kill a [Forsworn](/wiki/Skyrim:Forsworn "Skyrim:Forsworn") leader for a bounty reward.
- **[The Ghost of Old Hroldan](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Ghost_of_Old_Hroldan "Skyrim:The Ghost of Old Hroldan")**: Put an [ancient ghost](/wiki/Skyrim:Ghost_of_Old_Hroldan "Skyrim:Ghost of Old Hroldan") to rest.
- **[Kill the Forsworn Leader](/wiki/Skyrim:Kill_the_Forsworn_Leader_(Jarl) "Skyrim:Kill the Forsworn Leader (Jarl)")**: Do a favor for [Jarl Igmund](/wiki/Skyrim:Igmund "Skyrim:Igmund") by killing a [Forsworn](/wiki/Skyrim:Forsworn "Skyrim:Forsworn") leader.
- **[Lisbet's Missing Shipment](/wiki/Skyrim:Lisbet%27s_Missing_Shipment "Skyrim:Lisbet's Missing Shipment")**: Retrieve a missing Dibella Statue for a struggling store.

## Walkthrough

The camp, which is on a cliff overlooking Dragon Bridge, can be accessed by following the [Karth River](/wiki/Skyrim:Karth_River "Skyrim:Karth River") upstream (southwest) from Dragon Bridge and then descending upon the camp, or by starting from [Bruca's Leap Redoubt](/wiki/Skyrim:Bruca%27s_Leap_Redoubt "Skyrim:Bruca's Leap Redoubt") and heading east. It consists of two Forsworn tents, one on either side of a campfire. Sharpened stakes and stretched hides surround the camp, which features [blue](/wiki/Skyrim:Blue_Mountain_Flower "Skyrim:Blue Mountain Flower"), [red](/wiki/Skyrim:Red_Mountain_Flower "Skyrim:Red Mountain Flower"), and [purple mountain flowers](/wiki/Skyrim:Purple_Mountain_Flower "Skyrim:Purple Mountain Flower"), [thistles](/wiki/Skyrim:Thistle "Skyrim:Thistle"), and two patches of [mora tapinella](/wiki/Skyrim:Mora_Tapinella "Skyrim:Mora Tapinella") fungus on a huge tree stump. The camp is home to two Forsworn, one of whom is typically found inside one of the tents, while the other is on the cliff edge overlooking the town, with a quiver of [Forsworn arrows](/wiki/Skyrim:Forsworn_Arrow "Skyrim:Forsworn Arrow") and an [iron dagger](/wiki/Skyrim:Iron_Dagger "Skyrim:Iron Dagger") on top of a piece of wooden boarding at their feet. The first tent contains an unowned hay pile, a pair of [Forsworn gauntlets](/wiki/Skyrim:Forsworn_Gauntlets "Skyrim:Forsworn Gauntlets"), a bottle of [ale](/wiki/Skyrim:Ale "Skyrim:Ale"), and two [deer pelts](/wiki/Skyrim:Deer_Pelt "Skyrim:Deer Pelt"). The second tent contains a novice-locked [chest](/wiki/Skyrim:Chest "Skyrim:Chest") as well as a long wooden table holding a tactical map of [Skyrim](/wiki/Lore:Skyrim "Lore:Skyrim"), a [Forsworn axe](/wiki/Skyrim:Forsworn_Axe "Skyrim:Forsworn Axe"), an iron dagger, a random [potion of magicka](/wiki/Skyrim:Potion_of_Magicka "Skyrim:Potion of Magicka"), two bottles of ale, and a [leg of goat](/wiki/Skyrim:Leg_of_Goat "Skyrim:Leg of Goat").

Dragon Bridge

**Dragon Bridge** is a milling [town](/wiki/Skyrim:Towns "Skyrim:Towns") in southern [Haafingar](/wiki/Skyrim:Haafingar "Skyrim:Haafingar").

The town and its iconic bridge are of vital interest to both the [Stormcloak](/wiki/Skyrim:Stormcloaks "Skyrim:Stormcloaks") rebels and the [Imperials](/wiki/Skyrim:Imperial_Legion "Skyrim:Imperial Legion") in the [Civil War](/wiki/Skyrim:Civil_War "Skyrim:Civil War"). The townspeople of Dragon Bridge are worried that either side may seek to destroy the bridge as a means of preventing the other from crossing.

There are two families that live in Dragon Bridge: [Horgeir](/wiki/Skyrim:Horgeir "Skyrim:Horgeir") and [Olda](/wiki/Skyrim:Olda "Skyrim:Olda"), and the [Lylvieve family](/wiki/Skyrim:Lylvieve_Family_House_Occupants "Skyrim:Lylvieve Family House Occupants"). The guards have been harassing the Lylvieve family and [Faida](/wiki/Skyrim:Faida "Skyrim:Faida"), the proprietor of the inn by refusing to pay, stealing, and attempting to "have their way" with [Julienne Lylvieve](/wiki/Skyrim:Julienne_Lylvieve "Skyrim:Julienne Lylvieve"). The mill, however, has prospered due to the increased demand for lumber.

The town consists of a main road running northeast from the bridge toward [Solitude](/wiki/Skyrim:Solitude "Skyrim:Solitude"). [Dragon Bridge lumber camp](/wiki/Skyrim:Dragon_Bridge_Lumber_Camp "Skyrim:Dragon Bridge Lumber Camp") and sawmill are the first buildings to the left of the road after crossing the bridge into Dragon Bridge. The mill is powered by the [Karth River](/wiki/Skyrim:Karth_River "Skyrim:Karth River"), which flows beneath the bridge on its way to the [Sea of Ghosts](/wiki/Skyrim:Sea_of_Ghosts "Skyrim:Sea of Ghosts"). Next to the lumber camp is the only outpost for the [Penitus Oculatus](/wiki/Skyrim:Penitus_Oculatus "Skyrim:Penitus Oculatus"), who replaced the [Blades](/wiki/Skyrim:Blades "Skyrim:Blades") as the personal security and espionage force for the [Emperor](/wiki/Skyrim:Emperor_Titus_Mede_II_(real) "Skyrim:Emperor Titus Mede II (real)") when the Blades disbanded. Northeast of the outpost is [Horgeir's house](/wiki/Skyrim:Horgeir%27s_House "Skyrim:Horgeir's House"), home to Horgeir, his wife, and his brother [Lodvar](/wiki/Skyrim:Lodvar "Skyrim:Lodvar").

Opposite his house is the town's inn, the [Four Shields Tavern](/wiki/Skyrim:Four_Shields_Tavern "Skyrim:Four Shields Tavern"), which is the only building on the eastern side of the main road. Behind the inn is a secondary road that starts near the bridge and circles the inn before rejoining the main road at the other end of town. Next door to Horgeir's house is the [Lylvieve family's house](/wiki/Skyrim:Lylvieve_Family%27s_House "Skyrim:Lylvieve Family's House"), where [Azzada Lylvieve](/wiki/Skyrim:Azzada_Lylvieve "Skyrim:Azzada Lylvieve") lives with his [wife](/wiki/Skyrim:Michel_Lylvieve "Skyrim:Michel Lylvieve") and two children.

## Dragon Bridge Residents

#### Dark Brotherhood

- **[Breaching Security](/wiki/Skyrim:Breaching_Security "Skyrim:Breaching Security")**: Kill and frame the [son](/wiki/Skyrim:Gaius_Maro "Skyrim:Gaius Maro") of a high-ranking [Imperial guard](/wiki/Skyrim:Commander_Maro "Skyrim:Commander Maro").
- **[Destroy the Dark Brotherhood!](/wiki/Skyrim:Destroy_the_Dark_Brotherhood! "Skyrim:Destroy the Dark Brotherhood!")**: Finish the [Dark Brotherhood](/wiki/Skyrim:Dark_Brotherhood "Skyrim:Dark Brotherhood") and rid Skyrim of their kind.

#### Dawnguard

- **[Prophet (Dawnguard)](/wiki/Skyrim:Prophet_(Dawnguard) "Skyrim:Prophet (Dawnguard)")**[DG](/wiki/Skyrim:Dawnguard "Skyrim:Dawnguard"): Find and rescue [a Moth Priest](/wiki/Skyrim:Dexion_Evicus "Skyrim:Dexion Evicus") from the [vampires](/wiki/Skyrim:Volkihar_Vampire_Clan "Skyrim:Volkihar Vampire Clan").
- **[Prophet (Vampire)](/wiki/Skyrim:Prophet_(Vampire) "Skyrim:Prophet (Vampire)")**[DG](/wiki/Skyrim:Dawnguard "Skyrim:Dawnguard"): The time of prophecy has arrived! Locate [a Moth Priest](/wiki/Skyrim:Dexion_Evicus "Skyrim:Dexion Evicus") for the [vampires](/wiki/Skyrim:Volkihar_Vampire_Clan "Skyrim:Volkihar Vampire Clan").

#### Creation Club

- **[Over the Edge](/wiki/Skyrim:Over_the_Edge "Skyrim:Over the Edge")**[CC](/wiki/Skyrim:Alternative_Armors_-_Steel_Soldier "Skyrim:Alternative Armors - Steel Soldier"): A criminal has sensed his past catching up with him.

## Notes

- The treasure of [Treasure Map VIII](/wiki/Skyrim:Treasure_Map_VIII "Skyrim:Treasure Map VIII") is underwater near the bridge. A [satchel](/wiki/Skyrim:Satchel "Skyrim:Satchel") containing its key can be found a few paces upstream of the bridge.
- A [gold ore vein](/wiki/Skyrim:Gold_Ore_Vein "Skyrim:Gold Ore Vein") is upstream from the bridge on the bank opposite the town, and an [iron ore vein](/wiki/Skyrim:Iron_Ore_Vein "Skyrim:Iron Ore Vein") is upstream from the bridge on the right next to a [Nirnroot](/wiki/Skyrim:Nirnroot "Skyrim:Nirnroot").
- If *[Hearthfire](/wiki/Skyrim:Hearthfire "Skyrim:Hearthfire")* is installed, a [stone quarry](/wiki/Skyrim:Stone_Quarry "Skyrim:Stone Quarry") is behind the lumber camp at the foot of the cliff wall.
- With the [Fishing](/wiki/Skyrim:Fishing "Skyrim:Fishing") [Creation](/wiki/Skyrim:Creation_Club "Skyrim:Creation Club") installed, some [Fishing Supplies](/wiki/Skyrim:Fishing_Supplies "Skyrim:Fishing Supplies") are by the water near the mill. There is also a static copy of the [fishing map for Haafingar](/wiki/Skyrim:Fishing_Map_-_Haafingar "Skyrim:Fishing Map - Haafingar") and two [ales](/wiki/Skyrim:Ale "Skyrim:Ale") on top of a barrel, and two [river betties](/wiki/Skyrim:River_Betty "Skyrim:River Betty"), a [brook bass](/wiki/Skyrim:Brook_Bass "Skyrim:Brook Bass"), and an [abecean longfin](/wiki/Skyrim:Abecean_Longfin "Skyrim:Abecean Longfin") in a wooden crate on the ground.
- Dragon Bridge also appears in *[Arena](/wiki/Arena:Dragon_Bridge "Arena:Dragon Bridge")* and [ESO](/wiki/Online:Dragon_Bridge "Online:Dragon Bridge").

## Bugs

- The [guards](/wiki/Skyrim:Guard "Skyrim:Guard") in Dragon Bridge are mistakenly named "Imperial Soldier" instead of "Haafingar Guard".
  -  The [Unofficial Skyrim Patch](/wiki/Skyrim_Mod:Unofficial_Skyrim_Patch "Skyrim Mod:Unofficial Skyrim Patch"), version 2.0.7, fixes this bug.
- The Stormcloak guards who occupy Dragon Bridge once Solitude has fallen are not members of the town's guard faction, causing them to drop town specific dialogue they should have.
  -  The [Unofficial Skyrim Patch](/wiki/Skyrim_Mod:Unofficial_Skyrim_Patch "Skyrim Mod:Unofficial Skyrim Patch"), version 1.2.5, fixes this bug.
- The fast travel arrival point here is farther away from where your [horse](/wiki/Skyrim:Horses "Skyrim:Horses") would end up. This is inconsistent with how other locations with horse markers are handled.
  -  The [Unofficial Skyrim Patch](/wiki/Skyrim_Mod:Unofficial_Skyrim_Patch "Skyrim Mod:Unofficial Skyrim Patch"), version 1.2.6, fixes this bug.
- Female Stormcloak soldiers who occupy Dragon Bridge once Solitude has fallen won't say anything about the Moth Priest if you ask them about it during [Prophet](/wiki/Skyrim:Prophet "Skyrim:Prophet").
  -  The [Unofficial Skyrim Legendary Edition Patch](/wiki/Skyrim_Mod:Unofficial_Skyrim_Legendary_Edition_Patch "Skyrim Mod:Unofficial Skyrim Legendary Edition Patch"), version 3.0.7, addresses this issue. The female Stormcloak soldiers here had no audio recorded for that. You'll need to ask someone else.

**Dragon Cultists** are the restless spirits of members of the ancient [Dragon Cult](/wiki/Skyrim:Dragon_Cult "Skyrim:Dragon Cult") who chose to take their own lives rather than fall to King Harald's army. They only appear to attack invaders in [Forelhost](/wiki/Skyrim:Forelhost "Skyrim:Forelhost").

Dragon Cultists make use of [ancient Nord](/wiki/Skyrim:Ancient_Nord "Skyrim:Ancient Nord") weapons and armor, and may also carry a [dragon priest dagger](/wiki/Skyrim:Dragon_Priest_Dagger "Skyrim:Dragon Priest Dagger"). Some Cultists are capable of using [Destruction](/wiki/Skyrim:Destruction "Skyrim:Destruction") magic.

## Related Quests

- **[Siege on the Dragon Cult](/wiki/Skyrim:Siege_on_the_Dragon_Cult "Skyrim:Siege on the Dragon Cult")**: Enter the ruins of [Forelhost](/wiki/Skyrim:Forelhost "Skyrim:Forelhost") and defeat [Rahgot](/wiki/Skyrim:Rahgot_(creature) "Skyrim:Rahgot (creature)") to recover his mask for [Captain Valmir](/wiki/Skyrim:Captain_Valmir "Skyrim:Captain Valmir").

## Notes

- Dragon Cultists make the sounds of [Draugr](/wiki/Skyrim:Draugr "Skyrim:Draugr"), even though normally ghosts don't show that behavior.

# Skyrim:Dragon Hunting

## Overview

|  |
| --- |
| **This page is currently being rewritten as part of the [Skyrim Quest Redesign Project](/wiki/UESPWiki:Skyrim_Quest_Redesign_Project "UESPWiki:Skyrim Quest Redesign Project").** The page is being rewritten and checked in several stages. All users are welcome to make changes to the page. If you make a change that is relevant to the project, please update this template accordingly, and make sure you have observed the [project guidelines](/wiki/UESPWiki:Skyrim_Quest_Redesign_Project#Guidelines "UESPWiki:Skyrim Quest Redesign Project").  Details  **Walkthrough**: written by [Neondrmr](/wiki/User:Neondrmr "User:Neondrmr"), *not checked*  **Reward**: written by [RobinHood70](/wiki/User:RobinHood70 "User:RobinHood70"), *not checked* |

|  |  |
| --- | --- |
| **Kill a [dragon](/wiki/Skyrim:Dragon "Skyrim:Dragon") at its [lair](/wiki/Skyrim:Dragon_Lairs "Skyrim:Dragon Lairs").** | |

| |  |  | | --- | --- | | ← Previous | [Rebuilding the Blades](/wiki/Skyrim:Rebuilding_the_Blades "Skyrim:Rebuilding the Blades") | | → Next | [Dragon Research](/wiki/Skyrim:Dragon_Research "Skyrim:Dragon Research") | | |

*"Die, dragon!"*

## Quick Walkthrough

1. Ask [Esbern](/wiki/Skyrim:Esbern "Skyrim:Esbern") about dragon lairs.
2. Meet the [Blades](/wiki/Skyrim:Blades "Skyrim:Blades") at the given location.
3. Slay the [dragon](/wiki/Skyrim:Dragon "Skyrim:Dragon").
4. Return to Esbern.

## Detailed Walkthrough

This is a [radiant](/wiki/Skyrim:Radiant "Skyrim:Radiant") quest and can be completed any number of times in a number of different locations. This quest only becomes available once the quests [Alduin's Wall](/wiki/Skyrim:Alduin%27s_Wall "Skyrim:Alduin's Wall") and [Rebuilding the Blades](/wiki/Skyrim:Rebuilding_the_Blades "Skyrim:Rebuilding the Blades") are complete. If the quest [Paarthurnax](/wiki/Skyrim:Paarthurnax_(quest) "Skyrim:Paarthurnax (quest)") is active this quest cannot be received until it is completed.

In [Sky Haven Temple](/wiki/Skyrim:Sky_Haven_Temple "Skyrim:Sky Haven Temple"), talk to [Esbern](/wiki/Skyrim:Esbern "Skyrim:Esbern") to see if he has discovered the location of a [dragon's](/wiki/Skyrim:Dragon "Skyrim:Dragon") lair. If he has, he'll tell you that his research has uncovered a location, and will offer to send the [Blades](/wiki/Skyrim:Blades "Skyrim:Blades") to meet you there. If you accept, the quest begins: a location is marked on the your map, and an entry is added to the Miscellaneous quests to "Kill the Dragon in <location>".

Travel to the given location. The Blades recruited during Rebuilding the Blades will be waiting nearby. Once you arrive they will charge the lair, attacking the dragon. If you attack the dragon without having triggered the charge of the Blades, the attack will trigger the charge. Once the dragon is slain, the Blades will return to Sky Haven Temple, leaving you to loot the dragon and collect any nearby treasure.

Return to Sky Haven Temple and tell Esbern the dragon is slain. This will end the quest but it is possible to repeat the quest if desired.

## Notes

- This can be a useful tool for finding some [word walls](/wiki/Skyrim:Word_Wall "Skyrim:Word Wall") if [Arngeir](/wiki/Skyrim:Arngeir "Skyrim:Arngeir") will no longer provide the information after killing [Paarthurnax](/wiki/Skyrim:Paarthurnax_(dragon) "Skyrim:Paarthurnax (dragon)").
- Blades who do not live at Sky Haven Temple will not appear to help you fight the dragon. This includes Blades whom you have [married](/wiki/Skyrim:Marriage "Skyrim:Marriage") and moved to one of your homes, and Blades whom you have made a [steward](/wiki/Skyrim:Personal_Steward "Skyrim:Personal Steward")[HF](/wiki/Skyrim:Hearthfire "Skyrim:Hearthfire") of a Hearthfire house. However, after you kill the dragon, they may sometimes move to Sky Haven Temple. They will eventually return to their proper homes.

## Bugs

- Killing a dragon (in particular, if you've begun [Rebuilding the Blades](/wiki/Skyrim:Rebuilding_the_Blades "Skyrim:Rebuilding the Blades") but have not started this quest yet) may sometimes add the "Return to Esbern" task to your quest log, but Esbern will not complete the quest for you.
  -  The [Unofficial Skyrim Patch](/wiki/Skyrim_Mod:Unofficial_Skyrim_Patch "Skyrim Mod:Unofficial Skyrim Patch"), version 1.2.5, fixes this bug.
  -  You can use the console to finish the quest by entering `setStage FreeformSkyHavenTempleB 100`.
- Sometimes, upon starting the quest, the quest marker will show that the dragon is in a different, unreachable location.
  -  This can be fixed with the console by entering `setStage FreeformSkyHavenTempleB 20`.
- Sometimes Esbern won't give you a dragon to hunt.

## Quest Stages

| Dragon Hunting (FreeformSkyHavenTempleB) | | |
| --- | --- | --- |
| Stage | Finishes Quest | Journal Entry |
| 10 |  | *Objective 10:* Kill the Dragon in <Alias=DragonLair> |
| 20 |  | *Objective 20:* Return to Esbern |

- The following empty quest stages were omitted from the table: 5, 15, 25, 100.

Notes

- Any text displayed in angle brackets (e.g., `<Alias=LocationHold>`) is dynamically set by the Radiant Quest system, and will be filled in with the appropriate word(s) when seen in game.
- Not all Journal Entries may appear in your journal; which entries appear and which entries do not depends on the manner in which the quest is done.
- Stages are not always in order of progress. This is usually the case with quests that have multiple possible outcomes or quests where certain tasks may be done in any order. Some stages may therefore repeat objectives seen in other stages.
- If an entry is marked as "Finishes Quest" it means the quest disappears from the Active Quest list, but you may still receive new entries for that quest.
- On the PC, it is possible to use the [console](/wiki/Skyrim:Console "Skyrim:Console") to advance through the quest by entering `setstage FreeformSkyHavenTempleB stage`, where `stage` is the number of the stage you wish to complete. It is not possible to un-complete (i.e. go back) quest stages, but it is possible to clear all stages of the quest using `resetquest FreeformSkyHavenTempleB`.

# Skyrim:Dragon Lairs

## Overview

Northwind Summit

 This page lists all the **dragon lairs** in [Skyrim](/wiki/Skyrim:Skyrim "Skyrim:Skyrim"). All dragon lairs also contain [word walls](/wiki/Skyrim:Word_Wall "Skyrim:Word Wall"). Stationary [dragons](/wiki/Skyrim:Dragon "Skyrim:Dragon") can commonly be found at dragon lairs, making them a good place to look for [dragon bones](/wiki/Skyrim:Dragon_Bone "Skyrim:Dragon Bone"), [dragon scales](/wiki/Skyrim:Dragon_Scales "Skyrim:Dragon Scales"), dragon souls, and words for [shouts](/wiki/Skyrim:Dragon_Shouts "Skyrim:Dragon Shouts").

:    **[Ancient's Ascent](/wiki/Skyrim:Ancient%27s_Ascent "Skyrim:Ancient's Ascent")** — A mountaintop dragon lair southwest of Helgen. [(map)](https://gamemap.uesp.net/sr/?world=Skyrim&centeron=Ancient%27s+Ascent)
:    **[Autumnwatch Tower](/wiki/Skyrim:Autumnwatch_Tower "Skyrim:Autumnwatch Tower")** — A dragon lair south of Ivarstead. [(map)](https://gamemap.uesp.net/sr/?world=Skyrim&centeron=Autumnwatch+Tower)
:    **[Bonestrewn Crest](/wiki/Skyrim:Bonestrewn_Crest "Skyrim:Bonestrewn Crest")** — A mountaintop dragon lair south of Windhelm. [(map)](https://gamemap.uesp.net/sr/?world=Skyrim&centeron=Bonestrewn+Crest)
:    **[Dragontooth Crater](/wiki/Skyrim:Dragontooth_Crater "Skyrim:Dragontooth Crater")** — A dragon lair north-northwest of Karthwasten. [(map)](https://gamemap.uesp.net/sr/?world=Skyrim&centeron=Dragontooth+Crater)
:    **[Eldersblood Peak](/wiki/Skyrim:Eldersblood_Peak "Skyrim:Eldersblood Peak")** — A mountaintop dragon lair south of Morthal. [(map)](https://gamemap.uesp.net/sr/?world=Skyrim&centeron=Eldersblood+Peak)
:    **[Lost Tongue Overlook](/wiki/Skyrim:Lost_Tongue_Overlook "Skyrim:Lost Tongue Overlook")** — A dragon lair south of Riften. [(map)](https://gamemap.uesp.net/sr/?world=Skyrim&centeron=Lost+Tongue+Overlook)
:    **[Mount Anthor](/wiki/Skyrim:Mount_Anthor "Skyrim:Mount Anthor")** — A mountaintop dragon lair south-southwest of Winterhold. [(map)](https://gamemap.uesp.net/sr/?world=Skyrim&centeron=Mount+Anthor)
:    **[Northwind Summit](/wiki/Skyrim:Northwind_Summit "Skyrim:Northwind Summit")** — A mountaintop dragon lair northwest of Shor's Stone. [(map)](https://gamemap.uesp.net/sr/?world=Skyrim&centeron=Northwind+Summit)
:    **[Saering's Watch](/wiki/Skyrim:Saering%27s_Watch "Skyrim:Saering's Watch")**[DB](/wiki/Skyrim:Dragonborn "Skyrim:Dragonborn") — A dragon lair in the shadow of Frykte Peak on Solstheim. [(map)](https://gamemap.uesp.net/sr/?world=solstheim&centeron=Saering%27s+Watch)
:    **[Shearpoint](/wiki/Skyrim:Shearpoint "Skyrim:Shearpoint")** — A mountaintop dragon lair northeast of Whiterun. [(map)](https://gamemap.uesp.net/sr/?world=Skyrim&centeron=Shearpoint)
:    **[Skyborn Altar](/wiki/Skyrim:Skyborn_Altar "Skyrim:Skyborn Altar")** — A mountaintop dragon lair east-southeast of Morthal. [(map)](https://gamemap.uesp.net/sr/?world=Skyrim&centeron=Skyborn+Altar)

## Notes

- If you visit a dragon lair prior to [Dragon Rising](/wiki/Skyrim:Dragon_Rising "Skyrim:Dragon Rising"), it will only be inhabited by generic enemies, often enabling you to learn its word with minimal effort. More details can be found on the individual location pages.
- The dragons found at dragon lairs will always respawn, no matter how many times they are killed. This is an excellent way for any player with the skill to kill them to earn valuable experience and items and to test their combat prowess. It is especially helpful for lower to intermediate level players.
- Talking to guards is an easy way to have some dragon lairs marked on your map. An example is Shearpoint.

## Bugs

- Respawned dragons found in previously cleared lairs will not always give dragon souls.
  -  The [Unofficial Skyrim Patch](/wiki/Skyrim_Mod:Unofficial_Skyrim_Patch "Skyrim Mod:Unofficial Skyrim Patch"), version 1.0, fixes this bug.
- The miscellaneous objective "Return to [Esbern](/wiki/Skyrim:Esbern "Skyrim:Esbern")" may appear in your quest log upon killing a dragon at any dragon lair; this is related to the bugged quest [Dragon Research](/wiki/Skyrim:Dragon_Research "Skyrim:Dragon Research"). The objective does not update after speaking to Esbern and cannot be completed, unless you clear all dragon lairs before first entering [High Hrothgar](/wiki/Skyrim:High_Hrothgar "Skyrim:High Hrothgar"). Then the bugged quest will not initiate, and all dragon lairs can be cleared (even just before [A Cornered Rat](/wiki/Skyrim:A_Cornered_Rat "Skyrim:A Cornered Rat")).
  -  The [Unofficial Skyrim Patch](/wiki/Skyrim_Mod:Unofficial_Skyrim_Patch "Skyrim Mod:Unofficial Skyrim Patch"), version 1.2.5, fixes this bug.

# Skyrim:Dragon Mounds

## Overview

Dragon Mound near [Kynesgrove](/wiki/Skyrim:Kynesgrove "Skyrim:Kynesgrove")

**Dragon Mounds** are ancient [dragon](/wiki/Skyrim:Dragon "Skyrim:Dragon") burial sites that dot Skyrim's landscape. In appearance, they are simply large, flat, circular areas created out of rings of paving stones. There are no map markers associated with the dragon mounds, and early in the game there is no indication that there is anything remarkable about these features. There are a total of 24 dragon mounds, with 22 being found in Skyrim and two being found on [Solstheim](/wiki/Skyrim:Solstheim "Skyrim:Solstheim").

The dragon mounds were created in the First Era by surviving members of the [Dragon Cult](/wiki/Skyrim:Dragon_Cult "Skyrim:Dragon Cult"), as documented by *[The Dragon War](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Dragon_War "Skyrim:The Dragon War"):*

:   *They built the dragon mounds, entombing the remains of dragons that fell in the war. They believed that one day the dragons would rise again and reward the faithful.*

The *[Atlas of Dragons](/wiki/Skyrim:Atlas_of_Dragons "Skyrim:Atlas of Dragons")* notes the location of a few dragon mounds, but there are few other surviving records of them or their locations.

When the return of the dragons spurs a renewed interest in dragons, the only way to locate all the mounds is to retrieve an ancient [Dragonstone](/wiki/Skyrim:Dragonstone "Skyrim:Dragonstone") from [Bleak Falls Barrow](/wiki/Skyrim:Bleak_Falls_Barrow_(place) "Skyrim:Bleak Falls Barrow (place)"). The back of the stone shows a map of Skyrim, with stars representing the location of each dragon mound. [Delphine](/wiki/Skyrim:Delphine "Skyrim:Delphine") transcribes this information onto a [Map of Dragon Burials](/wiki/Skyrim:Map_of_Dragon_Burials "Skyrim:Map of Dragon Burials"), although Delphine's map is less accurate than the original stone (for example, the mound near [Dawnstar](/wiki/Skyrim:Dawnstar "Skyrim:Dawnstar") is missing from Delphine's map). All 24 dragon mound locations are listed below; for more detailed information, see the [Skyrim map](https://gamemap.uesp.net/sr/?search=Dragon+Mound).

As the [Main Quest](/wiki/Skyrim:Main_Quest "Skyrim:Main Quest") progresses, you learn that the dragons buried in the mounds are not truly dead, and that they are now rising up again. During [A Blade in the Dark](/wiki/Skyrim:A_Blade_in_the_Dark "Skyrim:A Blade in the Dark"), you witness this happening when [Alduin](/wiki/Skyrim:Alduin "Skyrim:Alduin") raises [Sahloknir](/wiki/Skyrim:Sahloknir "Skyrim:Sahloknir") from his mound east of [Kynesgrove](/wiki/Skyrim:Kynesgrove "Skyrim:Kynesgrove") [(map)](https://gamemap.uesp.net/sr/?x=146095&y=13652&zoom=15&legacy=true). From this point in the game onward, dragons will proceed to emerge from their mounds.

### State 0: Dormant

During this state, the dragon mound is closed and looks similar to ancient Nordic burial mounds. All mounds begin in this state.

### State 1: Resurrection

During this state, you will be able to witness Alduin resurrect the dragon from the mound. Alduin will then fly off and the resurrected dragon can then be fought.

### State 2: Awakened

During this state, the dragon has been resurrected by Alduin and the reborn dragon has stayed at the mound to gather its strength.

### State 3: Deserted

During this state, the mound will be open but the dragon will not be near the mound. However the dragon is usually found at a nearby Dragon Lair.

## Notes

- Some dragon mounds may spawn dragons of a much higher level than you would normally expect to encounter at your current character level.

## Bugs

- If you attack Alduin before the resurrection properly commences, the resurrection will not take place. The cylinder of light above the mound will not disappear either.

# Skyrim:Dragon Research

## Overview
