### Main Quest

- **[Before the Storm](/wiki/Skyrim:Before_the_Storm "Skyrim:Before the Storm")**: Inform the [Jarl](/wiki/Skyrim:Balgruuf_the_Greater "Skyrim:Balgruuf the Greater") of [Whiterun](/wiki/Skyrim:Whiterun "Skyrim:Whiterun") about the dragon attack on [Helgen](/wiki/Skyrim:Helgen "Skyrim:Helgen").
- **[Bleak Falls Barrow](/wiki/Skyrim:Bleak_Falls_Barrow_(quest) "Skyrim:Bleak Falls Barrow (quest)")**: Retrieve the [Dragonstone](/wiki/Skyrim:Dragonstone "Skyrim:Dragonstone").
- **[Dragon Rising](/wiki/Skyrim:Dragon_Rising "Skyrim:Dragon Rising")**: Investigate a [dragon](/wiki/Skyrim:Dragon "Skyrim:Dragon") sighting near [Whiterun](/wiki/Skyrim:Whiterun "Skyrim:Whiterun").
- **[Season Unending](/wiki/Skyrim:Season_Unending "Skyrim:Season Unending")**: Enforce a ceasefire to secure Dragonsreach.
- **[The Fallen](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Fallen "Skyrim:The Fallen")**: Capture and interrogate [an ally](/wiki/Skyrim:Odahviing "Skyrim:Odahviing") of [Alduin](/wiki/Skyrim:Alduin "Skyrim:Alduin").

### Civil War Quests

- **[Message to Whiterun](/wiki/Skyrim:Message_to_Whiterun_(Imperial) "Skyrim:Message to Whiterun (Imperial)")**: Deliver the message that will decide [Whiterun](/wiki/Skyrim:Whiterun "Skyrim:Whiterun")'s allegiance.
- **[Message to Whiterun](/wiki/Skyrim:Message_to_Whiterun_(Stormcloaks) "Skyrim:Message to Whiterun (Stormcloaks)")**: Deliver an axe to the [Jarl](/wiki/Skyrim:Balgruuf_the_Greater "Skyrim:Balgruuf the Greater") of [Whiterun](/wiki/Skyrim:Whiterun "Skyrim:Whiterun").
- **[Battle for Whiterun](/wiki/Skyrim:Battle_for_Whiterun_(Imperial) "Skyrim:Battle for Whiterun (Imperial)")**: Protect [Whiterun](/wiki/Skyrim:Whiterun "Skyrim:Whiterun") from the [Stormcloak](/wiki/Skyrim:Stormcloaks "Skyrim:Stormcloaks") invasion. ([radiant](/wiki/Skyrim:Radiant "Skyrim:Radiant"))
- **[Battle for Whiterun](/wiki/Skyrim:Battle_for_Whiterun_(Stormcloaks) "Skyrim:Battle for Whiterun (Stormcloaks)")**: Take [Whiterun](/wiki/Skyrim:Whiterun "Skyrim:Whiterun") in the name of the [Stormcloaks](/wiki/Skyrim:Stormcloaks "Skyrim:Stormcloaks"). ([radiant](/wiki/Skyrim:Radiant "Skyrim:Radiant"))

### Thieves Guild

- **[Imitation Amnesty](/wiki/Skyrim:Imitation_Amnesty "Skyrim:Imitation Amnesty")**: Help get a convicted prisoner released from jail.
- **[No Stone Unturned](/wiki/Skyrim:No_Stone_Unturned "Skyrim:No Stone Unturned")**: Find the [24 gems](/wiki/Skyrim:Unusual_Gem "Skyrim:Unusual Gem") to restore the Crown of Barenziah.

### Dark Brotherhood

- **[Breaching Security](/wiki/Skyrim:Breaching_Security "Skyrim:Breaching Security")**: Kill and frame the [son](/wiki/Skyrim:Gaius_Maro "Skyrim:Gaius Maro") of a high-ranking [Imperial guard](/wiki/Skyrim:Commander_Maro "Skyrim:Commander Maro").

### Other Quests

- **[Beyond the Grave](/wiki/Skyrim:Beyond_the_Grave "Skyrim:Beyond the Grave")**[CC](/wiki/Skyrim:Alternative_Armors_-_Daedric_Plate "Skyrim:Alternative Armors - Daedric Plate"): Follow the trail of a set of valuable [Daedric Plate](/wiki/Skyrim:Daedric_Plate_Armor "Skyrim:Daedric Plate Armor") armor.
- **[Enchanting Tutorial](/wiki/Skyrim:Enchanting_Tutorial "Skyrim:Enchanting Tutorial")**: Use an [Arcane Enchanter](/wiki/Skyrim:Arcane_Enchanter "Skyrim:Arcane Enchanter").
- **[Greatsword for a Great Man](/wiki/Skyrim:Greatsword_for_a_Great_Man "Skyrim:Greatsword for a Great Man")**: Adrianne asks you to deliver a sword to [Proventus Avenicci](/wiki/Skyrim:Proventus_Avenicci "Skyrim:Proventus Avenicci"), her father.
- **[In My Time Of Need](/wiki/Skyrim:In_My_Time_Of_Need "Skyrim:In My Time Of Need")**: Find a [Redguard woman](/wiki/Skyrim:Saadia "Skyrim:Saadia") who is on the run from [her past](/wiki/Lore:Taneth "Lore:Taneth").
- **[In the Shadows](/wiki/Skyrim:In_the_Shadows "Skyrim:In the Shadows")**[CC](/wiki/Skyrim:Bow_of_Shadows "Skyrim:Bow of Shadows"): Save the Jarl of Whiterun from an assassination plot.
- **[Salt for Arcadia](/wiki/Skyrim:Salt_for_Arcadia "Skyrim:Salt for Arcadia")**: [Farengar](/wiki/Skyrim:Farengar_Secret-Fire "Skyrim:Farengar Secret-Fire") asks you to deliver some [frost salts](/wiki/Skyrim:Frost_Salts "Skyrim:Frost Salts") to [Arcadia](/wiki/Skyrim:Arcadia "Skyrim:Arcadia").
- **[The Whispering Door](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Whispering_Door "Skyrim:The Whispering Door")**: Investigate [Nelkir](/wiki/Skyrim:Nelkir "Skyrim:Nelkir")'s story of a Whispering Lady behind a locked door.

### Dragonsreach

Dragonsreach Hall

The hall is focused towards the Jarl's throne, which is visible through the shimmer from the fire, adding a certain mystical quality to his appearance. The entrance room is a waiting area, with four benches for sitting in. The servants [Fianna](/wiki/Skyrim:Fianna "Skyrim:Fianna") and [Gerda](/wiki/Skyrim:Gerda "Skyrim:Gerda") spend most of their time here, keeping it clean. The stairs lead up to the dining area and throne. Centered around a large fire, there are two dining tables with five chairs at each, while up the steps is the throne area and [Jarl Balgruuf's](/wiki/Skyrim:Balgruuf_the_Greater "Skyrim:Balgruuf the Greater") throne, which is on an additionally raised platform. Balgruuf is flanked by two [guards](/wiki/Skyrim:Whiterun_Guard "Skyrim:Whiterun Guard"), his steward [Proventus Avenicci](/wiki/Skyrim:Proventus_Avenicci "Skyrim:Proventus Avenicci"), and his housecarl [Irileth](/wiki/Skyrim:Irileth "Skyrim:Irileth"). His brother [Hrongar](/wiki/Skyrim:Hrongar "Skyrim:Hrongar") acts as an additional guard, but wanders the room, and his court wizard, [Farengar Secret-Fire](/wiki/Skyrim:Farengar_Secret-Fire "Skyrim:Farengar Secret-Fire"), only rarely ventures out of his shop, except when the main quest has progressed to Odahviing's capture. To the left of the throne is a table, and to the right is another table and two bookshelves. The Jarl's three children—[Frothar](/wiki/Skyrim:Frothar "Skyrim:Frothar"), [Nelkir](/wiki/Skyrim:Nelkir "Skyrim:Nelkir") and [Dagny](/wiki/Skyrim:Dagny "Skyrim:Dagny")—have free rein of the palace, and can be found anywhere from the kitchen to the balconies above the hall; sometimes they can even be found outside the palace.

Dragonsreach Kitchen

To the west of the fire is the kitchen, just before which, to the right-hand side and down some steps, is a door to the dungeons, and to the left is a table with some green apples, and two bookshelves. The food table closest to the fire contains [raw meat](/wiki/Skyrim:Food#Raw_Meat "Skyrim:Food"), and on and underneath the other food table are some [food](/wiki/Skyrim:Food "Skyrim:Food") items and some [garlic](/wiki/Skyrim:Garlic "Skyrim:Garlic"), with a cupboard at one end. There are two wardrobes and a cupboard by the southern wall, and a rack with two harvestable [salmon](/wiki/Skyrim:Salmon_(dead) "Skyrim:Salmon (dead)") and one dried [elves ear](/wiki/Skyrim:Elves_Ear "Skyrim:Elves Ear") hanging beside the cupboard. The north wall is mainly a large fireplace with a [cooking spit](/wiki/Skyrim:Cooking_Pot "Skyrim:Cooking Pot") in front of it, with an end table and a cupboard in the eastern corner with some more food items on it. Hanging down from the kitchen's ceiling are two [rabbits](/wiki/Skyrim:Rabbit_(dead) "Skyrim:Rabbit (dead)"), two salmon, three garlic braids, three dried [frost mirriam](/wiki/Skyrim:Frost_Mirriam "Skyrim:Frost Mirriam"), and eight dried elves ear, all of which can be harvested. The northwestern corner leads down some stairs to a storage area and a servants' bedroom. The storage area contains a few sacks and barrels, while the bedroom contains an owned bed, a dresser, an end table, and a chest. A copy of the rare book *[A Dream of Sovngarde](/wiki/Skyrim:A_Dream_of_Sovngarde "Skyrim:A Dream of Sovngarde")* can be found on top of a bookshelf. A door on the western wall leads to the servants' section of the Living Quarters, and to the right of that is another door which leads to a room with more sacks and barrels, and a locked door[†](#intnote_Ebony_Blade).

Dragonsreach Laboratory

To the east of the fire is the court wizard's research and living area. To the right of the door is an additional dining table with two benches and a wardrobe. There is an [alchemy lab](/wiki/Skyrim:Alchemy_Lab "Skyrim:Alchemy Lab"), an [arcane enchanter](/wiki/Skyrim:Arcane_Enchanter "Skyrim:Arcane Enchanter"), a chest, a cupboard, and a large map of [Skyrim](/wiki/Skyrim:Skyrim "Skyrim:Skyrim"). On the desk display are a few [potions](/wiki/Skyrim:Potions "Skyrim:Potions"), a common [soul gem](/wiki/Skyrim:Soul_Gems "Skyrim:Soul Gems"), and a [bone meal](/wiki/Skyrim:Bone_Meal "Skyrim:Bone Meal"), and on the cupboard is a petty soul gem. The study to the left contains a cupboard, a coin purse on the table, and a copy of both *[Lost Legends](/wiki/Skyrim:Lost_Legends "Skyrim:Lost Legends")* and *[The Legend of Red Eagle](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Legend_of_Red_Eagle "Skyrim:The Legend of Red Eagle")* on the bookshelves, which both lead to quests. The bedroom to the right contains an owned bed, an end table, and a dresser. A copy of *[Holdings of Jarl Gjalund](/wiki/Skyrim:Holdings_of_Jarl_Gjalund "Skyrim:Holdings of Jarl Gjalund")* is added to the court wizard's desk at the end of [Bleak Falls Barrow](/wiki/Skyrim:Bleak_Falls_Barrow_(quest) "Skyrim:Bleak Falls Barrow (quest)"). Nothing on the court wizard's desk is free to take.

At the top of the stairs to the side of the Jarl is his war room. Contained here are a chest, an end table, and two wardrobes. The balconies to either side are accessible from here, although there is nothing to be found on them. On the end table is a display case with an Apprentice-level lock containing a leveled [dagger](/wiki/Skyrim:Dagger "Skyrim:Dagger"), and on the bookshelves beside that is a copy of the hard-to-find *[The Wolf Queen, v6](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Wolf_Queen,_v6 "Skyrim:The Wolf Queen, v6")*, and a copy of *[An Explorer's Guide to Skyrim](/wiki/Skyrim:An_Explorer%27s_Guide_to_Skyrim "Skyrim:An Explorer's Guide to Skyrim")*, which adds some map markers. There are two maps on the table and two on the wall behind it. The left-hand map on the table and the right-hand map on the wall show the different [Hold](/wiki/Skyrim:Holds "Skyrim:Holds") borders and their [capitals](/wiki/Skyrim:Cities "Skyrim:Cities"). The left-hand map on the wall is a detailed map of Skyrim, and the left-hand map in the table is also a detailed map, with the addition of little colored flags, which can be activated to add locations to your map. The red flags mark [Imperial](/wiki/Skyrim:Imperial_Legion "Skyrim:Imperial Legion")-held cities, towns, and forts, while the blue flags mark [Stormcloak](/wiki/Skyrim:Stormcloaks "Skyrim:Stormcloaks")-held locations. This map and others similar to it will update to show the changes made during any [Civil War](/wiki/Skyrim:Civil_War "Skyrim:Civil War") quests. Doors to the Jarl's Quarters and the Great Porch are to the east and north, respectively.

[†](#note_Ebony_Blade)The locked room contains the book *[Admonition Against Ebony](/wiki/Skyrim:Admonition_Against_Ebony "Skyrim:Admonition Against Ebony")* and the [Ebony Blade](/wiki/Skyrim:Ebony_Blade "Skyrim:Ebony Blade"). It can only be unlocked during the quest [The Whispering Door](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Whispering_Door "Skyrim:The Whispering Door") with a [key](/wiki/Skyrim:Whispering_Door_Key "Skyrim:Whispering Door Key") obtained from either Balgruuf or Farengar.

### Dragonsreach Jarl's Quarters

There are six bedrooms here, for all the palace's residents, and a door to an outdoor balcony that overlooks all of Whiterun. In the hall at the bottom of the stairs are four display cases; three with Apprentice-level locks and one with a Master-level lock. The master-locked case has an [elven sword](/wiki/Skyrim:Elven_Sword "Skyrim:Elven Sword"), the case to the east has a [Whiterun Guard's armor](/wiki/Skyrim:Whiterun_Guard%27s_Armor "Skyrim:Whiterun Guard's Armor") and shield, the case to the north has a [steel dagger](/wiki/Skyrim:Steel_Dagger "Skyrim:Steel Dagger") and a [banded iron shield](/wiki/Skyrim:Banded_Iron_Shield "Skyrim:Banded Iron Shield"), and the case to the west has a few household items. There are three flower beds which contain three [lavender](/wiki/Skyrim:Lavender "Skyrim:Lavender") plants each, one at the bottom of the stairs and two at the top.

To the northeast of the hall lies [Proventus](/wiki/Skyrim:Proventus_Avenicci "Skyrim:Proventus Avenicci")'s room, which contains his bed, three wardrobes, a chest, and a display case with an Adept-level lock containing a necklace. On both sides of the chest is a potion. The stairs lead to the servants' quarters, which are divided into five rooms: a dining room with a larder, a sitting room, and two small bedrooms. There are a few wardrobes, chests, barrels, and sacks spread throughout these rooms, and the door to the Main Hall storage room is here.

To the left at the top of the stairs is [Hrongar](/wiki/Skyrim:Hrongar "Skyrim:Hrongar")'s room, which contains his bed, two end tables, a dresser, a cupboard, two [silver ingots](/wiki/Skyrim:Silver "Skyrim:Silver"), and a coin purse.

Opposite to Hrongar's room is the children's room, which contains the three children's beds, an end table, a dresser, a wardrobe, a chest at the bottom of each bed and on the end table is a silver sapphire necklace.

The [Jarl](/wiki/Skyrim:Balgruuf_the_Greater "Skyrim:Balgruuf the Greater")'s room has three sections: a dining room, a study, and his bedroom. In the study is the [Illusion](/wiki/Skyrim:Illusion "Skyrim:Illusion") [skill book](/wiki/Skyrim:Skill_Books "Skyrim:Skill Books") *[Before the Ages of Man](/wiki/Skyrim:Before_the_Ages_of_Man "Skyrim:Before the Ages of Man")*, two coin purses, a leveled [Paralysis](/wiki/Skyrim:Paralysis "Skyrim:Paralysis") potion, and seven silver ingots. The Jarl's bed is surrounded by two end tables and three wardrobes. On the end table to the right is an [Unusual Gem](/wiki/Skyrim:Unusual_Gem "Skyrim:Unusual Gem"). The door leads to an outside balcony from which you can see all of Whiterun; it is also possible to make out [Honningbrew Meadery](/wiki/Skyrim:Honningbrew_Meadery "Skyrim:Honningbrew Meadery") to the south and [Bleak Falls Barrow](/wiki/Skyrim:Bleak_Falls_Barrow_(place) "Skyrim:Bleak Falls Barrow (place)") in the mountains to the southeast.

### Dragonsreach, Great Porch

Dragonsreach Great Porch

The porch is used as a practice room for the guards and an additional dining area for the Jarl. Just before the dining table are two flower beds with two [lavender](/wiki/Skyrim:Lavender "Skyrim:Lavender") plants each. There are large piles of hay with a training dummy surrounding two large mechanisms, which are revealed to be parts of a dragon trap during [The Fallen](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Fallen "Skyrim:The Fallen"). On both sides of the door are a set of stairs which lead to a small balcony at either side. On the pillars above the mechanisms are pull chains, which, when pulled, do nothing; they are used in the aforementioned quest. The porch faces slightly northeast, and to the north can be seen [Whitewatch Tower](/wiki/Skyrim:Whitewatch_Tower "Skyrim:Whitewatch Tower") and [Loreius Farm](/wiki/Skyrim:Loreius_Farm "Skyrim:Loreius Farm").

### Dragonsreach Dungeon

Dragonsreach Dungeon

The Dungeon contains four cells kept by three guards. The cell that you occupy if you are arrested has an "Escape Route" [shadowmark](/wiki/Skyrim:Shadowmarks_(Thieves_Guild) "Skyrim:Shadowmarks (Thieves Guild)") to the right of the novice-locked grate and a dead [bandit](/wiki/Skyrim:Bandit "Skyrim:Bandit"). Three of the cells are adept-locked and contain cots that can be used at any time. One of them contains a dead prisoner. The third cell is unlockable and is where an [Alik'r warrior](/wiki/Skyrim:Alik%27r_Prisoner "Skyrim:Alik'r Prisoner") is imprisoned during [In My Time Of Need](/wiki/Skyrim:In_My_Time_Of_Need "Skyrim:In My Time Of Need"). At both ends of the main section are some barrels and sacks. The room to the northwest has an Adept-level lock, serves as a dining room for the guards, and contains some food and barrels. A second room is furnished with four beds for the guards. The room to the southeast is the public side of the jail. There is nearly always a guard on duty at the desk. The prisoners' belongings chest and the evidence chest sit in the eastern corner. After [Dampened Spirits](/wiki/Skyrim:Dampened_Spirits "Skyrim:Dampened Spirits"), [Sabjorn](/wiki/Skyrim:Sabjorn "Skyrim:Sabjorn") resides in the dungeon but comes and goes freely. He sleeps in one of the cells, but walks around outside the cells without harassment.

The escape tunnel is a virtually linear path from the locked grate to the [Guard Barracks](/wiki/Skyrim:Guard_Barracks "Skyrim:Guard Barracks"), and contains a [fly amanita](/wiki/Skyrim:Fly_Amanita "Skyrim:Fly Amanita") plant, a [hanging moss](/wiki/Skyrim:Hanging_Moss "Skyrim:Hanging Moss") plant, and nine torches. Nothing in the Dungeon is free to take, except for the torches.

## Notes

- The books *[Lost Legends](/wiki/Skyrim:Lost_Legends "Skyrim:Lost Legends")* and *[The Legend of Red Eagle](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Legend_of_Red_Eagle "Skyrim:The Legend of Red Eagle")* (both quest starters) can be found in Farengar's study.
- The book *[An Explorer's Guide to Skyrim](/wiki/Skyrim:An_Explorer%27s_Guide_to_Skyrim "Skyrim:An Explorer's Guide to Skyrim")*, which adds map markers, can be found by the map table.
- Dragonsreach is mentioned in the books *[A Gentleman's Guide to Whiterun](/wiki/Skyrim:A_Gentleman%27s_Guide_to_Whiterun "Skyrim:A Gentleman's Guide to Whiterun")*, *[Olaf and the Dragon](/wiki/Skyrim:Olaf_and_the_Dragon "Skyrim:Olaf and the Dragon")*, and *[Adonato's Book](/wiki/Skyrim:Adonato%27s_Book "Skyrim:Adonato's Book")*.
- According to [Proventus Avenicci](/wiki/Skyrim:Proventus_Avenicci "Skyrim:Proventus Avenicci"), Dragonsreach allows Balgruuf to see everything that happens in Whiterun.
- Once you have completed [Dragon Rising](/wiki/Skyrim:Dragon_Rising "Skyrim:Dragon Rising"), the Jarl's bed is usable and all low-level items are free to take.

## Bugs

- If one is facing the door to Dragonsreach and going over to the left side of the drawbridge, then going over to the top of the stairs and standing on the left of it next to the draw bridge, it is possible to slip under Dragonsreach and walk under the map.
  -  The [Unofficial Skyrim Patch](/wiki/Skyrim_Mod:Unofficial_Skyrim_Patch "Skyrim Mod:Unofficial Skyrim Patch"), version 1.2, fixes this bug.
- The cell where the [Alik'r Prisoner](/wiki/Skyrim:Alik%27r_Prisoner "Skyrim:Alik'r Prisoner") gets sent to during "[In My Time Of Need](/wiki/Skyrim:In_My_Time_Of_Need "Skyrim:In My Time Of Need")" cannot be unlocked.
  -  The [Unofficial Skyrim Patch](/wiki/Skyrim_Mod:Unofficial_Skyrim_Patch "Skyrim Mod:Unofficial Skyrim Patch"), version 1.2.4, addresses this issue. The door will now open with the Whiterun Jail Key like all the others.
- Starting from the balcony on the Great Porch, it is possible to use [Whirlwind Sprint](/wiki/Skyrim:Whirlwind_Sprint "Skyrim:Whirlwind Sprint") to fly over the porch edge. Surviving the fall can potentially leave you stuck underneath the map. **?**
- The books on the large table near the Prisoner's Belongings Chest and Evidence Chest in the Dungeon may clip through the table and into each other. **?**
- If you talk to a guard on the Great Porch while he aims his bow, he may stop firing and freeze, though he'll still react if you talk to him. **?**
  - Exit and re-enter the Great Porch, and he'll no longer be frozen.
- If Brill is killed while he is steward to Vignar Gray-Mane (after the [Battle for Whiterun](/wiki/Skyrim:Battle_for_Whiterun_(Stormcloaks) "Skyrim:Battle for Whiterun (Stormcloaks)")), Proventus Avenicci will return from exile to replace him in this position. He will offer the same dialogue as if Jarl Balgruuf still controlled Whiterun.
  -  The [Unofficial Skyrim Patch](/wiki/Skyrim_Mod:Unofficial_Skyrim_Patch "Skyrim Mod:Unofficial Skyrim Patch"), version 1.2.2, addresses this issue. Like other stewards, Brill has been made [essential](/wiki/Skyrim:Essential_NPCs "Skyrim:Essential NPCs").
- If Balgruuf is exiled to the [Blue Palace](/wiki/Skyrim:Blue_Palace "Skyrim:Blue Palace"), his children do not move with him, and they will act the same as if he was still there.
  -  The [Unofficial Skyrim Patch](/wiki/Skyrim_Mod:Unofficial_Skyrim_Patch "Skyrim Mod:Unofficial Skyrim Patch"), version 1.2.2, addresses this issue. His children will move with him to the Blue Palace.

Dragonsreach

**Dragonsreach** is the residence of the [Jarl](/wiki/Skyrim:Jarl "Skyrim:Jarl") of [Whiterun Hold](/wiki/Skyrim:Whiterun_Hold "Skyrim:Whiterun Hold"), the hold's seat of political power, and the location of the hold's jail.

Concept Art of Dragonsreach

Dragonsreach with the Throat of the World looming in the background

It is initially occupied by [Balgruuf the Greater](/wiki/Skyrim:Balgruuf_the_Greater "Skyrim:Balgruuf the Greater") and his court, but may be seized by [Vignar Gray-Mane](/wiki/Skyrim:Vignar_Gray-Mane "Skyrim:Vignar Gray-Mane") if the [Stormcloak Rebels](/wiki/Skyrim:Stormcloaks "Skyrim:Stormcloaks") prevail in the [Civil War](/wiki/Skyrim:Civil_War "Skyrim:Civil War"). The palace, which is divided into four sections - *[Dragonsreach](#Dragonsreach)*, the *[Jarl's Quarters](#Dragonsreach_Jarl.27s_Quarters)*, the *[Great Porch](#Dragonsreach.2C_Great_Porch)*, and the *[Dungeon](#Dragonsreach_Dungeon)* - is in the Cloud District of [Whiterun](/wiki/Skyrim:Whiterun "Skyrim:Whiterun"), overlooking the city.

The main entrance is at the top of three flights of stairs starting from the [Gildergreen](/wiki/Lore:Gildergreen "Lore:Gildergreen") tree, with two pools intersected by the stairs. There are four doors to the outside, though only two are accessible from the ground: one opens to the main hall, while the other leads to the dungeon, which serves as the hold's jail. A third door opens to a balcony high above ground from the living quarters and the other opens to the Great Porch from the main hall. The palace was built around a [dragon](/wiki/Skyrim:Dragon "Skyrim:Dragon") supposedly captured by [Olaf One-Eye](/wiki/Skyrim:Olaf_One-Eye "Skyrim:Olaf One-Eye") and imprisoned in the present-day Great Porch.

Around the first pool are a few specimens of [hanging moss](/wiki/Skyrim:Hanging_Moss "Skyrim:Hanging Moss"). In the second pool, there is a skeleton, eight [Nordic barnacle clusters](/wiki/Skyrim:Nordic_Barnacle "Skyrim:Nordic Barnacle"), and some [salmon](/wiki/Skyrim:Salmon_(creature) "Skyrim:Salmon (creature)"). To the left side of the second pool are two [lavender](/wiki/Skyrim:Lavender "Skyrim:Lavender") plants, and to the right are another three lavender plants and the door to the dungeon.

\* If the Stormcloaks capture Whiterun, these people will be exiled to the [Blue Palace](/wiki/Skyrim:Blue_Palace "Skyrim:Blue Palace") in [Solitude](/wiki/Skyrim:Solitude "Skyrim:Solitude") (Balgruuf's children will not, see [bugs](#Bugs)).
\*\* Until the Stormcloaks capture Whiterun, these people reside in [Jorrvaskr](/wiki/Skyrim:Jorrvaskr "Skyrim:Jorrvaskr").
† Until the Stormcloaks capture Whiterun, [Olfina Gray-Mane](/wiki/Skyrim:Olfina_Gray-Mane "Skyrim:Olfina Gray-Mane") resides in [House Gray-Mane.](/wiki/Skyrim:House_Gray-Mane "Skyrim:House Gray-Mane")
‡ Depending on who wins the battle for Whiterun, the guards are replaced by either [Imperial soldiers](/wiki/Skyrim:Imperial_Soldier "Skyrim:Imperial Soldier") or [Stormcloak soldiers](/wiki/Skyrim:Stormcloak_Soldier "Skyrim:Stormcloak Soldier").

### Main Quest

- **[Before the Storm](/wiki/Skyrim:Before_the_Storm "Skyrim:Before the Storm")**: Inform the [Jarl](/wiki/Skyrim:Balgruuf_the_Greater "Skyrim:Balgruuf the Greater") of [Whiterun](/wiki/Skyrim:Whiterun "Skyrim:Whiterun") about the dragon attack on [Helgen](/wiki/Skyrim:Helgen "Skyrim:Helgen").
- **[Bleak Falls Barrow](/wiki/Skyrim:Bleak_Falls_Barrow_(quest) "Skyrim:Bleak Falls Barrow (quest)")**: Retrieve the [Dragonstone](/wiki/Skyrim:Dragonstone "Skyrim:Dragonstone").
- **[Dragon Rising](/wiki/Skyrim:Dragon_Rising "Skyrim:Dragon Rising")**: Investigate a [dragon](/wiki/Skyrim:Dragon "Skyrim:Dragon") sighting near [Whiterun](/wiki/Skyrim:Whiterun "Skyrim:Whiterun").
- **[Season Unending](/wiki/Skyrim:Season_Unending "Skyrim:Season Unending")**: Enforce a ceasefire to secure Dragonsreach.
- **[The Fallen](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Fallen "Skyrim:The Fallen")**: Capture and interrogate [an ally](/wiki/Skyrim:Odahviing "Skyrim:Odahviing") of [Alduin](/wiki/Skyrim:Alduin "Skyrim:Alduin").

### Civil War Quests

- **[Message to Whiterun](/wiki/Skyrim:Message_to_Whiterun_(Imperial) "Skyrim:Message to Whiterun (Imperial)")**: Deliver the message that will decide [Whiterun](/wiki/Skyrim:Whiterun "Skyrim:Whiterun")'s allegiance.
- **[Message to Whiterun](/wiki/Skyrim:Message_to_Whiterun_(Stormcloaks) "Skyrim:Message to Whiterun (Stormcloaks)")**: Deliver an axe to the [Jarl](/wiki/Skyrim:Balgruuf_the_Greater "Skyrim:Balgruuf the Greater") of [Whiterun](/wiki/Skyrim:Whiterun "Skyrim:Whiterun").
- **[Battle for Whiterun](/wiki/Skyrim:Battle_for_Whiterun_(Imperial) "Skyrim:Battle for Whiterun (Imperial)")**: Protect [Whiterun](/wiki/Skyrim:Whiterun "Skyrim:Whiterun") from the [Stormcloak](/wiki/Skyrim:Stormcloaks "Skyrim:Stormcloaks") invasion. ([radiant](/wiki/Skyrim:Radiant "Skyrim:Radiant"))
- **[Battle for Whiterun](/wiki/Skyrim:Battle_for_Whiterun_(Stormcloaks) "Skyrim:Battle for Whiterun (Stormcloaks)")**: Take [Whiterun](/wiki/Skyrim:Whiterun "Skyrim:Whiterun") in the name of the [Stormcloaks](/wiki/Skyrim:Stormcloaks "Skyrim:Stormcloaks"). ([radiant](/wiki/Skyrim:Radiant "Skyrim:Radiant"))

### Thieves Guild

- **[Imitation Amnesty](/wiki/Skyrim:Imitation_Amnesty "Skyrim:Imitation Amnesty")**: Help get a convicted prisoner released from jail.
- **[No Stone Unturned](/wiki/Skyrim:No_Stone_Unturned "Skyrim:No Stone Unturned")**: Find the [24 gems](/wiki/Skyrim:Unusual_Gem "Skyrim:Unusual Gem") to restore the Crown of Barenziah.

### Dark Brotherhood

- **[Breaching Security](/wiki/Skyrim:Breaching_Security "Skyrim:Breaching Security")**: Kill and frame the [son](/wiki/Skyrim:Gaius_Maro "Skyrim:Gaius Maro") of a high-ranking [Imperial guard](/wiki/Skyrim:Commander_Maro "Skyrim:Commander Maro").

### Other Quests

- **[Beyond the Grave](/wiki/Skyrim:Beyond_the_Grave "Skyrim:Beyond the Grave")**[CC](/wiki/Skyrim:Alternative_Armors_-_Daedric_Plate "Skyrim:Alternative Armors - Daedric Plate"): Follow the trail of a set of valuable [Daedric Plate](/wiki/Skyrim:Daedric_Plate_Armor "Skyrim:Daedric Plate Armor") armor.
- **[Enchanting Tutorial](/wiki/Skyrim:Enchanting_Tutorial "Skyrim:Enchanting Tutorial")**: Use an [Arcane Enchanter](/wiki/Skyrim:Arcane_Enchanter "Skyrim:Arcane Enchanter").
- **[Greatsword for a Great Man](/wiki/Skyrim:Greatsword_for_a_Great_Man "Skyrim:Greatsword for a Great Man")**: Adrianne asks you to deliver a sword to [Proventus Avenicci](/wiki/Skyrim:Proventus_Avenicci "Skyrim:Proventus Avenicci"), her father.
- **[In My Time Of Need](/wiki/Skyrim:In_My_Time_Of_Need "Skyrim:In My Time Of Need")**: Find a [Redguard woman](/wiki/Skyrim:Saadia "Skyrim:Saadia") who is on the run from [her past](/wiki/Lore:Taneth "Lore:Taneth").
- **[In the Shadows](/wiki/Skyrim:In_the_Shadows "Skyrim:In the Shadows")**[CC](/wiki/Skyrim:Bow_of_Shadows "Skyrim:Bow of Shadows"): Save the Jarl of Whiterun from an assassination plot.
- **[Salt for Arcadia](/wiki/Skyrim:Salt_for_Arcadia "Skyrim:Salt for Arcadia")**: [Farengar](/wiki/Skyrim:Farengar_Secret-Fire "Skyrim:Farengar Secret-Fire") asks you to deliver some [frost salts](/wiki/Skyrim:Frost_Salts "Skyrim:Frost Salts") to [Arcadia](/wiki/Skyrim:Arcadia "Skyrim:Arcadia").
- **[The Whispering Door](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Whispering_Door "Skyrim:The Whispering Door")**: Investigate [Nelkir](/wiki/Skyrim:Nelkir "Skyrim:Nelkir")'s story of a Whispering Lady behind a locked door.

### Dragonsreach

Dragonsreach Hall

The hall is focused towards the Jarl's throne, which is visible through the shimmer from the fire, adding a certain mystical quality to his appearance. The entrance room is a waiting area, with four benches for sitting in. The servants [Fianna](/wiki/Skyrim:Fianna "Skyrim:Fianna") and [Gerda](/wiki/Skyrim:Gerda "Skyrim:Gerda") spend most of their time here, keeping it clean. The stairs lead up to the dining area and throne. Centered around a large fire, there are two dining tables with five chairs at each, while up the steps is the throne area and [Jarl Balgruuf's](/wiki/Skyrim:Balgruuf_the_Greater "Skyrim:Balgruuf the Greater") throne, which is on an additionally raised platform. Balgruuf is flanked by two [guards](/wiki/Skyrim:Whiterun_Guard "Skyrim:Whiterun Guard"), his steward [Proventus Avenicci](/wiki/Skyrim:Proventus_Avenicci "Skyrim:Proventus Avenicci"), and his housecarl [Irileth](/wiki/Skyrim:Irileth "Skyrim:Irileth"). His brother [Hrongar](/wiki/Skyrim:Hrongar "Skyrim:Hrongar") acts as an additional guard, but wanders the room, and his court wizard, [Farengar Secret-Fire](/wiki/Skyrim:Farengar_Secret-Fire "Skyrim:Farengar Secret-Fire"), only rarely ventures out of his shop, except when the main quest has progressed to Odahviing's capture. To the left of the throne is a table, and to the right is another table and two bookshelves. The Jarl's three children—[Frothar](/wiki/Skyrim:Frothar "Skyrim:Frothar"), [Nelkir](/wiki/Skyrim:Nelkir "Skyrim:Nelkir") and [Dagny](/wiki/Skyrim:Dagny "Skyrim:Dagny")—have free rein of the palace, and can be found anywhere from the kitchen to the balconies above the hall; sometimes they can even be found outside the palace.

Dragonsreach Kitchen

To the west of the fire is the kitchen, just before which, to the right-hand side and down some steps, is a door to the dungeons, and to the left is a table with some green apples, and two bookshelves. The food table closest to the fire contains [raw meat](/wiki/Skyrim:Food#Raw_Meat "Skyrim:Food"), and on and underneath the other food table are some [food](/wiki/Skyrim:Food "Skyrim:Food") items and some [garlic](/wiki/Skyrim:Garlic "Skyrim:Garlic"), with a cupboard at one end. There are two wardrobes and a cupboard by the southern wall, and a rack with two harvestable [salmon](/wiki/Skyrim:Salmon_(dead) "Skyrim:Salmon (dead)") and one dried [elves ear](/wiki/Skyrim:Elves_Ear "Skyrim:Elves Ear") hanging beside the cupboard. The north wall is mainly a large fireplace with a [cooking spit](/wiki/Skyrim:Cooking_Pot "Skyrim:Cooking Pot") in front of it, with an end table and a cupboard in the eastern corner with some more food items on it. Hanging down from the kitchen's ceiling are two [rabbits](/wiki/Skyrim:Rabbit_(dead) "Skyrim:Rabbit (dead)"), two salmon, three garlic braids, three dried [frost mirriam](/wiki/Skyrim:Frost_Mirriam "Skyrim:Frost Mirriam"), and eight dried elves ear, all of which can be harvested. The northwestern corner leads down some stairs to a storage area and a servants' bedroom. The storage area contains a few sacks and barrels, while the bedroom contains an owned bed, a dresser, an end table, and a chest. A copy of the rare book *[A Dream of Sovngarde](/wiki/Skyrim:A_Dream_of_Sovngarde "Skyrim:A Dream of Sovngarde")* can be found on top of a bookshelf. A door on the western wall leads to the servants' section of the Living Quarters, and to the right of that is another door which leads to a room with more sacks and barrels, and a locked door[†](#intnote_Ebony_Blade).

Dragonsreach Laboratory

To the east of the fire is the court wizard's research and living area. To the right of the door is an additional dining table with two benches and a wardrobe. There is an [alchemy lab](/wiki/Skyrim:Alchemy_Lab "Skyrim:Alchemy Lab"), an [arcane enchanter](/wiki/Skyrim:Arcane_Enchanter "Skyrim:Arcane Enchanter"), a chest, a cupboard, and a large map of [Skyrim](/wiki/Skyrim:Skyrim "Skyrim:Skyrim"). On the desk display are a few [potions](/wiki/Skyrim:Potions "Skyrim:Potions"), a common [soul gem](/wiki/Skyrim:Soul_Gems "Skyrim:Soul Gems"), and a [bone meal](/wiki/Skyrim:Bone_Meal "Skyrim:Bone Meal"), and on the cupboard is a petty soul gem. The study to the left contains a cupboard, a coin purse on the table, and a copy of both *[Lost Legends](/wiki/Skyrim:Lost_Legends "Skyrim:Lost Legends")* and *[The Legend of Red Eagle](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Legend_of_Red_Eagle "Skyrim:The Legend of Red Eagle")* on the bookshelves, which both lead to quests. The bedroom to the right contains an owned bed, an end table, and a dresser. A copy of *[Holdings of Jarl Gjalund](/wiki/Skyrim:Holdings_of_Jarl_Gjalund "Skyrim:Holdings of Jarl Gjalund")* is added to the court wizard's desk at the end of [Bleak Falls Barrow](/wiki/Skyrim:Bleak_Falls_Barrow_(quest) "Skyrim:Bleak Falls Barrow (quest)"). Nothing on the court wizard's desk is free to take.

At the top of the stairs to the side of the Jarl is his war room. Contained here are a chest, an end table, and two wardrobes. The balconies to either side are accessible from here, although there is nothing to be found on them. On the end table is a display case with an Apprentice-level lock containing a leveled [dagger](/wiki/Skyrim:Dagger "Skyrim:Dagger"), and on the bookshelves beside that is a copy of the hard-to-find *[The Wolf Queen, v6](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Wolf_Queen,_v6 "Skyrim:The Wolf Queen, v6")*, and a copy of *[An Explorer's Guide to Skyrim](/wiki/Skyrim:An_Explorer%27s_Guide_to_Skyrim "Skyrim:An Explorer's Guide to Skyrim")*, which adds some map markers. There are two maps on the table and two on the wall behind it. The left-hand map on the table and the right-hand map on the wall show the different [Hold](/wiki/Skyrim:Holds "Skyrim:Holds") borders and their [capitals](/wiki/Skyrim:Cities "Skyrim:Cities"). The left-hand map on the wall is a detailed map of Skyrim, and the left-hand map in the table is also a detailed map, with the addition of little colored flags, which can be activated to add locations to your map. The red flags mark [Imperial](/wiki/Skyrim:Imperial_Legion "Skyrim:Imperial Legion")-held cities, towns, and forts, while the blue flags mark [Stormcloak](/wiki/Skyrim:Stormcloaks "Skyrim:Stormcloaks")-held locations. This map and others similar to it will update to show the changes made during any [Civil War](/wiki/Skyrim:Civil_War "Skyrim:Civil War") quests. Doors to the Jarl's Quarters and the Great Porch are to the east and north, respectively.

[†](#note_Ebony_Blade)The locked room contains the book *[Admonition Against Ebony](/wiki/Skyrim:Admonition_Against_Ebony "Skyrim:Admonition Against Ebony")* and the [Ebony Blade](/wiki/Skyrim:Ebony_Blade "Skyrim:Ebony Blade"). It can only be unlocked during the quest [The Whispering Door](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Whispering_Door "Skyrim:The Whispering Door") with a [key](/wiki/Skyrim:Whispering_Door_Key "Skyrim:Whispering Door Key") obtained from either Balgruuf or Farengar.

### Dragonsreach Jarl's Quarters

There are six bedrooms here, for all the palace's residents, and a door to an outdoor balcony that overlooks all of Whiterun. In the hall at the bottom of the stairs are four display cases; three with Apprentice-level locks and one with a Master-level lock. The master-locked case has an [elven sword](/wiki/Skyrim:Elven_Sword "Skyrim:Elven Sword"), the case to the east has a [Whiterun Guard's armor](/wiki/Skyrim:Whiterun_Guard%27s_Armor "Skyrim:Whiterun Guard's Armor") and shield, the case to the north has a [steel dagger](/wiki/Skyrim:Steel_Dagger "Skyrim:Steel Dagger") and a [banded iron shield](/wiki/Skyrim:Banded_Iron_Shield "Skyrim:Banded Iron Shield"), and the case to the west has a few household items. There are three flower beds which contain three [lavender](/wiki/Skyrim:Lavender "Skyrim:Lavender") plants each, one at the bottom of the stairs and two at the top.

To the northeast of the hall lies [Proventus](/wiki/Skyrim:Proventus_Avenicci "Skyrim:Proventus Avenicci")'s room, which contains his bed, three wardrobes, a chest, and a display case with an Adept-level lock containing a necklace. On both sides of the chest is a potion. The stairs lead to the servants' quarters, which are divided into five rooms: a dining room with a larder, a sitting room, and two small bedrooms. There are a few wardrobes, chests, barrels, and sacks spread throughout these rooms, and the door to the Main Hall storage room is here.

To the left at the top of the stairs is [Hrongar](/wiki/Skyrim:Hrongar "Skyrim:Hrongar")'s room, which contains his bed, two end tables, a dresser, a cupboard, two [silver ingots](/wiki/Skyrim:Silver "Skyrim:Silver"), and a coin purse.

Opposite to Hrongar's room is the children's room, which contains the three children's beds, an end table, a dresser, a wardrobe, a chest at the bottom of each bed and on the end table is a silver sapphire necklace.

The [Jarl](/wiki/Skyrim:Balgruuf_the_Greater "Skyrim:Balgruuf the Greater")'s room has three sections: a dining room, a study, and his bedroom. In the study is the [Illusion](/wiki/Skyrim:Illusion "Skyrim:Illusion") [skill book](/wiki/Skyrim:Skill_Books "Skyrim:Skill Books") *[Before the Ages of Man](/wiki/Skyrim:Before_the_Ages_of_Man "Skyrim:Before the Ages of Man")*, two coin purses, a leveled [Paralysis](/wiki/Skyrim:Paralysis "Skyrim:Paralysis") potion, and seven silver ingots. The Jarl's bed is surrounded by two end tables and three wardrobes. On the end table to the right is an [Unusual Gem](/wiki/Skyrim:Unusual_Gem "Skyrim:Unusual Gem"). The door leads to an outside balcony from which you can see all of Whiterun; it is also possible to make out [Honningbrew Meadery](/wiki/Skyrim:Honningbrew_Meadery "Skyrim:Honningbrew Meadery") to the south and [Bleak Falls Barrow](/wiki/Skyrim:Bleak_Falls_Barrow_(place) "Skyrim:Bleak Falls Barrow (place)") in the mountains to the southeast.

### Dragonsreach, Great Porch

Dragonsreach Great Porch

The porch is used as a practice room for the guards and an additional dining area for the Jarl. Just before the dining table are two flower beds with two [lavender](/wiki/Skyrim:Lavender "Skyrim:Lavender") plants each. There are large piles of hay with a training dummy surrounding two large mechanisms, which are revealed to be parts of a dragon trap during [The Fallen](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Fallen "Skyrim:The Fallen"). On both sides of the door are a set of stairs which lead to a small balcony at either side. On the pillars above the mechanisms are pull chains, which, when pulled, do nothing; they are used in the aforementioned quest. The porch faces slightly northeast, and to the north can be seen [Whitewatch Tower](/wiki/Skyrim:Whitewatch_Tower "Skyrim:Whitewatch Tower") and [Loreius Farm](/wiki/Skyrim:Loreius_Farm "Skyrim:Loreius Farm").

### Dragonsreach Dungeon

Dragonsreach Dungeon

The Dungeon contains four cells kept by three guards. The cell that you occupy if you are arrested has an "Escape Route" [shadowmark](/wiki/Skyrim:Shadowmarks_(Thieves_Guild) "Skyrim:Shadowmarks (Thieves Guild)") to the right of the novice-locked grate and a dead [bandit](/wiki/Skyrim:Bandit "Skyrim:Bandit"). Three of the cells are adept-locked and contain cots that can be used at any time. One of them contains a dead prisoner. The third cell is unlockable and is where an [Alik'r warrior](/wiki/Skyrim:Alik%27r_Prisoner "Skyrim:Alik'r Prisoner") is imprisoned during [In My Time Of Need](/wiki/Skyrim:In_My_Time_Of_Need "Skyrim:In My Time Of Need"). At both ends of the main section are some barrels and sacks. The room to the northwest has an Adept-level lock, serves as a dining room for the guards, and contains some food and barrels. A second room is furnished with four beds for the guards. The room to the southeast is the public side of the jail. There is nearly always a guard on duty at the desk. The prisoners' belongings chest and the evidence chest sit in the eastern corner. After [Dampened Spirits](/wiki/Skyrim:Dampened_Spirits "Skyrim:Dampened Spirits"), [Sabjorn](/wiki/Skyrim:Sabjorn "Skyrim:Sabjorn") resides in the dungeon but comes and goes freely. He sleeps in one of the cells, but walks around outside the cells without harassment.

The escape tunnel is a virtually linear path from the locked grate to the [Guard Barracks](/wiki/Skyrim:Guard_Barracks "Skyrim:Guard Barracks"), and contains a [fly amanita](/wiki/Skyrim:Fly_Amanita "Skyrim:Fly Amanita") plant, a [hanging moss](/wiki/Skyrim:Hanging_Moss "Skyrim:Hanging Moss") plant, and nine torches. Nothing in the Dungeon is free to take, except for the torches.

## Notes

- The books *[Lost Legends](/wiki/Skyrim:Lost_Legends "Skyrim:Lost Legends")* and *[The Legend of Red Eagle](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Legend_of_Red_Eagle "Skyrim:The Legend of Red Eagle")* (both quest starters) can be found in Farengar's study.
- The book *[An Explorer's Guide to Skyrim](/wiki/Skyrim:An_Explorer%27s_Guide_to_Skyrim "Skyrim:An Explorer's Guide to Skyrim")*, which adds map markers, can be found by the map table.
- Dragonsreach is mentioned in the books *[A Gentleman's Guide to Whiterun](/wiki/Skyrim:A_Gentleman%27s_Guide_to_Whiterun "Skyrim:A Gentleman's Guide to Whiterun")*, *[Olaf and the Dragon](/wiki/Skyrim:Olaf_and_the_Dragon "Skyrim:Olaf and the Dragon")*, and *[Adonato's Book](/wiki/Skyrim:Adonato%27s_Book "Skyrim:Adonato's Book")*.
- According to [Proventus Avenicci](/wiki/Skyrim:Proventus_Avenicci "Skyrim:Proventus Avenicci"), Dragonsreach allows Balgruuf to see everything that happens in Whiterun.
- Once you have completed [Dragon Rising](/wiki/Skyrim:Dragon_Rising "Skyrim:Dragon Rising"), the Jarl's bed is usable and all low-level items are free to take.

## Bugs

- If one is facing the door to Dragonsreach and going over to the left side of the drawbridge, then going over to the top of the stairs and standing on the left of it next to the draw bridge, it is possible to slip under Dragonsreach and walk under the map.
  -  The [Unofficial Skyrim Patch](/wiki/Skyrim_Mod:Unofficial_Skyrim_Patch "Skyrim Mod:Unofficial Skyrim Patch"), version 1.2, fixes this bug.
- The cell where the [Alik'r Prisoner](/wiki/Skyrim:Alik%27r_Prisoner "Skyrim:Alik'r Prisoner") gets sent to during "[In My Time Of Need](/wiki/Skyrim:In_My_Time_Of_Need "Skyrim:In My Time Of Need")" cannot be unlocked.
  -  The [Unofficial Skyrim Patch](/wiki/Skyrim_Mod:Unofficial_Skyrim_Patch "Skyrim Mod:Unofficial Skyrim Patch"), version 1.2.4, addresses this issue. The door will now open with the Whiterun Jail Key like all the others.
- Starting from the balcony on the Great Porch, it is possible to use [Whirlwind Sprint](/wiki/Skyrim:Whirlwind_Sprint "Skyrim:Whirlwind Sprint") to fly over the porch edge. Surviving the fall can potentially leave you stuck underneath the map. **?**
- The books on the large table near the Prisoner's Belongings Chest and Evidence Chest in the Dungeon may clip through the table and into each other. **?**
- If you talk to a guard on the Great Porch while he aims his bow, he may stop firing and freeze, though he'll still react if you talk to him. **?**
  - Exit and re-enter the Great Porch, and he'll no longer be frozen.
- If Brill is killed while he is steward to Vignar Gray-Mane (after the [Battle for Whiterun](/wiki/Skyrim:Battle_for_Whiterun_(Stormcloaks) "Skyrim:Battle for Whiterun (Stormcloaks)")), Proventus Avenicci will return from exile to replace him in this position. He will offer the same dialogue as if Jarl Balgruuf still controlled Whiterun.
  -  The [Unofficial Skyrim Patch](/wiki/Skyrim_Mod:Unofficial_Skyrim_Patch "Skyrim Mod:Unofficial Skyrim Patch"), version 1.2.2, addresses this issue. Like other stewards, Brill has been made [essential](/wiki/Skyrim:Essential_NPCs "Skyrim:Essential NPCs").
- If Balgruuf is exiled to the [Blue Palace](/wiki/Skyrim:Blue_Palace "Skyrim:Blue Palace"), his children do not move with him, and they will act the same as if he was still there.
  -  The [Unofficial Skyrim Patch](/wiki/Skyrim_Mod:Unofficial_Skyrim_Patch "Skyrim Mod:Unofficial Skyrim Patch"), version 1.2.2, addresses this issue. His children will move with him to the Blue Palace.

# Skyrim:Dragontooth Crater

## Overview

Dragontooth Crater

**Dragontooth Crater** is a [dragon lair](/wiki/Skyrim:Dragon_Lairs "Skyrim:Dragon Lairs") north-northwest of [Karthwasten](/wiki/Skyrim:Karthwasten "Skyrim:Karthwasten"). Its [word wall](/wiki/Skyrim:Word_Wall "Skyrim:Word Wall") teaches part of the [Elemental Fury](/wiki/Skyrim:Elemental_Fury "Skyrim:Elemental Fury") [dragon shout](/wiki/Skyrim:Dragon_Shouts "Skyrim:Dragon Shouts").

## Related Quests

- **[Bounty: Dragon](/wiki/Skyrim:Bounty:_Dragon "Skyrim:Bounty: Dragon")**: Kill a [dragon](/wiki/Skyrim:Dragon "Skyrim:Dragon") in its [lair](/wiki/Skyrim:Dragon_Lairs "Skyrim:Dragon Lairs"). ([radiant](/wiki/Skyrim:Radiant "Skyrim:Radiant"))
- **[Dragon Seekers](/wiki/Skyrim:Dragon_Seekers "Skyrim:Dragon Seekers")**: Go to a [dragon lair](/wiki/Skyrim:Dragon_Lairs "Skyrim:Dragon Lairs") with [Farkas](/wiki/Skyrim:Farkas "Skyrim:Farkas") or [Vilkas](/wiki/Skyrim:Vilkas "Skyrim:Vilkas") and kill the dragon. ([radiant](/wiki/Skyrim:Radiant "Skyrim:Radiant"))

- This location is one of many potential targets for [one or more of the Radiant quests](/wiki/Skyrim:Radiant#Quest_Locations "Skyrim:Radiant").

## Walkthrough

Dragontooth Crater can be approached from either the north or the west. Starting from Karthwasten, you must navigate east around the mountain and approach from the north. From the [Shrine to Peryite](/wiki/Skyrim:Shrine_to_Peryite "Skyrim:Shrine to Peryite"), you must navigate west around the mountain and approach from the west.

### Before the Dragons Return

Before the [dragons' return](/wiki/Skyrim:Dragon_Rising "Skyrim:Dragon Rising"), the area will be occupied by [Forsworn](/wiki/Skyrim:Forsworn "Skyrim:Forsworn") led by a [hagraven](/wiki/Skyrim:Hagraven "Skyrim:Hagraven"). There are three tents with two hay piles for sleeping, an [arcane enchanter](/wiki/Skyrim:Arcane_Enchanter "Skyrim:Arcane Enchanter") in front of the word wall, a campfire in the middle of the camp, and a gruesome table with the remains of two people spread upon it between the fire and the enchanter. Around the camp are up to four leveled Forsworn standing on lookout, warming themselves by the fire, or sleeping, and a hagraven can be seen using the arcane enchanter in front of the wall. On the enchanter is a random [soul gem](/wiki/Skyrim:Soul_Gems "Skyrim:Soul Gems"), under it is a [Forsworn headdress](/wiki/Skyrim:Forsworn_Headdress "Skyrim:Forsworn Headdress"), behind it is a dead [hunter](/wiki/Skyrim:Hunter "Skyrim:Hunter"), and the boss chest is against the wall.

The tower to the north along the entrance path has three floors. The first floor contains a dead [bandit](/wiki/Skyrim:Bandit "Skyrim:Bandit") on the floor, and on the table under a shrine are two potions, a [human heart](/wiki/Skyrim:Human_Heart "Skyrim:Human Heart"), a random dagger, and some bloody rags. The second floor contains a level-locked chest, and the third floor has a random potion of magicka.

### After the Dragons Return

After the dragons' return, along the path in front of the tower will be found a [burnt corpse](/wiki/Skyrim:Burnt_Corpse "Skyrim:Burnt Corpse") and the corpse of an [Imperial soldier](/wiki/Skyrim:Imperial_Soldier "Skyrim:Imperial Soldier"). A leveled [dragon](/wiki/Skyrim:Dragon "Skyrim:Dragon") lairs in front of the word wall near some bloodstains, instead of resting upon it like most dragons. The wall still has a [Forsworn](/wiki/Skyrim:Forsworn "Skyrim:Forsworn") shrine attached, and the boss chest still sits just inside the semicircle of the wall.

The tower to the north along the entrance path has three floors. The first floor contains a burnt corpse in the doorway and a dead bandit on the floor, and on the table behind some rubble are a random potion of healing, a random dagger, and some bloody rags. The second floor contains a level-locked chest, and the third floor has a random potion of magicka.

## Notes

- An [iron ore vein](/wiki/Skyrim:Iron_Ore_Vein "Skyrim:Iron Ore Vein") is in the rocks by the T-junction at the beginning of the path to the lair.
- A pool to the west contains an undressed captive, with her clothes, a [journal](/wiki/Skyrim:Journal_(pond) "Skyrim:Journal (pond)"), a [satchel](/wiki/Skyrim:Satchel "Skyrim:Satchel"), and jewelry on the shore ([see here for full details](/wiki/Skyrim:Unmarked_Places_The_Reach#The_Incautious_Bather "Skyrim:Unmarked Places The Reach")).

## Bugs

- The dragon in this area sometimes has half of its body stuck in the ground. This may happen when you successfully sneak up and attack the dragon. It will try to face you and clip through the ground. In this state, the dragon will not attack or fly, and it cannot be killed.
  - After depleting its health bar, entering an interior cell (with a loading screen) may trigger the dragon to register as dead.
- If you attack the dragon from the cliff above, it may fly above it, use a swoop attack, and become stuck in this animation and unkillable. The dragon may also be rendered unkillable if you use the [Bend Will](/wiki/Skyrim:Bend_Will "Skyrim:Bend Will")[DB](/wiki/Skyrim:Dragonborn "Skyrim:Dragonborn") shout on it but don't actually ride it. If you then fast travel to the location, the dragon's corpse will be there and you will receive the dragon soul, but the dragon will never respawn, making quests that require it to be slain impossible to complete.
- The location might not be marked as cleared after you kill the dragon and absorb the shout word. Leaving the area and returning by fast travel may correct this.

Drahff

**Drahff** is a [Nord](/wiki/Skyrim:Nord "Skyrim:Nord") [bandit archer](/wiki/Skyrim:Bandit_Archer "Skyrim:Bandit Archer") who can be found scheming alongside [Hewnon Black-Skeever](/wiki/Skyrim:Hewnon_Black-Skeever "Skyrim:Hewnon Black-Skeever") in the entrance to the [Ratway](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Ratway "Skyrim:The Ratway"). Both men will attack you on sight.

Drahff wears a set of [fur armor](/wiki/Skyrim:Fur_Armor "Skyrim:Fur Armor") and a pair of [ragged boots](/wiki/Skyrim:Ragged_Boots "Skyrim:Ragged Boots"). He is equipped with a leveled [bow](/wiki/Skyrim:Bow "Skyrim:Bow") supplemented with 12 leveled [arrows](/wiki/Skyrim:Arrow "Skyrim:Arrow"), both of which can be up to [Daedric](/wiki/Skyrim:Daedric "Skyrim:Daedric") quality. He carries a random leveled [gem](/wiki/Skyrim:Gems "Skyrim:Gems"), and a leveled amount of gold ranging from 25 to 125 gold.

## Related Quests

- **[Taking Care of Business](/wiki/Skyrim:Taking_Care_of_Business "Skyrim:Taking Care of Business")**: Collect some debts for the [Thieves Guild](/wiki/Skyrim:Thieves_Guild_(faction) "Skyrim:Thieves Guild (faction)").

## Dialogue

As soon as you enter the Ratway and move down the first tunnel, you will hear Drahff and Hewnon discuss their little scheme, although Hewnon is starting to doubt if the plan will ever pay off:

:   **Hewnon**: *"I dunno, Drahff. [They'd](/wiki/Skyrim:Thieves_Guild_(faction) "Skyrim:Thieves Guild (faction)") skin us alive if they knew we were doin' this."*
:   **Drahff**: *"Why are you always acting like such a big baby? I've gotten us this far."*
:   **Hewnon**: *"This far? We're livin' in a sewer. You said we'd have a house as big as [the Black-Briars'](/wiki/Skyrim:Black-Briar_Manor "Skyrim:Black-Briar Manor") by now."*
:   **Drahff**: *"You worry about bashing people's heads in, I'll worry about the Guild. Okay?"*
:   **Hewnon**: *"Okay, okay."*
:   **Drahff**: *"I'm going to check the entrance to the Ratway. Be right back."*

## Unused Dialogue

Hewnon and Drahff were not always supposed to attack you on sight, this much can be learned from unused AI packages and dialogue. Unused dialogue for Drahff explains their scheme much better. Drahff would stop you in the very first tunnel and say:

:   *"Hey, you. Stop right there! Empty your pockets or end up as [skeever](/wiki/Skyrim:Skeever "Skyrim:Skeever") food."*

:   **I'm just looking for the [Ragged Flagon](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Ragged_Flagon "Skyrim:The Ragged Flagon").**
:   *"[Brynjolf](/wiki/Skyrim:Brynjolf "Skyrim:Brynjolf")'s been sending idiots like you down here for years looking for their hideout. Funny thing is his stupid Thieves Guild never counted on me and my partner blocking the way. Now, empty your pockets or I'll pick the gold off your corpse."*

At this point, three options would have been available:

:   **I've killed dozens like you. (Persuade)**: *"No need to get hasty. I... I was just testing you. You can go on ahead. Let 'em go, Hewnon. All clear."* **or** *"I doubt that very much."*
:   **How much to let me pass?**: *"You aren't going to pass. You're going to give me everything you have. Whether you leave here in one piece is up to you."*
:   **How about I kill you instead?**: *"Suit yourself. Get 'em Hewnon!"*

If you instead opt out of conversation, he would say:

:   *"Ignoring me, huh? Suit yourself. Get 'em Hewnon!"*

For future encounters, a few friendlier greetings would've gotten used:

:   *"Don't worry, Hewnon will let you pass."*
:   *"We won't give you any more trouble."*
:   *"Sorry to have bothered you. I'll just be out of your way now."*

## Bugs

- Drahff and Hewnon Black-Skeever's corpses may remain in the Ratway indefinitely.
  -  The [Unofficial Skyrim Patch](/wiki/Skyrim_Mod:Unofficial_Skyrim_Patch "Skyrim Mod:Unofficial Skyrim Patch"), version 1.2.4, addresses this issue. They were missing the dead body cleanup script.

Dravin Llanith

**Dravin Llanith** is a [Dark Elf](/wiki/Skyrim:Dark_Elf "Skyrim:Dark Elf") [farmer](/wiki/Skyrim:Classes#Farmer "Skyrim:Classes") who works and lives at [Merryfair Farm](/wiki/Skyrim:Merryfair_Farm "Skyrim:Merryfair Farm"). He is married to [Synda Llanith](/wiki/Skyrim:Synda_Llanith "Skyrim:Synda Llanith").

Dravin wears a set of farm [clothes](/wiki/Skyrim:Clothes#0006c1d9 "Skyrim:Clothes") and a pair of [boots](/wiki/Skyrim:Boots#000209a5 "Skyrim:Boots"). He is equipped with a leveled [dagger](/wiki/Skyrim:Dagger "Skyrim:Dagger") which can be up to [elven](/wiki/Skyrim:Elven "Skyrim:Elven") quality, and carries a selection of [common loot and gold](/wiki/Skyrim:Leveled_Lists#Common "Skyrim:Leveled Lists").

He gets up early at 5am and starts his day with a one-hour breakfast. He then heads outside to farm for most of the day, only to stop for a one-hour dinner in the farmhouse. At 11pm, he finally calls it a day and goes to bed.

## Dialogue

His greetings can be:

:   *"Who in the name of Azura are you?"*
:   *"It's not safe around here. There's thieves out there looking to steal everything you own."*
:   *"You look suspicious. You better not be one of those damn thieves."*
:   *"You even think of taking something from my house... and I'll kill you."*

His goodbyes:

:   *"Watch yourself out there or they'll take everything away from you."*
:   *"[Dragons](/wiki/Skyrim:Dragon "Skyrim:Dragon"), thieves and [war](/wiki/Skyrim:Civil_War "Skyrim:Civil War"). I should have stayed in [Morrowind](/wiki/Lore:Morrowind "Lore:Morrowind")."*

## Related Quests

- **[Bow to the Master](/wiki/Skyrim:Bow_to_the_Master "Skyrim:Bow to the Master")**: Retrieve a farmer's stolen bow.

### Bow to the Master

:   **You've had trouble with thieves?**
:   *"Are you kidding me? We're all alone out here except for a few guards who couldn't give a damn about us. We make easy pickings for thieves looking to steal everything we worked so hard for. Not only did they take my bow, but they took all of our coin as well. Nothing's sacred to these people."*
:   **What happened to your bow?**
:   *"A few days ago, some thieves from [Riften](/wiki/Skyrim:Riften "Skyrim:Riften") broke in here and stole it! Can you imagine? Took the only thing of value we had. If you have the guts to head into the [Ratway](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Ratway "Skyrim:The Ratway") and get my bow back, I'll pay you what I can."*

:   **Sorry, I try and avoid thieves.**

    :   *"Fine. I'll wait until someone else with a little more courage comes along."*

If you have already found the bow before meeting him, you can say:

:   **No need. It's right here.**
:   *"That's it! That's my bow!"*

Otherwise:

:   **I'll see what I can do.**

    :   *"Thanks. It would be nice to have it back... means a lot to me."*

:   **How do you know the thieves were from Riften?**
:   *"I bumped into them when I was coming back to my farm after buying supplies. I know those lowlifes took it with them back to the Ratway. They left an unmistakable stench behind. It was a family heirloom. I can't even put a price on how much that thing means to me."*

As you leave to find the bow he will further tell you:

:   *"The Ratway is somewhere under Riften, shouldn't be too tough to find."*

And upon returning:

:   *"So, has my bow turned up yet?"*
:   **I found your bow.**
:   *"That's it! You found it!"*

Either way, upon returning his bow he will continue with:

:   *"I don't know how you got it back, and I don't want to know. Frankly, I don't even care... I'm just so glad to see it again. Here, this is all can afford to give you as compensation. Hope it's enough."*

After the quest, he'll now greet you with:

:   *"Thanks again for getting my bow back from those thieves. Next time they come knocking I'll be ready."*

## Conversations

Dravin can often be seen talking to his wife about life as an elf in Skyrim:

*"Dravin! What's come over you?"*

**Dravin**: *"Synda... you left your dagger behind again yesterday. I told you, the road isn't safe."*
**Synda**: *"Husband, you worry far too much. We are within an hour's walk of Riften."*
**Dravin**: *"That doesn't matter. All it would take is a stray wolf or a bandit crossing your path... I can't bare*[[sic](/wiki/UESPWiki:Spelling#Books_and_Direct_Quotes "UESPWiki:Spelling")] *to lose you after everything we've done."*
**Synda**: *"If it puts your mind at ease, I'll take it with me. I'm sorry."*

**Synda**: *"Dravin! One of the soldiers I spoke to on the way home said you threatened them. What's come over you?"*
**Dravin**: *"I can't stand them, they represent everything I hate about Skyrim. They're tearing the place apart!"*
**Synda**: *"All you'll accomplish by threatening them is ending up in the Riften dungeon. You're lucky they didn't take you seriously."*
**Dravin**: *"Sorry, Marise*[[sic](/wiki/UESPWiki:Spelling#Books_and_Direct_Quotes "UESPWiki:Spelling")]*. I just can't sit back and watch them treat us like a resource. This is our home!"*
**Synda**: *"I don't care! Just stay away from the soldiers and keep to your business. It's the only way we'll make it through this."*

## Notes

- It is best to do Dravin's quest while you are still comparatively low leveled: since there is a wildlife spawning point very close to the farm, and despite the best efforts of the local guards, either or both of the Llaniths may be killed by wildlife, most usually bears. It doesn't help that they have a tendency to rush into combat rather than run away and leave the fight to the guards. They are also vulnerable to potential dragon attacks that spawn just outside Riften.

# Skyrim:Dravynea's Frost Salts

## Overview

| **Find some [frost salts](/wiki/Skyrim:Frost_Salts "Skyrim:Frost Salts") for [Dravynea the Stoneweaver](/wiki/Skyrim:Dravynea_the_Stoneweaver "Skyrim:Dravynea the Stoneweaver").** | |

|  |  |
| --- | --- |
| Quest Giver: | [Dravynea the Stoneweaver](/wiki/Skyrim:Dravynea_the_Stoneweaver "Skyrim:Dravynea the Stoneweaver") |
| Location(s): | [Kynesgrove](/wiki/Skyrim:Kynesgrove "Skyrim:Kynesgrove") |
| Reward: | +1 [Alteration](/wiki/Skyrim:Alteration "Skyrim:Alteration") skill boost |
| [Disposition](/wiki/Skyrim:Disposition "Skyrim:Disposition"): | =1 ([Dravynea the Stoneweaver](/wiki/Skyrim:Dravynea_the_Stoneweaver "Skyrim:Dravynea the Stoneweaver")) |
| ID: | FreeformKynesgroveA |

Dravynea needs frost salts for a potion to keep the heat in Steamscorch Mine bearable

## Quick Walkthrough

1. Talk to [Dravynea the Stoneweaver](/wiki/Skyrim:Dravynea_the_Stoneweaver "Skyrim:Dravynea the Stoneweaver").
2. Obtain a sample of [frost salts](/wiki/Skyrim:Frost_Salts "Skyrim:Frost Salts").
3. Return for your reward.

### Keeping the Mine Safe

[Dravynea the Stoneweaver](/wiki/Skyrim:Dravynea_the_Stoneweaver "Skyrim:Dravynea the Stoneweaver") is a [Dark Elf](/wiki/Skyrim:Dark_Elf "Skyrim:Dark Elf") [alteration expert](/wiki/Skyrim:TrainerAlterationExpert "Skyrim:TrainerAlterationExpert") living in [Kynesgrove](/wiki/Skyrim:Kynesgrove "Skyrim:Kynesgrove"). When she is not working in the [Steamscorch Mine](/wiki/Skyrim:Steamscorch_Mine "Skyrim:Steamscorch Mine"), you can find her wandering the town or in the [Braidwood Inn](/wiki/Skyrim:Braidwood_Inn "Skyrim:Braidwood Inn"). Should you be in the market for some free [Alteration](/wiki/Skyrim:Alteration "Skyrim:Alteration") training, ask her about her business in Kynesgrove. She will explain that she uses her powers as a mage to keep the mine safe. She is able to make a potion using [frost salts](/wiki/Skyrim:Frost_Salts "Skyrim:Frost Salts") to keep the temperature in the mine bearable, but is out of frost salts at the moment. Tell her that you can get some for her. She will off-handedly offer you free training if you actually bring her the salts.

### Finding Frost Salts

The quest will update to "Bring some Frost Salts to Dravynea". While the term "some" is rather ambiguous, only one bowl of frost salts is required to fulfill the objective. If you do not have a sample in your inventory already, there are many ways to obtain a sample: from the corpse of a [frost atronach](/wiki/Skyrim:Frost_Atronach "Skyrim:Frost Atronach"), purchasing one from an apothecary merchant, creating a sample at the [Atronach Forge](/wiki/Skyrim:Atronach_Forge "Skyrim:Atronach Forge"), or placed randomly on shelves. If you are a member of the [College of Winterhold](/wiki/Skyrim:College_of_Winterhold_(faction) "Skyrim:College of Winterhold (faction)"), you have access to two free samples in the [Hall of Countenance](/wiki/Skyrim:Hall_of_Countenance "Skyrim:Hall of Countenance") alchemy lab.

### The Reward

When you have your sample, take it to Dravynea to complete the quest. She will seem surprised that you actually came through, and will give you a free training session equaling one level of Alteration as a reward.

## Notes

- Because this is a favor quest which affects Dravynea's disposition, it will count towards the "Help the People" part of the [Thane of Eastmarch](/wiki/Skyrim:Thane_of_Eastmarch "Skyrim:Thane of Eastmarch") quest.

## Bugs

- This quest can be assigned multiple times, resulting in a +1 Alteration skill improvement every time the quest is completed.
  -  The [Unofficial Skyrim Patch](/wiki/Skyrim_Mod:Unofficial_Skyrim_Patch "Skyrim Mod:Unofficial Skyrim Patch"), version 2.0.1, fixes this bug.

## Quest Stages

| Dravynea's Frost Salts (FreeformKynesgroveA) | | |
| --- | --- | --- |
| Stage | Finishes Quest | Journal Entry |
| 10 |  | *Objective 10:* Bring some Frost Salts to Dravynea |

- The following empty quest stages were omitted from the table: 20, 200.

Notes

- Any text displayed in angle brackets (e.g., `<Alias=LocationHold>`) is dynamically set by the Radiant Quest system, and will be filled in with the appropriate word(s) when seen in game.
- Not all Journal Entries may appear in your journal; which entries appear and which entries do not depends on the manner in which the quest is done.
- Stages are not always in order of progress. This is usually the case with quests that have multiple possible outcomes or quests where certain tasks may be done in any order. Some stages may therefore repeat objectives seen in other stages.
- If an entry is marked as "Finishes Quest" it means the quest disappears from the Active Quest list, but you may still receive new entries for that quest.
- On the PC, it is possible to use the [console](/wiki/Skyrim:Console "Skyrim:Console") to advance through the quest by entering `setstage FreeformKynesgroveA stage`, where `stage` is the number of the stage you wish to complete. It is not possible to un-complete (i.e. go back) quest stages, but it is possible to clear all stages of the quest using `resetquest FreeformKynesgroveA`.

| [Faction(s)](/wiki/Skyrim:Factions "Skyrim:Factions") | [Alteration Trainer](/wiki/Skyrim:Alteration_Trainer "Skyrim:Alteration Trainer"); [CrimeFactionEastmarch](/wiki/Skyrim:CrimeFactionEastmarch "Skyrim:CrimeFactionEastmarch"); [Dravynea Services](/wiki/Skyrim:Dravynea_Services "Skyrim:Dravynea Services"); [KynesgroveDravyneaFaction](/wiki/Skyrim:KynesgroveDravyneaFaction "Skyrim:KynesgroveDravyneaFaction"); [PotentialMarriageFaction](/wiki/Skyrim:PotentialMarriageFaction "Skyrim:PotentialMarriageFaction"); [Skill Trainer](/wiki/Skyrim:Skill_Trainer "Skyrim:Skill Trainer"); [TownKynesgroveFaction](/wiki/Skyrim:TownKynesgroveFaction "Skyrim:TownKynesgroveFaction") | | |

Dravynea the Stoneweaver

**Dravynea the Stoneweaver** is a [Dark Elf](/wiki/Skyrim:Dark_Elf "Skyrim:Dark Elf") [elemental mage](/wiki/Skyrim:TrainerAlterationExpert "Skyrim:TrainerAlterationExpert") living in [Kynesgrove](/wiki/Skyrim:Kynesgrove "Skyrim:Kynesgrove"). She is responsible for maintaining a low temperature in [Steamscorch Mine](/wiki/Skyrim:Steamscorch_Mine "Skyrim:Steamscorch Mine") so that the workers are able to continue mining.

After raising her disposition, she becomes a potential candidate for [marriage](/wiki/Skyrim:Marriage "Skyrim:Marriage"). She is the expert [trainer](/wiki/Skyrim:Trainers "Skyrim:Trainers") in [Alteration](/wiki/Skyrim:Alteration "Skyrim:Alteration").

Dravynea dedicates much of her day to working inside the mine. She wakes up at 6am and takes a one-hour breakfast inside the [Braidwood Inn](/wiki/Skyrim:Braidwood_Inn "Skyrim:Braidwood Inn"). She will then wander about for the next four hours, dividing her time between relaxing inside the inn or wandering about the campsite area set up outside the mine. At 10am, she heads inside the mine where she will spend her time wandering through the tunnels of the mine, making sure that none of them are ready to collapse. After five hours of being inside the mine, she leaves at 3pm to resume her routine of wandering around the Braidwood Inn and the campsite area outside the mine. At 5pm, she finds a seat inside the inn to take a one-hour dinner. After her meal, she will wander about until 8pm, when she heads back to the mine. She will spend three hours working inside the mine, this time mining the [ore](/wiki/Skyrim:Malachite_Ore "Skyrim:Malachite Ore") inside the mine. At 11pm, she leaves the mine to wander around for three more hours until she heads to her bed inside the inn at 2am.

Dravynea wears [blue mage robes](/wiki/Skyrim:Blue_Mage_Robes "Skyrim:Blue Mage Robes") and a pair of [boots](/wiki/Skyrim:Boots#0006b46c "Skyrim:Boots"). She wields an [iron dagger](/wiki/Skyrim:Iron_Dagger "Skyrim:Iron Dagger") and carries a selection of [common loot and gold](/wiki/Skyrim:Leveled_Lists#Common "Skyrim:Leveled Lists").

Roggi will occasionally mention Dravynea, claiming that she keeps the mine running: *"Working our mine is dangerous work, but Dravynea keeps it going. Well, Dravynea and the promise of more mead."*

## Related Quests

- **[The Bonds of Matrimony](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Bonds_of_Matrimony "Skyrim:The Bonds of Matrimony")**: Find someone in [Skyrim](/wiki/Lore:Skyrim "Lore:Skyrim") to [marry](/wiki/Skyrim:Marriage "Skyrim:Marriage").
- **[Dravynea's Frost Salts](/wiki/Skyrim:Dravynea%27s_Frost_Salts "Skyrim:Dravynea's Frost Salts")**: Find some [frost salts](/wiki/Skyrim:Frost_Salts "Skyrim:Frost Salts") for Dravynea the Stoneweaver.
- **[A Blade in the Dark](/wiki/Skyrim:A_Blade_in_the_Dark "Skyrim:A Blade in the Dark")**: Prove you are Dragonborn to [Delphine](/wiki/Skyrim:Delphine "Skyrim:Delphine") by slaying the dragon [Sahloknir](/wiki/Skyrim:Sahloknir "Skyrim:Sahloknir").

## Dialogue

When you first approach her, Dravynea will tell you that there is nothing of interest to see in Kynesgrove:

:   *"An outsider? No reason to stop in Kynesgrove. Keep moving."*

She will then tell you about the work she does in the mine. She may also provide you with her opinion of her homeland. Occasionally, she discusses the poor treatment Dunmer receive in Skyrim, but will mention that Roggi Knot-Beard treats her fairly. She will also express her interest in seeing how the Dunmer refugees in [Windhelm](/wiki/Skyrim:Windhelm "Skyrim:Windhelm") are faring.

:   *"The mine's always on the verge of collapse. Good thing I'm around to keep it up."*

:   *"[Morrowind](/wiki/Lore:Morrowind "Lore:Morrowind") used to be a lovely place, but you couldn't pay me to live there these days."*

:   *"Most people in Skyrim don't care for Dunmer. Roggi's the only one around here even half-decent."*

:   *"I should get over to Windhelm more. See how the other Morrowind refugees are getting along."*

You can ask her where you can learn more about magic, which will have her point you toward the [College of Winterhold](/wiki/Skyrim:College_of_Winterhold_(place) "Skyrim:College of Winterhold (place)").

:   **Where can I learn more about magic?**
:   *"Not here. Definitely not here. You want to learn, join the College in [Winterhold](/wiki/Skyrim:Winterhold "Skyrim:Winterhold"). They'll deal with it."*

### Conversations

She can often be seen conversing in the mine with Roggi or [Kjeld](/wiki/Skyrim:Kjeld "Skyrim:Kjeld"):

:   **Kjeld**: *"Roggi tell you about the scorcher we found under the scaffolding?"*
:   **Dravynea**: *"Again? But there shouldn't be any earthstreams over there."*
:   **Kjeld**: *"Well I nearly lost my eyebrows to it."*
:   **Dravynea**: *"All right, I'll take a look at it."*

:   **Dravynea**: *"What did I tell you about snooping around my wards?"*
:   **Kjeld**: *"Woman, there's a vein of malachite as thick as my leg back there."*
:   **Dravynea**: *"And if you don't let me secure the steam channel, your leg could get blown off. So go dig at the other corner for a bit."*
:   **Kjeld**: *"Well... just get it done."*

:   **Kjeld**: *"Is the new shaft cleared yet?"*
:   **Dravynea**: *"No, I've been busy trying to keep the whole mine from collapsing, if that's all right with you."*
:   **Kjeld**: *"You're busy. I'll come back later."*

:   **Roggi**: *"Kjeld bothering you again?"*
:   **Dravynea**: *"Nothing I can't handle."*
:   **Roggi**: *"Well, you send that blowhard to me if he steps over the line."*

:   **Roggi**: *"How's the mine today?"*
:   **Dravynea**: *"Not too bad. Careful around the more obvious scorchers."*
:   **Roggi**: *"As usual. I've always got an eye on the rocks."*

### Dravynea's Frost Salts

You can also ask Dravynea about what she does in Kynesgrove, to which she will tell you about how she uses her magical abilities to keep the tunnels inside the mine safe.

:   **What do you do in Kynesgrove?**
:   *"Nosy one, huh? I was a mage back in Morrowind. I lend my talents to the mines here, helping them keep the tunnels safe. By [Azura](/wiki/Lore:Azura "Lore:Azura"), it gets hot in there. I use [Frost Salts](/wiki/Skyrim:Frost_Salts "Skyrim:Frost Salts") for a potion to keep the heat bearable, but I'm out."*

    :   **Sorry to hear that.**
    :   *"It's not any of your bother, so I don't see what you're apologizing for."*

:   :   **I could find those frost salts for you.**
    :   *"If you want to go to the trouble, feel free. I suppose I could offer you a bit of free Alteration training when you get back."*

If you choose to tell her that you can find some frost salts for her, she will accept your help and offer some training as a reward. When you return to her with some frost salts, she will be surprised but happy to see that you completed her errand.

:   **I have your frost salts.**
:   *"Well, well, you actually did what you said you were going to do. I'm impressed. Here, let me teach you a thing or two about Alteration magic. It's the least I can do."*

### A Blade in the Dark

She will hide in Steamscorch Mine and can say:

:   *"I wouldn't go out there for all the money in the world."*
:   *"Do you think it's gone yet?"*
:   *"Don't you know there's a dragon attacking?"*
:   *"We've got to find someplace to hide!"*
:   *"I'm not going out there. Not with that dragon on the loose."*

## Notes

- According to a relationship marker in the [Creation Kit](/wiki/Skyrim_Mod:Creation_Kit "Skyrim Mod:Creation Kit"), Dravynea is [Ambarys Rendar](/wiki/Skyrim:Ambarys_Rendar "Skyrim:Ambarys Rendar")'s confidant.
- Interestingly, despite being a mage, Dravynea is not able to use any spells.
  -  The [Unofficial Skyrim Patch](/wiki/Skyrim_Mod:Unofficial_Skyrim_Patch "Skyrim Mod:Unofficial Skyrim Patch"), version 2.0.7, addresses this issue. She will use spells when in combat.

## Bugs

- Dravynea was supposed to be the backup vendor for [Wuunferth the Unliving](/wiki/Skyrim:Wuunferth_the_Unliving "Skyrim:Wuunferth the Unliving") if he died, but the vendor data was not set up correctly.
  -  The [Unofficial Skyrim Patch](/wiki/Skyrim_Mod:Unofficial_Skyrim_Patch "Skyrim Mod:Unofficial Skyrim Patch"), version 1.2.2, fixes this bug.
- The quest Dravynea's Frost Salts appears to reset every two days, thus permitting free Alteration skill boosts.
  -  The [Unofficial Skyrim Patch](/wiki/Skyrim_Mod:Unofficial_Skyrim_Patch "Skyrim Mod:Unofficial Skyrim Patch"), version 2.0.1, fixes this bug.
- Dravnea doesn't know any spells despite her being a mage.
  -  The [Unofficial Skyrim Patch](/wiki/Skyrim_Mod:Unofficial_Skyrim_Patch "Skyrim Mod:Unofficial Skyrim Patch"), version 2.0.7, fixes this bug.
