# Skyrim:Dreams of the Dead

## Overview

|  |  |
| --- | --- |
| [SR-qico-Miscellaneous.png](/wiki/File:SR-qico-Miscellaneous.png) | **Unlock the secrets of a necromancer's lair and make it your own.** |

|  |  |
| --- | --- |
| Location(s): | [Gallows Hall](/wiki/Skyrim:Gallows_Hall_(place) "Skyrim:Gallows Hall (place)") |
| Reward: | [Staff of Worms](/wiki/Skyrim:Staff_of_Worms "Skyrim:Staff of Worms"), [Bloodworm Helm](/wiki/Skyrim:Bloodworm_Helm "Skyrim:Bloodworm Helm"), [Helm of Oreyn Bearclaw](/wiki/Skyrim:Helm_of_Oreyn_Bearclaw "Skyrim:Helm of Oreyn Bearclaw"), access to [Bone Forge](/wiki/Skyrim:Bone_Forge "Skyrim:Bone Forge") |
| ID: | ccRMSSSE001\_Quest |
| Added by: | [Gallows Hall](/wiki/Skyrim:Gallows_Hall "Skyrim:Gallows Hall") |

A necromancer's lair is yours to claim

## Quick Walkthrough

1. Enter Gallows Hall, the small fortress on the northern shore of Mara's Eye Pond.
2. Read Naara's Journal.
3. Read the [first clue](/wiki/Skyrim:Arch_Necromancer%27s_First_Clue "Skyrim:Arch Necromancer's First Clue").
4. Choose the following torches in this order: Morthal, Falkreath, Nightgate Inn, Fort Dunstad
5. Retrieve the [Staff of Worms](/wiki/Skyrim:Staff_of_Worms "Skyrim:Staff of Worms").
6. Reanimate the Skeleton Mage found to the East of the initial entrance to this room.
7. Retrieve a key by searching the Skeleton Mage.
8. Take the contents of the safe the key opens left of the Enchanting Table.
9. Read the [second clue](/wiki/Skyrim:Arch_Necromancer%27s_Second_Clue "Skyrim:Arch Necromancer's Second Clue").
10. Pray to the small Statue of Vaermina along the west wall.
11. Go to sleep in the bedroll next to the Altar of the Revenant at the center of the room.
12. Starting from left of the Statue of Vaermina, search the coffin in front of you for a Dreamer's Greater Soul Gem. Find another in the hand of the skeleton in the open coffin next to it, then search the closed coffin on the lowest shelf on the other side of the main entrance.
13. Read the [final instructions](/wiki/Skyrim:Arch_Necromancer%27s_Final_Instructions "Skyrim:Arch Necromancer's Final Instructions").
14. Place the four Dreamer's Greater Soul Gems in the Soul Gem Holders.

## Detailed Walkthrough

Naara's body and journal

Begin by approaching Mara's Eye Pond, which is southwest of Windhelm. On one of the shores, built into the side of a mountain, is a wooden door to Gallows Hall which the player can enter.

As you approach the wooden door on the first floor of Gallows Hall, it will be slammed shut, the room will fill with a mist, and objects in the room will start to fly around. You will need to read [Naara's journal](/wiki/Skyrim:Naara%27s_Journal "Skyrim:Naara's Journal"), which can be found next to [her body](/wiki/Skyrim:Naara "Skyrim:Naara"), alongside three [notes](/wiki/Skyrim:Naara%27s_Plea "Skyrim:Naara's Plea"). The journal will mention that the map in the center of the room is a good place to start. Go to the map to find that there is a [clue](/wiki/Skyrim:Arch_Necromancer%27s_First_Clue "Skyrim:Arch Necromancer's First Clue") placed on top of it.

Interact with the torches on the walls of the room based on the clue, which each torch given the name of a place in Skyrim, which will prevent any errors with trying to align cities and towns with the circle of sconces.

The solution is as follows:

1. Morthal
2. Falkreath
3. Nightgate Inn
4. Fort Dunstad

Pray to the shrine

The mist will then dissipate and any flying objects will fall to the ground. Pick up the [Staff of Worms](/wiki/Skyrim:Staff_of_Worms "Skyrim:Staff of Worms") and use it on the skeleton mage corpse lying within an open coffin in the eastern part of the room. Once resurrected, the skeleton mage can be searched to find the [Arch Necromancer's key](/wiki/Skyrim:Arch_Necromancer%27s_Key "Skyrim:Arch Necromancer's Key"). This will unlock the safe next to the arcane enchanter. The safe contains the [Bloodworm Helm](/wiki/Skyrim:Bloodworm_Helm "Skyrim:Bloodworm Helm"), random leveled treasure and the [second clue](/wiki/Skyrim:Arch_Necromancer%27s_Second_Clue "Skyrim:Arch Necromancer's Second Clue").

Look for a small, white statue to Vaermina on the perimeter of the room and interact with it to pray. After praying, go to sleep in the bedroll\* that is in the center of the room (see Notes). Once you wake up, the purple mist will reappear, there will be blurring at the edges of the screen and you will have to search the coffins in the room for three [Dreamer's Greater Soul Gems](/w/index.php?title=Skyrim:Dreamer%27s_Greater_Soul_Gem&action=edit&redlink=1 "Skyrim:Dreamer's Greater Soul Gem (page does not exist)"). Two of them are within closed coffins and one is being held by a skeleton in an open casket. After picking up the third Soul Gem, the player will find themselves back at the altar in the middle of the room, and they should read the Arch Necromancer's [final instructions](/wiki/Skyrim:Arch_Necromancer%27s_Final_Instructions "Skyrim:Arch Necromancer's Final Instructions") that is upon it.

Pick up the soul gem that is near Naara's corpse and head towards the table in the center of the room. Place all four soul gems (the three found in the dream, plus the one just now obtained) into the soul gems on the holders and activate the center of the altar. This will transform all four Greater Soul Gems into Black Soul Gems. With this, the quest will conclude.

## Notes

- Even if using Survival Mode[CC](/wiki/Skyrim:Survival_Mode "Skyrim:Survival Mode"), you can pray at the Shrine of Vaermina for free.
- Naara cannot be resurrected, even with the Staff of Worms.
- Using the staff on the hooded skeleton is considered an assault.
- You can use the Altar of the Revenant again and again after completing the quest, turning 4 filled or empty Greater or Grand Soul Gems into empty Black Soul Gems, and there does not appear to be a limit to this beyond the number of greater or grand soul gems you can get hold of. Given the scarcity of monsters with actual Grand-level souls, compared to the sheer number of available human or elven enemies that require a Black soul gem (Bandits, Necromancers, Conjurers, enemy civil war soldiers, Thalmor Justiciars, Dark Brotherhood victims, any non-essential NPC that you find particularly obnoxious, and so on), this is a good way to get a huge number of Black Soul Gems to fill easily.
- Placing the soul gems in the holders will place Greater soul gems, in preference, before Grand soul gems.
- Sleeping during the second part of the quest *will* activate the [Dark Brotherhood](/wiki/Skyrim:Dark_Brotherhood "Skyrim:Dark Brotherhood") quest, [With Friends Like These...](/wiki/Skyrim:With_Friends_Like_These... "Skyrim:With Friends Like These..."), so if you are trying to avoid doing that quest at this point in time, it is recommended to either do this quest before [activating the Dark Brotherhood questline](/wiki/Skyrim:Dark_Brotherhood#Joining "Skyrim:Dark Brotherhood"), or if you've already activated it, then to wait to start this quest until you are ready to complete the Dark Brotherhood one (you will not be able to leave this quest once it's triggered). This is important because per [the Dark Brotherhood article](/wiki/Skyrim:Dark_Brotherhood#Destroying_the_Dark_Brotherhood "Skyrim:Dark Brotherhood"), the With Friends Like These... quest "will be your only opportunity to attack the Dark Brotherhood" if you ultimately decide you want to destroy them instead of joining them.

## Bugs

- You can take the soul gem from the skeleton's hand before it's time and therefore be unable to finish the quest. On the PC, you could try `setstage ccRMSSSE001_Quest 100`, and if you were short by one soul gem continue with  `player.additem FE03BD09 1`. Otherwise, you can try to load the previous auto save from entry into the cell.
- It may be difficult or impossible to remove the black soul gem from one of the four holders after creating it. This may sometimes be fixed by saving and reloading. **?**

Notes

- Any text displayed in angle brackets (e.g., `<Alias=LocationHold>`) is dynamically set by the Radiant Quest system, and will be filled in with the appropriate word(s) when seen in game.
- Not all Journal Entries may appear in your journal; which entries appear and which entries do not depends on the manner in which the quest is done.
- Stages are not always in order of progress. This is usually the case with quests that have multiple possible outcomes or quests where certain tasks may be done in any order. Some stages may therefore repeat objectives seen in other stages.
- If an entry is marked as "Finishes Quest" it means the quest disappears from the Active Quest list, but you may still receive new entries for that quest.
- On the PC, it is possible to use the [console](/wiki/Skyrim:Console "Skyrim:Console") to advance through the quest by entering `setstage ccRMSSSE001_Quest stage`, where `stage` is the number of the stage you wish to complete. It is not possible to un-complete (i.e. go back) quest stages, but it is possible to clear all stages of the quest using `resetquest ccRMSSSE001_Quest`.

Drelas' Cottage

**Drelas' Cottage** is an isolated [cottage](/wiki/Skyrim:Shacks "Skyrim:Shacks") at the foot of a mountain in northern [Whiterun Hold](/wiki/Skyrim:Whiterun_Hold "Skyrim:Whiterun Hold"), and south of [Morthal](/wiki/Skyrim:Morthal "Skyrim:Morthal").

It is home to [Drelas](/wiki/Skyrim:Drelas "Skyrim:Drelas"), a powerful elemental mage who will attack on sight. It consists of one zone, *[Drelas' Cottage](#Drelas.27_Cottage)*.

| --- |
| [Drelas](/wiki/Skyrim:Drelas "Skyrim:Drelas") |

## Exterior

| Crops | Plants | Mushrooms | Animals | Other |
| --- | --- | --- | --- | --- |
| 4 [Cabbage](/wiki/Skyrim:Cabbage "Skyrim:Cabbage")  4 [Gourd](/wiki/Skyrim:Gourd "Skyrim:Gourd")  6 [Leek](/wiki/Skyrim:Leek "Skyrim:Leek")  6 [Potato](/wiki/Skyrim:Potato "Skyrim:Potato") | 2 [Blue Mountain Flower](/wiki/Skyrim:Blue_Mountain_Flower "Skyrim:Blue Mountain Flower")  1 [Purple Mountain Flower](/wiki/Skyrim:Purple_Mountain_Flower "Skyrim:Purple Mountain Flower")  2 [Tundra Cotton](/wiki/Skyrim:Tundra_Cotton "Skyrim:Tundra Cotton") | 1 [Mora Tapinella](/wiki/Skyrim:Mora_Tapinella "Skyrim:Mora Tapinella") | 3 [Chicken](/wiki/Skyrim:Chicken "Skyrim:Chicken") | 2 [Chickens' Nest](/wiki/Skyrim:Chicken%27s_Egg "Skyrim:Chicken's Egg") |

## Drelas' Cottage

Cooking and dining area

Enchanting and alchemy area

Drelas' cottage is a spacious residence sectioned off into a few areas. The ground floor consists of a fireplace and food area, a small alchemy and enchanting space, and a spacious sitting area, while the bedroom area can be found upstairs. Upon entering the front door, a large table will be to the right, holding a leveled potion, a sample of [elves ear](/wiki/Skyrim:Elves_Ear "Skyrim:Elves Ear"), a [gourd](/wiki/Skyrim:Gourd "Skyrim:Gourd"), a [fly amanita](/wiki/Skyrim:Fly_Amanita "Skyrim:Fly Amanita") mushroom, a [deathbell](/wiki/Skyrim:Deathbell "Skyrim:Deathbell"), two [chicken's eggs](/wiki/Skyrim:Chicken%27s_Egg "Skyrim:Chicken's Egg"), a [dragon's tongue](/wiki/Skyrim:Dragon%27s_Tongue "Skyrim:Dragon's Tongue"), an [orange dartwing](/wiki/Skyrim:Orange_Dartwing "Skyrim:Orange Dartwing"), a [nirnroot](/wiki/Skyrim:Nirnroot "Skyrim:Nirnroot"), two [pine thrush eggs](/wiki/Skyrim:Pine_Thrush_Egg "Skyrim:Pine Thrush Egg"), a [thistle branch](/wiki/Skyrim:Thistle_Branch "Skyrim:Thistle Branch"), a sample of [tundra cotton](/wiki/Skyrim:Tundra_Cotton "Skyrim:Tundra Cotton"), a cluster of [juniper berries](/wiki/Skyrim:Juniper_Berries "Skyrim:Juniper Berries"), a sample of [wheat](/wiki/Skyrim:Wheat "Skyrim:Wheat"), and a serving of [grilled leeks](/wiki/Skyrim:Grilled_Leeks "Skyrim:Grilled Leeks"). A large floor fireplace sits in the northeast corner, and the room holds two respawning large sacks—one along the wall between the door and the table, and the other in the northwest corner.

Proceeding through the doorway to the next area of the cottage, a small alchemy and enchanting space can be found on the north side. This is where [Drelas](/wiki/Skyrim:Drelas "Skyrim:Drelas") is likely to be found during the day. On the right side of this space is a small set of shelves holding a copy of *[Galerion The Mystic](/wiki/Skyrim:Galerion_The_Mystic "Skyrim:Galerion The Mystic")* and a thistle branch on the top shelf, and two [blue dartwings](/wiki/Skyrim:Blue_Dartwing "Skyrim:Blue Dartwing") on the bottom shelf. An [alchemy lab](/wiki/Skyrim:Alchemy_Lab "Skyrim:Alchemy Lab") is situated in the corner, with two wall shelves above—the right holding a non-respawning large sack, and the left holding a sample of [vampire dust](/wiki/Skyrim:Vampire_Dust "Skyrim:Vampire Dust"). Two [spider eggs](/wiki/Skyrim:Spider_Egg "Skyrim:Spider Egg") and a respawning large sack sit in a small crate to the left of the alchemy lab. At the top of the next set of shelves along the north wall is a sample of [hagraven feathers](/wiki/Skyrim:Hagraven_Feathers "Skyrim:Hagraven Feathers"), while a leveled magicka poison and a sample of [bone meal](/wiki/Skyrim:Bone_Meal "Skyrim:Bone Meal") can be found on the top shelf, and the bottom shelf holds a sample of [glow dust](/wiki/Skyrim:Glow_Dust "Skyrim:Glow Dust"), two deathbells, and a sample of [ice wraith teeth](/wiki/Skyrim:Ice_Wraith_Teeth "Skyrim:Ice Wraith Teeth"). The [arcane enchanter](/wiki/Skyrim:Arcane_Enchanter "Skyrim:Arcane Enchanter") sits in the left corner, to the left of which rests a large silver bowl containing three [scaly pholiota](/wiki/Skyrim:Scaly_Pholiota "Skyrim:Scaly Pholiota") mushrooms and two [sabre cat teeth](/wiki/Skyrim:Sabre_Cat_Tooth "Skyrim:Sabre Cat Tooth").

The remaining portion of the ground floor is a spacious sitting area, with the stairway leading to the bedroom upstairs. Along the railing separating the rooms on the east side, a small table is set with an [apple pie](/wiki/Skyrim:Apple_Pie "Skyrim:Apple Pie"), a bottle of [wine](/wiki/Skyrim:Wine "Skyrim:Wine"), and a bowl containing two [potatoes](/wiki/Skyrim:Potato "Skyrim:Potato"). In the southwest corner, a desk holds another bottle of wine and a copy of *[The Firmament](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Firmament "Skyrim:The Firmament")*, while a bookshelf holds a sample of vampire dust, a thistle branch, and one copy each of the following books: *[Life of Uriel Septim VII](/wiki/Skyrim:Life_of_Uriel_Septim_VII "Skyrim:Life of Uriel Septim VII")*; *[Brief History of the Empire, v4](/wiki/Skyrim:Brief_History_of_the_Empire,_v4 "Skyrim:Brief History of the Empire, v4")*; *[The Real Barenziah, v3](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Real_Barenziah,_v3 "Skyrim:The Real Barenziah, v3")*; *[Ruins of Kemel-Ze](/wiki/Skyrim:Ruins_of_Kemel-Ze "Skyrim:Ruins of Kemel-Ze")*; *[Yngol and the Sea-Ghosts](/wiki/Skyrim:Yngol_and_the_Sea-Ghosts "Skyrim:Yngol and the Sea-Ghosts")*; and *[Biography of Barenziah, v3](/wiki/Skyrim:Biography_of_Barenziah,_v3 "Skyrim:Biography of Barenziah, v3")*. Beneath the stairway are three respawning food barrels, one of which holds a respawning large sack, while another holds a [draught of strength](/wiki/Skyrim:Draught_of_Strength "Skyrim:Draught of Strength"), a leveled potion, and a sample of tundra cotton. Another respawning sack sits in front of the southernmost barrel.

Upstairs bedroom area

Heading upstairs, you'll find a small non-respawning cupboard directly ahead, atop which sits a glazed bowl containing two [goat cheese wedges](/wiki/Skyrim:Goat_Cheese_Wedge "Skyrim:Goat Cheese Wedge"). Against the wall to the right is a non-respawning dresser holding a bottle of [ale](/wiki/Skyrim:Ale "Skyrim:Ale") and another copy of *Biography of Barenziah, v3*. Turning the corner, there are two tall bookcases along the wall to the left, and a single bed in the main bedroom space on the right. At the foot of the bed is a respawning chest containing leveled items, and to the right of the bed is an end table holding a [potion of plentiful magicka](/wiki/Skyrim:Potion_of_Plentiful_Magicka "Skyrim:Potion of Plentiful Magicka") and a bottle of [alto wine](/wiki/Skyrim:Alto_Wine "Skyrim:Alto Wine"). On the bookshelves are two samples of [lavender](/wiki/Skyrim:Lavender "Skyrim:Lavender") in a basket, a sample of tundra cotton, and a basic [poison](/wiki/Skyrim:Potions#Poison "Skyrim:Potions"), as well as twelve more books: *The Real Barenziah, v3*; *[Antecedants of Dwemer Law](/wiki/Skyrim:Antecedants_of_Dwemer_Law "Skyrim:Antecedants of Dwemer Law")*; two copies of *[The Firsthold Revolt](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Firsthold_Revolt "Skyrim:The Firsthold Revolt")*; two copies of *[The Cake and The Diamond](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Cake_and_The_Diamond "Skyrim:The Cake and The Diamond")*; two copies of *[The Hope of the Redoran](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Hope_of_the_Redoran "Skyrim:The Hope of the Redoran")*; *[The Book of Daedra](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Book_of_Daedra "Skyrim:The Book of Daedra")*; *[Frontier, Conquest](/wiki/Skyrim:Frontier,_Conquest "Skyrim:Frontier, Conquest")*; *[Mysterious Akavir](/wiki/Skyrim:Mysterious_Akavir "Skyrim:Mysterious Akavir")*; and *[The Real Barenziah, v1](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Real_Barenziah,_v1 "Skyrim:The Real Barenziah, v1")*.

## Notes

- The door is not locked, but entering the cottage still counts as trespassing. Additionally, items in the house, other than those looted from Drelas' corpse, will remain owned by Drelas upon his death and will be marked as stolen if taken.
- The cottage is a hot spot for [dragon](/wiki/Skyrim:Dragon "Skyrim:Dragon") encounters due to the nearby [word wall](/wiki/Skyrim:Word_Wall "Skyrim:Word Wall") at [Eldersblood Peak](/wiki/Skyrim:Eldersblood_Peak "Skyrim:Eldersblood Peak").
- Two [deer](/wiki/Skyrim:Deer "Skyrim:Deer") or [elk](/wiki/Skyrim:Elk "Skyrim:Elk") are likely to be found nearby.
- All cupboards, dressers, and end tables in the location are non-respawning.
- A [stone quarry](/wiki/Skyrim:Quarried_Stone "Skyrim:Quarried Stone")[HF](/wiki/Skyrim:Hearthfire "Skyrim:Hearthfire") can be found just north of the cottage.

## Bugs

- The door to Drelas' cottage is owned by [Ulfberth War-Bear](/wiki/Skyrim:WhiterunUlfberthsHouseFaction "Skyrim:WhiterunUlfberthsHouseFaction").
  -  The [Unofficial Skyrim Patch](/wiki/Skyrim_Mod:Unofficial_Skyrim_Patch "Skyrim Mod:Unofficial Skyrim Patch"), version 2.0.5, fixes this bug.
- The grilled leeks, magicka potion, elves ear, thistle branch, bushel of wheat, juniper berry, and pine thrush eggs may clip or be misplaced, making them irretrievable. One of the mushrooms may be seen floating in the air as well.
  -  The [Unofficial Skyrim Patch](/wiki/Skyrim_Mod:Unofficial_Skyrim_Patch "Skyrim Mod:Unofficial Skyrim Patch"), version 2.1.2, fixes this bug.

Drelas in his house

**Drelas** is a [Dark Elf](/wiki/Skyrim:Dark_Elf "Skyrim:Dark Elf") [elemental mage](/wiki/Skyrim:CombatMageElemental "Skyrim:CombatMageElemental") who lives alone in his [cottage](/wiki/Skyrim:Drelas%27_Cottage "Skyrim:Drelas' Cottage") south of [Morthal](/wiki/Skyrim:Morthal "Skyrim:Morthal"). He is not overly prone to conversation; if you decide to enter his cottage, he will attack with powerful magic and a random leveled [dagger](/wiki/Skyrim:Dagger "Skyrim:Dagger") (up to [glass](/wiki/Skyrim:Malachite "Skyrim:Malachite") quality). He wears a random magical robe and a pair of [boots](/wiki/Skyrim:Boots#000c5d12 "Skyrim:Boots"), and keeps an assortment of random magical items with him such as [spell tomes](/wiki/Skyrim:Spell_Tomes "Skyrim:Spell Tomes") and [alchemical](/wiki/Skyrim:Alchemy "Skyrim:Alchemy") [ingredients](/wiki/Skyrim:Ingredients "Skyrim:Ingredients").

His house contains an [alchemy lab](/wiki/Skyrim:Alchemy_Lab "Skyrim:Alchemy Lab") and [arcane enchanter](/wiki/Skyrim:Arcane_Enchanter "Skyrim:Arcane Enchanter"), as well as a number of alchemical ingredients scattered about.

## Notes

- Due to his high aggression, if the fighting spills outside he will kill his own chickens.
- Although the door to his house is unlocked, entering still counts as trespassing, and taking anything other than the items looted from his corpse counts as theft.

The Dremora Butler

The **Dremora Butler** is a [Dremora](/wiki/Skyrim:Dremora "Skyrim:Dremora") you can summon to carry your excess items with the power [Secret Servant](/wiki/Skyrim:Secret_Servant "Skyrim:Secret Servant") if you choose it as a reward during the quest [Black Book: Untold Legends](/wiki/Skyrim:Black_Book:_Untold_Legends_(quest) "Skyrim:Black Book: Untold Legends (quest)").

He wears [fine clothes](/wiki/Skyrim:Fine_Clothes#DB0376DD "Skyrim:Fine Clothes") with a pair of [fine boots](/wiki/Skyrim:Fine_Boots#DB0376DE "Skyrim:Fine Boots").

## Related Quests

- **[Black Book: Untold Legends](/wiki/Skyrim:Black_Book:_Untold_Legends_(quest) "Skyrim:Black Book: Untold Legends (quest)")**: Learn the [Black Book](/wiki/Skyrim:Black_Book:_Untold_Legends_(book) "Skyrim:Black Book: Untold Legends (book)")'s hidden knowledge.

## Dialogue

Upon summoning him, his world-weary outlook will show as he will greet you with sarcasm.

:   *"At your service."*
:   *"Oh look. My new master."*
:   *"A new master. It's been centuries."*
:   *"More cups and plates for me to carry?"*
:   *"I don't suppose you'll carry some of this for a while."*

Once you tell him to carry your items, he will reply with the same attitude.

:   *"Certainly, sir/ma'am."*
:   *"I live to serve."*
:   *"I always dreamt of being a pack mule."*
:   *"I was hoping you'd say that."*

When you end your conversation with him, he will say one of the following before disappearing:

:   *"A butler's work is never done."*
:   *"I'll be going now."*
:   *"It's been so much fun."*

## Notes

- His carry weight is capped at 148. He won't carry more than that.
- The Dremora Butler is different from many other Dremora in that his voice is not the usual low pitch menacing sound, but uses the "haughty" voicetype used by most male [Altmer](/wiki/Skyrim:High_Elf "Skyrim:High Elf") and befitting his status as a butler.
- If you give him a weapon to carry, he may have the weapon equipped the next time you summon him.
- The Dremora Butler cannot be banished by any banish or expel Daedra spells.

Dremora Lyrkynaz

**Dremora Lyrkynaz** is a [Dremora](/wiki/Skyrim:Dremora "Skyrim:Dremora") mage whom you must summon during the quest [The Arms of Chaos](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Arms_of_Chaos "Skyrim:The Arms of Chaos") as part of the [Arms of Chaos](/wiki/Skyrim:Arms_of_Chaos "Skyrim:Arms of Chaos") [Creation](/wiki/Skyrim:Creation_Club "Skyrim:Creation Club"). Once you have obtained the [Sovereign Band](/wiki/Skyrim:Sovereign_Band "Skyrim:Sovereign Band"), you will be directed to use it at a Daedric altar east of [Skytemple Ruins](/wiki/Skyrim:Skytemple_Ruins "Skyrim:Skytemple Ruins") in order to summon three Guardians of the Sigil Stones. Activating the altar will summon three Daedra in short succession: [Dremora Sehtkynaz](/wiki/Skyrim:Dremora_Sehtkynaz "Skyrim:Dremora Sehtkynaz"), Dremora Lyrkynaz, and [Dremora Sovereign](/wiki/Skyrim:Dremora_Sovereign "Skyrim:Dremora Sovereign"). Dremora Lyrkynaz is the second Dremora to appear, and will be summoned as soon as you kill Dremora Sehtkynaz.

Dremora Lyrkynaz utilizes powerful [shock](/wiki/Skyrim:Shock_Damage "Skyrim:Shock Damage") magic in combat and can summon a [storm atronach](/wiki/Skyrim:Storm_Atronach "Skyrim:Storm Atronach"). He carries a dagger and warhammer along with a [Green Sigil Stone](/wiki/Skyrim:Green_Sigil_Stone "Skyrim:Green Sigil Stone"). He will drop a [Daedra Heart](/wiki/Skyrim:Daedra_Heart "Skyrim:Daedra Heart") when killed.

## Related Quests

- **[The Arms of Chaos](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Arms_of_Chaos "Skyrim:The Arms of Chaos")**[CC](/wiki/Skyrim:Arms_of_Chaos "Skyrim:Arms of Chaos"): Complete a mage's quest to reassemble two powerful staves.

The Dremora Merchant

The **Dremora Merchant** is a [Dremora](/wiki/Skyrim:Dremora "Skyrim:Dremora") that can be summoned by the [Black Market](/wiki/Skyrim:Black_Market "Skyrim:Black Market") power, one of the reward options from the quest [Black Book: Untold Legends](/wiki/Skyrim:Black_Book:_Untold_Legends_(quest) "Skyrim:Black Book: Untold Legends (quest)"). When summoned, he approaches you and goes into the sell screen. He wears [black robes](/wiki/Skyrim:Black_Robes_(xx0376da) "Skyrim:Black Robes (xx0376da)") and a pair of [Boots](/wiki/Skyrim:Boots_(xx0376d9) "Skyrim:Boots (xx0376d9)").

The Dremora merchant has a more pleasant personality than many of his kind—he speaks with a refined voice more akin to that of a [Dunmer](/wiki/Skyrim:Dark_Elf "Skyrim:Dark Elf") than the low-pitched growl common to his race, and seems to delight in providing his services to you, unlike the [Dremora Butler](/wiki/Skyrim:Dremora_Butler "Skyrim:Dremora Butler").

## Related Quests

- **[Black Book: Untold Legends](/wiki/Skyrim:Black_Book:_Untold_Legends_(quest) "Skyrim:Black Book: Untold Legends (quest)")**: Learn the [Black Book](/wiki/Skyrim:Black_Book:_Untold_Legends_(book) "Skyrim:Black Book: Untold Legends (book)")'s hidden knowledge.

## Dialogue

He will greet you by saying one of the following:

:   *"Ah, my favorite customer."*

:   *"You have many things I wish to buy."*

:   *"So soon? You must be hungry for a deal."*

:   *"Ah, a fresh mortal who seeks to bargain with me."*

:   *"So, we meet again."*

When you offer to sell your items to him, he will reply with one of the following:

:   *"I'm sure we can strike a bargain."*

:   *"Haggling with you can be so...entertaining."*

:   *"Let's make a deal."*

:   *"I can hardly wait."*

Once you have finished bartering with him, he will part ways by making one of the following remarks:

:   **Dremora Merchant:** *"Until you summon me again."*
:   **Dremora Merchant:** *"I do so love dealing with mortals."*
:   **Dremora Merchant:** *"Ah, sweet [Oblivion](/wiki/Lore:Oblivion "Lore:Oblivion"). Soon I shall return."*

## Standard Merchandise

This is the merchandise found in the Dremora Merchant's [merchant chest](/wiki/Skyrim:Merchant_Chest "Skyrim:Merchant Chest"). These items are only available if purchased from the merchant; they cannot be pickpocketed or stolen. They are [restocked](/wiki/Skyrim:Respawning "Skyrim:Respawning") every two days.

| Count | Item | Details |
| --- | --- | --- |
| 1 | Leveled [Heavy Armor](/wiki/Skyrim:Heavy_Armor "Skyrim:Heavy Armor") (unenchanted; Daedric is best possible) |  |
| 1 | Leveled [Enchanted Heavy Armor](/wiki/Skyrim:Generic_Magic_Apparel "Skyrim:Generic Magic Apparel") (Daedric is best possible) |  |
| 1 | Leveled [Enchanted Weapon](/wiki/Skyrim:Generic_Magic_Weapons "Skyrim:Generic Magic Weapons") (Daedric is best possible) |  |
| 1 | Leveled [Weapon](/wiki/Skyrim:Weapons "Skyrim:Weapons") (unenchanted; Daedric is best possible) |  |
| ~9 | Leveled [Arrows](/wiki/Skyrim:Arrows "Skyrim:Arrows") (Daedric is best possible) | Max 12 (12@75%) |

## Notes

- His inventory is leveled, and includes weapons, armor and arrows. At higher levels, he is a reliable source of [Daedric items](/wiki/Skyrim:Daedric "Skyrim:Daedric").
  - The Dremora Merchant is also a possible source for [Dragonplate armor](/wiki/Skyrim:Dragon_Items#Dragonplate_Armor "Skyrim:Dragon Items").
  - The Dremora Merchant sometimes can sell Daedric and Dragon items even before they start appearing in the world, making him one of only a few locations to do that. Another such example is [Glover Mallory's Thief Cache](/wiki/Skyrim:Glover_Mallory "Skyrim:Glover Mallory"). [*verification needed — At which level do they become available?*]
- While he doesn't have a large selection, his gold count is always 2000, making him a good choice if you need to sell some gear immediately.
- When selling items to the Dremora Merchant, you'll receive 9% less gold than from other merchants. If you don't have rank 2 or higher of the [Haggling perk](/wiki/Skyrim:Haggling "Skyrim:Haggling"), the Dremora Merchant will also charge 25% more for purchased items.
  - He won't accept stolen items unless you have the [Fence](/wiki/Skyrim:Fence "Skyrim:Fence") perk.
  - He is not affected by any other [Speech](/wiki/Skyrim:Speech "Skyrim:Speech") perks.
- The quest [Buy Dwarven artifact](/wiki/Skyrim:Buy_Dwarven_artifact "Skyrim:Buy Dwarven artifact") can be triggered when buying Dwarven equipment from him.

## Bugs

- If you try to summon the Dremora Merchant while trespassing, he will say, *"You're not supposed to be here."* and will refuse to do business with you.
  -  The [Unofficial Dragonborn Patch](/wiki/Skyrim_Mod:Unofficial_Dragonborn_Patch "Skyrim Mod:Unofficial Dragonborn Patch"), version 2.0.7, fixes this bug.
- The enchanted weapon offered by the Dremora Merchant may sometimes not be Daedric quality, even at level 52 or above despite the leveled lists specifying the appropriate items at this level. **?**

Dremora Sehtkynaz

**Dremora Sehtkynaz** is a [Dremora](/wiki/Skyrim:Dremora "Skyrim:Dremora") mage whom you must summon during the quest [The Arms of Chaos](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Arms_of_Chaos "Skyrim:The Arms of Chaos") as part of the [Arms of Chaos](/wiki/Skyrim:Arms_of_Chaos "Skyrim:Arms of Chaos") [Creation](/wiki/Skyrim:Creation_Club "Skyrim:Creation Club"). Once you have obtained the [Sovereign Band](/wiki/Skyrim:Sovereign_Band "Skyrim:Sovereign Band"), you will be directed to use it at a Daedric altar east of [Skytemple Ruins](/wiki/Skyrim:Skytemple_Ruins "Skyrim:Skytemple Ruins") in order to summon three Guardians of the Sigil Stones. Activating the altar will summon three Daedra in short succession: Dremora Sehtkynaz, [Dremora Lyrkynaz](/wiki/Skyrim:Dremora_Lyrkynaz "Skyrim:Dremora Lyrkynaz"), and [Dremora Sovereign](/wiki/Skyrim:Dremora_Sovereign "Skyrim:Dremora Sovereign"). Dremora Sehtkynaz is the first Dremora to appear.

Dremora Sehtkynaz utilizes powerful [frost](/wiki/Skyrim:Frost_Damage "Skyrim:Frost Damage") magic in combat and can summon a [frost atronach](/wiki/Skyrim:Frost_Atronach "Skyrim:Frost Atronach"). He carries a dagger and mace along with a [Blue Sigil Stone](/wiki/Skyrim:Blue_Sigil_Stone "Skyrim:Blue Sigil Stone"). He will drop a [Daedra Heart](/wiki/Skyrim:Daedra_Heart "Skyrim:Daedra Heart") when killed.

## Related Quests

- **[The Arms of Chaos](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Arms_of_Chaos "Skyrim:The Arms of Chaos")**[CC](/wiki/Skyrim:Arms_of_Chaos "Skyrim:Arms of Chaos"): Complete a mage's quest to reassemble two powerful staves.

Dremora Sovereign

**Dremora Sovereign** is a [Dremora](/wiki/Skyrim:Dremora "Skyrim:Dremora") warrior whom you must summon during the quest [The Arms of Chaos](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Arms_of_Chaos "Skyrim:The Arms of Chaos") as part of the [Arms of Chaos](/wiki/Skyrim:Arms_of_Chaos "Skyrim:Arms of Chaos") [Creation](/wiki/Skyrim:Creation_Club "Skyrim:Creation Club"). Once you have obtained the [Sovereign Band](/wiki/Skyrim:Sovereign_Band "Skyrim:Sovereign Band"), you will be directed to use it at a Daedric altar east of [Skytemple Ruins](/wiki/Skyrim:Skytemple_Ruins "Skyrim:Skytemple Ruins") in order to summon three Guardians of the Sigil Stones. Activating the altar will summon three Daedra in short succession: [Dremora Sehtkynaz](/wiki/Skyrim:Dremora_Sehtkynaz "Skyrim:Dremora Sehtkynaz"), [Dremora Lyrkynaz](/wiki/Skyrim:Dremora_Lyrkynaz "Skyrim:Dremora Lyrkynaz"), and Dremora Sovereign. Dremora Sovereign is the third Dremora to appear, and will be summoned as soon as you kill Dremora Lyrkynaz.

Dremora Sovereign utilizes powerful [fire](/wiki/Skyrim:Fire_Damage "Skyrim:Fire Damage") magic in combat and can summon a [flame atronach](/wiki/Skyrim:Flame_Atronach "Skyrim:Flame Atronach"). He carries a [Daedric Sword of the Inferno](/wiki/Skyrim:Daedric_Sword_of_the_Inferno "Skyrim:Daedric Sword of the Inferno") along with an [Orange Sigil Stone](/wiki/Skyrim:Orange_Sigil_Stone "Skyrim:Orange Sigil Stone"). He will drop a [Daedra Heart](/wiki/Skyrim:Daedra_Heart "Skyrim:Daedra Heart") when killed.

## Related Quests

- **[The Arms of Chaos](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Arms_of_Chaos "Skyrim:The Arms of Chaos")**[CC](/wiki/Skyrim:Arms_of_Chaos "Skyrim:Arms of Chaos"): Complete a mage's quest to reassemble two powerful staves.

## Notes

- His Daedric Sword of the Inferno will be present regardless of your level, potentially giving you access to a powerful weapon early on.

# Skyrim:Dremora

## Overview

Dremora at the Shrine of Mehrunes Dagon

**Dremora** are humanoid [Daedra](/wiki/Skyrim:Daedra "Skyrim:Daedra"). They are often very intelligent and are generally hostile. In [lore](/wiki/Lore:Dremora "Lore:Dremora"), it is said they can be found in clans of large numbers in the wastes of [Oblivion](/wiki/Lore:Oblivion "Lore:Oblivion"). Dremora are grouped into several different castes: Churl, Caitiff, Kynval, Kynreeve, Kynmarcher, Markynaz, and Valkynaz. Dremora are a rare sight in Skyrim, only appearing as summoned creatures and in a few set locations, such as the [Shrine of Mehrunes Dagon](/wiki/Skyrim:Shrine_of_Mehrunes_Dagon "Skyrim:Shrine of Mehrunes Dagon"), [Shalidor's Maze](/wiki/Skyrim:Shalidor%27s_Maze "Skyrim:Shalidor's Maze"), [Azura's Star Interior](/wiki/Skyrim:Azura%27s_Star_Interior "Skyrim:Azura's Star Interior"), and the [Deadlands](/wiki/Skyrim:Deadlands "Skyrim:Deadlands")[CC](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Cause "Skyrim:The Cause").

The other way to encounter Dremora in Skyrim is by summoning one. There are a few ways to summon Dremora:

- The [Sanguine Rose](/wiki/Skyrim:Sanguine_Rose "Skyrim:Sanguine Rose"), a reward from the quest [A Night To Remember](/wiki/Skyrim:A_Night_To_Remember "Skyrim:A Night To Remember"), will summon a leveled melee fighter Dremora for 60 seconds, or 120 seconds with the appropriate Conjuration perks.
- The [Conjuration](/wiki/Skyrim:Conjuration "Skyrim:Conjuration") spell [Conjure Dremora Lord](/wiki/Skyrim:Conjure_Dremora_Lord "Skyrim:Conjure Dremora Lord") will summon a [Dremora Lord](#Dremora_Lord) for 60 seconds, or 120 seconds with the appropriate Conjuration perks.
- The [Atronach Forge](/wiki/Skyrim:Atronach_Forge "Skyrim:Atronach Forge") can be used to summon hostile Dremora, which will obviously attack anybody or anything on sight.
- The [Conjuration Ritual Spell](/wiki/Skyrim:Conjuration_Ritual_Spell "Skyrim:Conjuration Ritual Spell") quest involves summoning an [Unbound Dremora](/wiki/Skyrim:Unbound_Dremora "Skyrim:Unbound Dremora"); this Dremora cannot be summoned anywhere other than the roof of the [Hall of Attainment](/wiki/Skyrim:Hall_of_Attainment "Skyrim:Hall of Attainment"). Once again, this will be automatically hostile to everything it encounters.
- The [Wabbajack](/wiki/Skyrim:Wabbajack "Skyrim:Wabbajack") has a chance to momentarily turn the target into a hostile Dremora.

## Dremora Types

There are three types of Dremora, based on their preferred fighting style: melee fighters, archers, and warlocks. All Dremora are [NPCs](/wiki/Skyrim:NPCs "Skyrim:NPCs") with [black souls](/wiki/Skyrim:Souls "Skyrim:Souls"). All types of Dremora always drop a [Daedra Heart](/wiki/Skyrim:Daedra_Heart "Skyrim:Daedra Heart") on death; they're one of the few guaranteed sources of this rare ingredient.

### Melee Fighters

These Dremora belong to the [Dremora](/wiki/Skyrim:Dremora_(class) "Skyrim:Dremora (class)") NPC [class](/wiki/Skyrim:Classes "Skyrim:Classes") and use one or two-handed weapons in battle. They wear a [unique version](/wiki/Skyrim:Specialty_Gear#Dremora_Equipment "Skyrim:Specialty Gear") of [Daedric Armor](/wiki/Skyrim:Daedric_Armor "Skyrim:Daedric Armor") available only to Dremora and wield a leveled [mace](/wiki/Skyrim:Mace "Skyrim:Mace"), [sword](/wiki/Skyrim:Sword "Skyrim:Sword"), [war axe](/wiki/Skyrim:War_Axe "Skyrim:War Axe"), [warhammer](/wiki/Skyrim:Greatsword "Skyrim:Greatsword"), [greatsword](/wiki/Skyrim:Greatsword "Skyrim:Greatsword"), or [battleaxe](/wiki/Skyrim:Battleaxe "Skyrim:Battleaxe"), all of which are enchanted with [fire damage](/wiki/Skyrim:Fire_Damage "Skyrim:Fire Damage"). The type of enchantment depends on the quality of the material, as follows:

- **[Iron](/wiki/Skyrim:Iron "Skyrim:Iron") or [steel](/wiki/Skyrim:Steel "Skyrim:Steel"):** [of Embers](/wiki/Skyrim:Generic_Magic_Weapons#of_Embers "Skyrim:Generic Magic Weapons"), [of Burning](/wiki/Skyrim:Generic_Magic_Weapons#of_Burning "Skyrim:Generic Magic Weapons"), [of Scorching](/wiki/Skyrim:Generic_Magic_Weapons#of_Scorching "Skyrim:Generic Magic Weapons")
- **[Glass](/wiki/Skyrim:Malachite "Skyrim:Malachite"):** of Scorching, [of Fire](/wiki/Skyrim:Generic_Magic_Weapons#of_Fire "Skyrim:Generic Magic Weapons"), [of the Blaze](/wiki/Skyrim:Generic_Magic_Weapons#of_the_Blaze "Skyrim:Generic Magic Weapons")
- **[Ebony](/wiki/Skyrim:Ebony "Skyrim:Ebony") or [Daedric](/wiki/Skyrim:Daedric "Skyrim:Daedric"):** of Fire, of the Blaze, [of the Inferno](/wiki/Skyrim:Generic_Magic_Weapons#of_the_Inferno "Skyrim:Generic Magic Weapons")

They also carry an [iron dagger](/wiki/Skyrim:Iron_Dagger "Skyrim:Iron Dagger") and will drop a Daedra Heart on death.

A Dremora warrior wielding a steel war axe

| Dremora Markynaz | 36 | 36 | 00016ff4 | 435 | 50 | 190 |
| Dremora Valynaz *[[sic](/wiki/UESPWiki:Spelling#Books_and_Direct_Quotes "UESPWiki:Spelling")]* | 46 | 46 | 00016ff8 [[1]](#intnote_DremoraLord) | 545 | 50 | 230 |

[^1](#note_DremoraLord)This Dremora is also the template used for the [Dremora Lord](#Dremora_Lord) summoned with Conjure Dremora Lord.

### Archers

These Dremora have the [Bandit](/wiki/Skyrim:Bandit_(class) "Skyrim:Bandit (class)") NPC class and wield fire-enchanted bows to fight from a distance. They wear the same unique Daedric Armor as their melee counterparts and use one of the following enchanted bows:

- **[Hunting Bow](/wiki/Skyrim:Hunting_Bow "Skyrim:Hunting Bow"):** of Embers, of Burning, of Scorching
- **[Glass Bow](/wiki/Skyrim:Glass_Bow "Skyrim:Glass Bow"):** of Scorching, of Fire, of the Blaze
- **[Ebony](/wiki/Skyrim:Ebony_Bow "Skyrim:Ebony Bow") or [Daedric Bow](/wiki/Skyrim:Daedric "Skyrim:Daedric"):** of Fire, of the Blaze, of the Inferno

They also carry an iron dagger, one iron arrow, and a quiver of up to 20 [iron](/wiki/Skyrim:Iron_Arrow "Skyrim:Iron Arrow"), [steel](/wiki/Skyrim:Steel_Arrow "Skyrim:Steel Arrow"), [orcish](/wiki/Skyrim:Orcish_Arrow "Skyrim:Orcish Arrow"), [dwarven](/wiki/Skyrim:Dwarven_Arrow "Skyrim:Dwarven Arrow"), or [elven arrows](/wiki/Skyrim:Elven_Arrow "Skyrim:Elven Arrow"), depending on their level.

| Name | PC Level | NPC Level | [ID](/wiki/Skyrim:Form_ID "Skyrim:Form ID") | [Health](/wiki/File:SkyrimTAG-icon-Health.png "Health") | [Magicka](/wiki/File:SkyrimTAG-icon-Magicka.png "Magicka") | [Stamina](/wiki/File:SkyrimTAG-icon-Stamina.png "Stamina") |

| Dremora Markynaz | 36 | 36 | 00016ff6 | 435 | 50 | 190 |
| Dremora Valkynaz | 46 | 46 | 00016ff9 | 545 | 50 | 230 |

### Warlocks

Dremora warlocks are members of the [Destruction Mage](/wiki/Skyrim:CombatMageDestruction "Skyrim:CombatMageDestruction") NPC class and prefer to use spells in combat. They wear unique [black robes and boots](/wiki/Skyrim:Specialty_Gear#Dremora_Equipment "Skyrim:Specialty Gear"). In case they are forced into melee combat, they carry an iron dagger and a mace, sword, war axe, warhammer, greatsword, or battleaxe (any quality from iron to elven).

A Dremora warlock wielding fire

### Summonable Dremora Lord

A Dremora Lord

A Dremora Lord can be summoned using either [Conjure Dremora Lord](/wiki/Skyrim:Conjure_Dremora_Lord "Skyrim:Conjure Dremora Lord"), an Expert level Conjuration spell or the [Sanguine Rose](/wiki/Skyrim:Sanguine_Rose "Skyrim:Sanguine Rose"). The Dremora Lord is a Dremora Valynaz, a melee fighter equipped with the standard unique Daedric armor that wields a [Daedric Greatsword of the Inferno](/wiki/Skyrim:Generic_Magic_Weapons#of_the_Inferno "Skyrim:Generic Magic Weapons").

The Dremora Lord has 545 health and 230 stamina. [Dragon Priests](/wiki/Skyrim:Undead#Dragon_Priests "Skyrim:Undead") cannot take control of conjured Dremora Lords. Furthermore, while the Dremora Lord is technically not an [Atronach](/wiki/Skyrim:Daedra "Skyrim:Daedra"), it is affected by the [Summoner](/wiki/Skyrim:Summoner "Skyrim:Summoner") and [Atromancy](/wiki/Skyrim:Atromancy "Skyrim:Atromancy") Conjuration perks, although it is **not** affected by [Elemental Potency](/wiki/Skyrim:Elemental_Potency "Skyrim:Elemental Potency"). The [Twin Souls](/wiki/Skyrim:Twin_Souls "Skyrim:Twin Souls") perk also applies to Dremora Lords, making it possible to have both a Dremora Lord and an [atronach](/wiki/Skyrim:Atronach "Skyrim:Atronach") or [thrall](/wiki/Skyrim:Thrall "Skyrim:Thrall"), or two Dremora Lords. Unlike other NPC Dremoras, Dremora Lords cannot be [pickpocketed](/wiki/Skyrim:Pickpocket "Skyrim:Pickpocket") for weapons or armor, and they will not drop Daedra Hearts because their bodies disappear upon death. They are also immune to [all Soul Trap effects](/wiki/Skyrim:Soul_Trap_(effect) "Skyrim:Soul Trap (effect)").

#### Dremora Lord Dialogue

| In combat | After defeating an enemy | After spotting an enemy | After losing sight of an enemy | After being defeated |
| --- | --- | --- | --- | --- |
| - *"I will feast on your heart."* - *"I honor my lord by destroying you!"* - *"You are weak, mortal."* - *"Are you prepared for your death?"* - *"Oblivion take you!"* - *"You will bleed!"* - *"Fall before me!"* | - *"No match at all."* - *"There could be no other end."* | - *"I smell weakness..."* - *"A challenger is near..."* - *"Another who seeks death."* - *"There you are weakling!"* - *"You meet your end, mortal."* - *"No one escapes!"* - *"Now you suffer!"* - *"You return, foolish mortal?"* | - *"Hiding will not save you now."* - *"You cannot escape me!"* - *"Quiet again."* - *"Nothing after all."* | - *"No... not by a mortal..."* - *"It cannot... end like this..."* |

## Notes

- In the [Creation Kit](/wiki/Skyrim_Mod:Creation_Kit "Skyrim Mod:Creation Kit"), you can see that the Dremora race uses the [Dark Elf](/wiki/Skyrim:Dark_Elf "Skyrim:Dark Elf") race as a base, with the only changes being: horns, their own unique skin tone (dark with red facial markings), unique eyes, and their in-game height being equal to that of the [High Elf](/wiki/Skyrim:High_Elf "Skyrim:High Elf").
- Although there is an Archer class for Dremora, they do not appear in the game; only the melee fighters and mages can be encountered.
- The Daedric Prince [Sanguine](/wiki/Skyrim:Sanguine "Skyrim:Sanguine") appears in the form of a Dremora.
- Several human NPCs are [classified](/wiki/Category:Skyrim-Dremora_Class "Category:Skyrim-Dremora Class") in the game data as Dremora, due to that class being used as a default value.
- Seven of the Dremora dialogue lines appear in the book *[I Was Summoned by a Mortal](/wiki/Online:I_was_Summoned_by_a_Mortal "Online:I was Summoned by a Mortal")* in [ESO](/wiki/Online:Online "Online:Online").

## Bugs

- The aforementioned Archer Dremora were given Nord voices rather than the voices given to Melee and Warlock Dremora. **?**
- Dremora may not voice their death quotes when they die; only pained grunts or yells are heard, instead.
- Reanimated Dremora may equip invisible items in their hands if they were placed on the corpse before reanimation took place.
  - The [Unofficial Skyrim Special Edition Patch](/wiki/Skyrim_Mod:Unofficial_Skyrim_Special_Edition_Patch "Skyrim Mod:Unofficial Skyrim Special Edition Patch"), version 4.1.1, fixes this bug.

- ***[Spirit of the Daedra](/wiki/Skyrim:Spirit_of_the_Daedra "Skyrim:Spirit of the Daedra")*** — A look into the Daedric mindset
- ***[There Be Dragons](/wiki/Skyrim:There_Be_Dragons "Skyrim:There Be Dragons")*** by [Torhal Bjorik](/wiki/Lore:Books_by_Author#Torhal_Bjorik "Lore:Books by Author") — A report on the nature of dragons
- ***[A Tragedy in Black](/wiki/Skyrim:A_Tragedy_in_Black "Skyrim:A Tragedy in Black")*** — The story of a youth summoning a Dremora
- ***[Varieties of Daedra](/wiki/Skyrim:Varieties_of_Daedra "Skyrim:Varieties of Daedra")*** by [Aranea Drethan](/wiki/Lore:Books_by_Author#Aranea_Drethan "Lore:Books by Author") — An analysis of Daedra forms, focusing primarily on the Dremora

# Skyrim:Dremora

## Overview

Dremora at the Shrine of Mehrunes Dagon

**Dremora** are humanoid [Daedra](/wiki/Skyrim:Daedra "Skyrim:Daedra"). They are often very intelligent and are generally hostile. In [lore](/wiki/Lore:Dremora "Lore:Dremora"), it is said they can be found in clans of large numbers in the wastes of [Oblivion](/wiki/Lore:Oblivion "Lore:Oblivion"). Dremora are grouped into several different castes: Churl, Caitiff, Kynval, Kynreeve, Kynmarcher, Markynaz, and Valkynaz. Dremora are a rare sight in Skyrim, only appearing as summoned creatures and in a few set locations, such as the [Shrine of Mehrunes Dagon](/wiki/Skyrim:Shrine_of_Mehrunes_Dagon "Skyrim:Shrine of Mehrunes Dagon"), [Shalidor's Maze](/wiki/Skyrim:Shalidor%27s_Maze "Skyrim:Shalidor's Maze"), [Azura's Star Interior](/wiki/Skyrim:Azura%27s_Star_Interior "Skyrim:Azura's Star Interior"), and the [Deadlands](/wiki/Skyrim:Deadlands "Skyrim:Deadlands")[CC](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Cause "Skyrim:The Cause").

The other way to encounter Dremora in Skyrim is by summoning one. There are a few ways to summon Dremora:

- The [Sanguine Rose](/wiki/Skyrim:Sanguine_Rose "Skyrim:Sanguine Rose"), a reward from the quest [A Night To Remember](/wiki/Skyrim:A_Night_To_Remember "Skyrim:A Night To Remember"), will summon a leveled melee fighter Dremora for 60 seconds, or 120 seconds with the appropriate Conjuration perks.
- The [Conjuration](/wiki/Skyrim:Conjuration "Skyrim:Conjuration") spell [Conjure Dremora Lord](/wiki/Skyrim:Conjure_Dremora_Lord "Skyrim:Conjure Dremora Lord") will summon a [Dremora Lord](#Dremora_Lord) for 60 seconds, or 120 seconds with the appropriate Conjuration perks.
- The [Atronach Forge](/wiki/Skyrim:Atronach_Forge "Skyrim:Atronach Forge") can be used to summon hostile Dremora, which will obviously attack anybody or anything on sight.
- The [Conjuration Ritual Spell](/wiki/Skyrim:Conjuration_Ritual_Spell "Skyrim:Conjuration Ritual Spell") quest involves summoning an [Unbound Dremora](/wiki/Skyrim:Unbound_Dremora "Skyrim:Unbound Dremora"); this Dremora cannot be summoned anywhere other than the roof of the [Hall of Attainment](/wiki/Skyrim:Hall_of_Attainment "Skyrim:Hall of Attainment"). Once again, this will be automatically hostile to everything it encounters.
- The [Wabbajack](/wiki/Skyrim:Wabbajack "Skyrim:Wabbajack") has a chance to momentarily turn the target into a hostile Dremora.

## Dremora Types

There are three types of Dremora, based on their preferred fighting style: melee fighters, archers, and warlocks. All Dremora are [NPCs](/wiki/Skyrim:NPCs "Skyrim:NPCs") with [black souls](/wiki/Skyrim:Souls "Skyrim:Souls"). All types of Dremora always drop a [Daedra Heart](/wiki/Skyrim:Daedra_Heart "Skyrim:Daedra Heart") on death; they're one of the few guaranteed sources of this rare ingredient.

### Melee Fighters

These Dremora belong to the [Dremora](/wiki/Skyrim:Dremora_(class) "Skyrim:Dremora (class)") NPC [class](/wiki/Skyrim:Classes "Skyrim:Classes") and use one or two-handed weapons in battle. They wear a [unique version](/wiki/Skyrim:Specialty_Gear#Dremora_Equipment "Skyrim:Specialty Gear") of [Daedric Armor](/wiki/Skyrim:Daedric_Armor "Skyrim:Daedric Armor") available only to Dremora and wield a leveled [mace](/wiki/Skyrim:Mace "Skyrim:Mace"), [sword](/wiki/Skyrim:Sword "Skyrim:Sword"), [war axe](/wiki/Skyrim:War_Axe "Skyrim:War Axe"), [warhammer](/wiki/Skyrim:Greatsword "Skyrim:Greatsword"), [greatsword](/wiki/Skyrim:Greatsword "Skyrim:Greatsword"), or [battleaxe](/wiki/Skyrim:Battleaxe "Skyrim:Battleaxe"), all of which are enchanted with [fire damage](/wiki/Skyrim:Fire_Damage "Skyrim:Fire Damage"). The type of enchantment depends on the quality of the material, as follows:

- **[Iron](/wiki/Skyrim:Iron "Skyrim:Iron") or [steel](/wiki/Skyrim:Steel "Skyrim:Steel"):** [of Embers](/wiki/Skyrim:Generic_Magic_Weapons#of_Embers "Skyrim:Generic Magic Weapons"), [of Burning](/wiki/Skyrim:Generic_Magic_Weapons#of_Burning "Skyrim:Generic Magic Weapons"), [of Scorching](/wiki/Skyrim:Generic_Magic_Weapons#of_Scorching "Skyrim:Generic Magic Weapons")
- **[Glass](/wiki/Skyrim:Malachite "Skyrim:Malachite"):** of Scorching, [of Fire](/wiki/Skyrim:Generic_Magic_Weapons#of_Fire "Skyrim:Generic Magic Weapons"), [of the Blaze](/wiki/Skyrim:Generic_Magic_Weapons#of_the_Blaze "Skyrim:Generic Magic Weapons")
- **[Ebony](/wiki/Skyrim:Ebony "Skyrim:Ebony") or [Daedric](/wiki/Skyrim:Daedric "Skyrim:Daedric"):** of Fire, of the Blaze, [of the Inferno](/wiki/Skyrim:Generic_Magic_Weapons#of_the_Inferno "Skyrim:Generic Magic Weapons")

They also carry an [iron dagger](/wiki/Skyrim:Iron_Dagger "Skyrim:Iron Dagger") and will drop a Daedra Heart on death.

A Dremora warrior wielding a steel war axe

[^1](#note_DremoraLord)This Dremora is also the template used for the [Dremora Lord](#Dremora_Lord) summoned with Conjure Dremora Lord.

### Archers

These Dremora have the [Bandit](/wiki/Skyrim:Bandit_(class) "Skyrim:Bandit (class)") NPC class and wield fire-enchanted bows to fight from a distance. They wear the same unique Daedric Armor as their melee counterparts and use one of the following enchanted bows:

- **[Hunting Bow](/wiki/Skyrim:Hunting_Bow "Skyrim:Hunting Bow"):** of Embers, of Burning, of Scorching
- **[Glass Bow](/wiki/Skyrim:Glass_Bow "Skyrim:Glass Bow"):** of Scorching, of Fire, of the Blaze
- **[Ebony](/wiki/Skyrim:Ebony_Bow "Skyrim:Ebony Bow") or [Daedric Bow](/wiki/Skyrim:Daedric "Skyrim:Daedric"):** of Fire, of the Blaze, of the Inferno

They also carry an iron dagger, one iron arrow, and a quiver of up to 20 [iron](/wiki/Skyrim:Iron_Arrow "Skyrim:Iron Arrow"), [steel](/wiki/Skyrim:Steel_Arrow "Skyrim:Steel Arrow"), [orcish](/wiki/Skyrim:Orcish_Arrow "Skyrim:Orcish Arrow"), [dwarven](/wiki/Skyrim:Dwarven_Arrow "Skyrim:Dwarven Arrow"), or [elven arrows](/wiki/Skyrim:Elven_Arrow "Skyrim:Elven Arrow"), depending on their level.

| Name | PC Level | NPC Level | [ID](/wiki/Skyrim:Form_ID "Skyrim:Form ID") | [Health](/wiki/File:SkyrimTAG-icon-Health.png "Health") | [Magicka](/wiki/File:SkyrimTAG-icon-Magicka.png "Magicka") | [Stamina](/wiki/File:SkyrimTAG-icon-Stamina.png "Stamina") |
| --- | --- | --- | --- | --- | --- | --- |
| Dremora Churl | 1 | 6 | 00025d1c | 105 | 50 | 70 |
| Dremora Caitiff | 12 | 12 | 00016ef6 | 171 | 50 | 94 |
| Dremora Kynval | 19 | 19 | 00016f46 | 248 | 50 | 122 |
| Dremora Kynreeve | 27 | 27 | 00016fe2 | 336 | 50 | 154 |
| Dremora Markynaz | 36 | 36 | 00016ff6 | 435 | 50 | 190 |
| Dremora Valkynaz | 46 | 46 | 00016ff9 | 545 | 50 | 230 |

### Warlocks

Dremora warlocks are members of the [Destruction Mage](/wiki/Skyrim:CombatMageDestruction "Skyrim:CombatMageDestruction") NPC class and prefer to use spells in combat. They wear unique [black robes and boots](/wiki/Skyrim:Specialty_Gear#Dremora_Equipment "Skyrim:Specialty Gear"). In case they are forced into melee combat, they carry an iron dagger and a mace, sword, war axe, warhammer, greatsword, or battleaxe (any quality from iron to elven).

A Dremora warlock wielding fire

### Summonable Dremora Lord

A Dremora Lord

A Dremora Lord can be summoned using either [Conjure Dremora Lord](/wiki/Skyrim:Conjure_Dremora_Lord "Skyrim:Conjure Dremora Lord"), an Expert level Conjuration spell or the [Sanguine Rose](/wiki/Skyrim:Sanguine_Rose "Skyrim:Sanguine Rose"). The Dremora Lord is a Dremora Valynaz, a melee fighter equipped with the standard unique Daedric armor that wields a [Daedric Greatsword of the Inferno](/wiki/Skyrim:Generic_Magic_Weapons#of_the_Inferno "Skyrim:Generic Magic Weapons").

The Dremora Lord has 545 health and 230 stamina. [Dragon Priests](/wiki/Skyrim:Undead#Dragon_Priests "Skyrim:Undead") cannot take control of conjured Dremora Lords. Furthermore, while the Dremora Lord is technically not an [Atronach](/wiki/Skyrim:Daedra "Skyrim:Daedra"), it is affected by the [Summoner](/wiki/Skyrim:Summoner "Skyrim:Summoner") and [Atromancy](/wiki/Skyrim:Atromancy "Skyrim:Atromancy") Conjuration perks, although it is **not** affected by [Elemental Potency](/wiki/Skyrim:Elemental_Potency "Skyrim:Elemental Potency"). The [Twin Souls](/wiki/Skyrim:Twin_Souls "Skyrim:Twin Souls") perk also applies to Dremora Lords, making it possible to have both a Dremora Lord and an [atronach](/wiki/Skyrim:Atronach "Skyrim:Atronach") or [thrall](/wiki/Skyrim:Thrall "Skyrim:Thrall"), or two Dremora Lords. Unlike other NPC Dremoras, Dremora Lords cannot be [pickpocketed](/wiki/Skyrim:Pickpocket "Skyrim:Pickpocket") for weapons or armor, and they will not drop Daedra Hearts because their bodies disappear upon death. They are also immune to [all Soul Trap effects](/wiki/Skyrim:Soul_Trap_(effect) "Skyrim:Soul Trap (effect)").

#### Dremora Lord Dialogue

| In combat | After defeating an enemy | After spotting an enemy | After losing sight of an enemy | After being defeated |
| --- | --- | --- | --- | --- |
| - *"I will feast on your heart."* - *"I honor my lord by destroying you!"* - *"You are weak, mortal."* - *"Are you prepared for your death?"* - *"Oblivion take you!"* - *"You will bleed!"* - *"Fall before me!"* | - *"No match at all."* - *"There could be no other end."* | - *"I smell weakness..."* - *"A challenger is near..."* - *"Another who seeks death."* - *"There you are weakling!"* - *"You meet your end, mortal."* - *"No one escapes!"* - *"Now you suffer!"* - *"You return, foolish mortal?"* | - *"Hiding will not save you now."* - *"You cannot escape me!"* - *"Quiet again."* - *"Nothing after all."* | - *"No... not by a mortal..."* - *"It cannot... end like this..."* |

## Notes

- In the [Creation Kit](/wiki/Skyrim_Mod:Creation_Kit "Skyrim Mod:Creation Kit"), you can see that the Dremora race uses the [Dark Elf](/wiki/Skyrim:Dark_Elf "Skyrim:Dark Elf") race as a base, with the only changes being: horns, their own unique skin tone (dark with red facial markings), unique eyes, and their in-game height being equal to that of the [High Elf](/wiki/Skyrim:High_Elf "Skyrim:High Elf").
- Although there is an Archer class for Dremora, they do not appear in the game; only the melee fighters and mages can be encountered.
- The Daedric Prince [Sanguine](/wiki/Skyrim:Sanguine "Skyrim:Sanguine") appears in the form of a Dremora.
- Several human NPCs are [classified](/wiki/Category:Skyrim-Dremora_Class "Category:Skyrim-Dremora Class") in the game data as Dremora, due to that class being used as a default value.
- Seven of the Dremora dialogue lines appear in the book *[I Was Summoned by a Mortal](/wiki/Online:I_was_Summoned_by_a_Mortal "Online:I was Summoned by a Mortal")* in [ESO](/wiki/Online:Online "Online:Online").

## Bugs

- The aforementioned Archer Dremora were given Nord voices rather than the voices given to Melee and Warlock Dremora. **?**
- Dremora may not voice their death quotes when they die; only pained grunts or yells are heard, instead.
- Reanimated Dremora may equip invisible items in their hands if they were placed on the corpse before reanimation took place.
  - The [Unofficial Skyrim Special Edition Patch](/wiki/Skyrim_Mod:Unofficial_Skyrim_Special_Edition_Patch "Skyrim Mod:Unofficial Skyrim Special Edition Patch"), version 4.1.1, fixes this bug.

- ***[There Be Dragons](/wiki/Skyrim:There_Be_Dragons "Skyrim:There Be Dragons")*** by [Torhal Bjorik](/wiki/Lore:Books_by_Author#Torhal_Bjorik "Lore:Books by Author") — A report on the nature of dragons

- ***[Varieties of Daedra](/wiki/Skyrim:Varieties_of_Daedra "Skyrim:Varieties of Daedra")*** by [Aranea Drethan](/wiki/Lore:Books_by_Author#Aranea_Drethan "Lore:Books by Author") — An analysis of Daedra forms, focusing primarily on the Dremora

# Skyrim:Dremora

## Overview

Dremora at the Shrine of Mehrunes Dagon

**Dremora** are humanoid [Daedra](/wiki/Skyrim:Daedra "Skyrim:Daedra"). They are often very intelligent and are generally hostile. In [lore](/wiki/Lore:Dremora "Lore:Dremora"), it is said they can be found in clans of large numbers in the wastes of [Oblivion](/wiki/Lore:Oblivion "Lore:Oblivion"). Dremora are grouped into several different castes: Churl, Caitiff, Kynval, Kynreeve, Kynmarcher, Markynaz, and Valkynaz. Dremora are a rare sight in Skyrim, only appearing as summoned creatures and in a few set locations, such as the [Shrine of Mehrunes Dagon](/wiki/Skyrim:Shrine_of_Mehrunes_Dagon "Skyrim:Shrine of Mehrunes Dagon"), [Shalidor's Maze](/wiki/Skyrim:Shalidor%27s_Maze "Skyrim:Shalidor's Maze"), [Azura's Star Interior](/wiki/Skyrim:Azura%27s_Star_Interior "Skyrim:Azura's Star Interior"), and the [Deadlands](/wiki/Skyrim:Deadlands "Skyrim:Deadlands")[CC](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Cause "Skyrim:The Cause").

The other way to encounter Dremora in Skyrim is by summoning one. There are a few ways to summon Dremora:

- The [Sanguine Rose](/wiki/Skyrim:Sanguine_Rose "Skyrim:Sanguine Rose"), a reward from the quest [A Night To Remember](/wiki/Skyrim:A_Night_To_Remember "Skyrim:A Night To Remember"), will summon a leveled melee fighter Dremora for 60 seconds, or 120 seconds with the appropriate Conjuration perks.
- The [Conjuration](/wiki/Skyrim:Conjuration "Skyrim:Conjuration") spell [Conjure Dremora Lord](/wiki/Skyrim:Conjure_Dremora_Lord "Skyrim:Conjure Dremora Lord") will summon a [Dremora Lord](#Dremora_Lord) for 60 seconds, or 120 seconds with the appropriate Conjuration perks.
- The [Atronach Forge](/wiki/Skyrim:Atronach_Forge "Skyrim:Atronach Forge") can be used to summon hostile Dremora, which will obviously attack anybody or anything on sight.
- The [Conjuration Ritual Spell](/wiki/Skyrim:Conjuration_Ritual_Spell "Skyrim:Conjuration Ritual Spell") quest involves summoning an [Unbound Dremora](/wiki/Skyrim:Unbound_Dremora "Skyrim:Unbound Dremora"); this Dremora cannot be summoned anywhere other than the roof of the [Hall of Attainment](/wiki/Skyrim:Hall_of_Attainment "Skyrim:Hall of Attainment"). Once again, this will be automatically hostile to everything it encounters.
- The [Wabbajack](/wiki/Skyrim:Wabbajack "Skyrim:Wabbajack") has a chance to momentarily turn the target into a hostile Dremora.

## Dremora Types

There are three types of Dremora, based on their preferred fighting style: melee fighters, archers, and warlocks. All Dremora are [NPCs](/wiki/Skyrim:NPCs "Skyrim:NPCs") with [black souls](/wiki/Skyrim:Souls "Skyrim:Souls"). All types of Dremora always drop a [Daedra Heart](/wiki/Skyrim:Daedra_Heart "Skyrim:Daedra Heart") on death; they're one of the few guaranteed sources of this rare ingredient.

### Melee Fighters

These Dremora belong to the [Dremora](/wiki/Skyrim:Dremora_(class) "Skyrim:Dremora (class)") NPC [class](/wiki/Skyrim:Classes "Skyrim:Classes") and use one or two-handed weapons in battle. They wear a [unique version](/wiki/Skyrim:Specialty_Gear#Dremora_Equipment "Skyrim:Specialty Gear") of [Daedric Armor](/wiki/Skyrim:Daedric_Armor "Skyrim:Daedric Armor") available only to Dremora and wield a leveled [mace](/wiki/Skyrim:Mace "Skyrim:Mace"), [sword](/wiki/Skyrim:Sword "Skyrim:Sword"), [war axe](/wiki/Skyrim:War_Axe "Skyrim:War Axe"), [warhammer](/wiki/Skyrim:Greatsword "Skyrim:Greatsword"), [greatsword](/wiki/Skyrim:Greatsword "Skyrim:Greatsword"), or [battleaxe](/wiki/Skyrim:Battleaxe "Skyrim:Battleaxe"), all of which are enchanted with [fire damage](/wiki/Skyrim:Fire_Damage "Skyrim:Fire Damage"). The type of enchantment depends on the quality of the material, as follows:

- **[Iron](/wiki/Skyrim:Iron "Skyrim:Iron") or [steel](/wiki/Skyrim:Steel "Skyrim:Steel"):** [of Embers](/wiki/Skyrim:Generic_Magic_Weapons#of_Embers "Skyrim:Generic Magic Weapons"), [of Burning](/wiki/Skyrim:Generic_Magic_Weapons#of_Burning "Skyrim:Generic Magic Weapons"), [of Scorching](/wiki/Skyrim:Generic_Magic_Weapons#of_Scorching "Skyrim:Generic Magic Weapons")
- **[Glass](/wiki/Skyrim:Malachite "Skyrim:Malachite"):** of Scorching, [of Fire](/wiki/Skyrim:Generic_Magic_Weapons#of_Fire "Skyrim:Generic Magic Weapons"), [of the Blaze](/wiki/Skyrim:Generic_Magic_Weapons#of_the_Blaze "Skyrim:Generic Magic Weapons")
- **[Ebony](/wiki/Skyrim:Ebony "Skyrim:Ebony") or [Daedric](/wiki/Skyrim:Daedric "Skyrim:Daedric"):** of Fire, of the Blaze, [of the Inferno](/wiki/Skyrim:Generic_Magic_Weapons#of_the_Inferno "Skyrim:Generic Magic Weapons")

They also carry an [iron dagger](/wiki/Skyrim:Iron_Dagger "Skyrim:Iron Dagger") and will drop a Daedra Heart on death.

[^1](#note_DremoraLord)This Dremora is also the template used for the [Dremora Lord](#Dremora_Lord) summoned with Conjure Dremora Lord.

### Archers

These Dremora have the [Bandit](/wiki/Skyrim:Bandit_(class) "Skyrim:Bandit (class)") NPC class and wield fire-enchanted bows to fight from a distance. They wear the same unique Daedric Armor as their melee counterparts and use one of the following enchanted bows:

- **[Hunting Bow](/wiki/Skyrim:Hunting_Bow "Skyrim:Hunting Bow"):** of Embers, of Burning, of Scorching
- **[Glass Bow](/wiki/Skyrim:Glass_Bow "Skyrim:Glass Bow"):** of Scorching, of Fire, of the Blaze
- **[Ebony](/wiki/Skyrim:Ebony_Bow "Skyrim:Ebony Bow") or [Daedric Bow](/wiki/Skyrim:Daedric "Skyrim:Daedric"):** of Fire, of the Blaze, of the Inferno

They also carry an iron dagger, one iron arrow, and a quiver of up to 20 [iron](/wiki/Skyrim:Iron_Arrow "Skyrim:Iron Arrow"), [steel](/wiki/Skyrim:Steel_Arrow "Skyrim:Steel Arrow"), [orcish](/wiki/Skyrim:Orcish_Arrow "Skyrim:Orcish Arrow"), [dwarven](/wiki/Skyrim:Dwarven_Arrow "Skyrim:Dwarven Arrow"), or [elven arrows](/wiki/Skyrim:Elven_Arrow "Skyrim:Elven Arrow"), depending on their level.

| Name | PC Level | NPC Level | [ID](/wiki/Skyrim:Form_ID "Skyrim:Form ID") | [Health](/wiki/File:SkyrimTAG-icon-Health.png "Health") | [Magicka](/wiki/File:SkyrimTAG-icon-Magicka.png "Magicka") | [Stamina](/wiki/File:SkyrimTAG-icon-Stamina.png "Stamina") |

| Dremora Valkynaz | 46 | 46 | 00016ff9 | 545 | 50 | 230 |

### Warlocks

Dremora warlocks are members of the [Destruction Mage](/wiki/Skyrim:CombatMageDestruction "Skyrim:CombatMageDestruction") NPC class and prefer to use spells in combat. They wear unique [black robes and boots](/wiki/Skyrim:Specialty_Gear#Dremora_Equipment "Skyrim:Specialty Gear"). In case they are forced into melee combat, they carry an iron dagger and a mace, sword, war axe, warhammer, greatsword, or battleaxe (any quality from iron to elven).

A Dremora warlock wielding fire

### Summonable Dremora Lord

A Dremora Lord

A Dremora Lord can be summoned using either [Conjure Dremora Lord](/wiki/Skyrim:Conjure_Dremora_Lord "Skyrim:Conjure Dremora Lord"), an Expert level Conjuration spell or the [Sanguine Rose](/wiki/Skyrim:Sanguine_Rose "Skyrim:Sanguine Rose"). The Dremora Lord is a Dremora Valynaz, a melee fighter equipped with the standard unique Daedric armor that wields a [Daedric Greatsword of the Inferno](/wiki/Skyrim:Generic_Magic_Weapons#of_the_Inferno "Skyrim:Generic Magic Weapons").

The Dremora Lord has 545 health and 230 stamina. [Dragon Priests](/wiki/Skyrim:Undead#Dragon_Priests "Skyrim:Undead") cannot take control of conjured Dremora Lords. Furthermore, while the Dremora Lord is technically not an [Atronach](/wiki/Skyrim:Daedra "Skyrim:Daedra"), it is affected by the [Summoner](/wiki/Skyrim:Summoner "Skyrim:Summoner") and [Atromancy](/wiki/Skyrim:Atromancy "Skyrim:Atromancy") Conjuration perks, although it is **not** affected by [Elemental Potency](/wiki/Skyrim:Elemental_Potency "Skyrim:Elemental Potency"). The [Twin Souls](/wiki/Skyrim:Twin_Souls "Skyrim:Twin Souls") perk also applies to Dremora Lords, making it possible to have both a Dremora Lord and an [atronach](/wiki/Skyrim:Atronach "Skyrim:Atronach") or [thrall](/wiki/Skyrim:Thrall "Skyrim:Thrall"), or two Dremora Lords. Unlike other NPC Dremoras, Dremora Lords cannot be [pickpocketed](/wiki/Skyrim:Pickpocket "Skyrim:Pickpocket") for weapons or armor, and they will not drop Daedra Hearts because their bodies disappear upon death. They are also immune to [all Soul Trap effects](/wiki/Skyrim:Soul_Trap_(effect) "Skyrim:Soul Trap (effect)").

#### Dremora Lord Dialogue

| In combat | After defeating an enemy | After spotting an enemy | After losing sight of an enemy | After being defeated |
| --- | --- | --- | --- | --- |
| - *"I will feast on your heart."* - *"I honor my lord by destroying you!"* - *"You are weak, mortal."* - *"Are you prepared for your death?"* - *"Oblivion take you!"* - *"You will bleed!"* - *"Fall before me!"* | - *"No match at all."* - *"There could be no other end."* | - *"I smell weakness..."* - *"A challenger is near..."* - *"Another who seeks death."* - *"There you are weakling!"* - *"You meet your end, mortal."* - *"No one escapes!"* - *"Now you suffer!"* - *"You return, foolish mortal?"* | - *"Hiding will not save you now."* - *"You cannot escape me!"* - *"Quiet again."* - *"Nothing after all."* | - *"No... not by a mortal..."* - *"It cannot... end like this..."* |

## Notes

- In the [Creation Kit](/wiki/Skyrim_Mod:Creation_Kit "Skyrim Mod:Creation Kit"), you can see that the Dremora race uses the [Dark Elf](/wiki/Skyrim:Dark_Elf "Skyrim:Dark Elf") race as a base, with the only changes being: horns, their own unique skin tone (dark with red facial markings), unique eyes, and their in-game height being equal to that of the [High Elf](/wiki/Skyrim:High_Elf "Skyrim:High Elf").
- Although there is an Archer class for Dremora, they do not appear in the game; only the melee fighters and mages can be encountered.
- The Daedric Prince [Sanguine](/wiki/Skyrim:Sanguine "Skyrim:Sanguine") appears in the form of a Dremora.
- Several human NPCs are [classified](/wiki/Category:Skyrim-Dremora_Class "Category:Skyrim-Dremora Class") in the game data as Dremora, due to that class being used as a default value.
- Seven of the Dremora dialogue lines appear in the book *[I Was Summoned by a Mortal](/wiki/Online:I_was_Summoned_by_a_Mortal "Online:I was Summoned by a Mortal")* in [ESO](/wiki/Online:Online "Online:Online").

## Bugs

- The aforementioned Archer Dremora were given Nord voices rather than the voices given to Melee and Warlock Dremora. **?**
- Dremora may not voice their death quotes when they die; only pained grunts or yells are heard, instead.
- Reanimated Dremora may equip invisible items in their hands if they were placed on the corpse before reanimation took place.
  - The [Unofficial Skyrim Special Edition Patch](/wiki/Skyrim_Mod:Unofficial_Skyrim_Special_Edition_Patch "Skyrim Mod:Unofficial Skyrim Special Edition Patch"), version 4.1.1, fixes this bug.

### Books

- ***[Darkest Darkness](/wiki/Skyrim:Darkest_Darkness "Skyrim:Darkest Darkness")*** — A description of various Daedra
- ***[Spirit of the Daedra](/wiki/Skyrim:Spirit_of_the_Daedra "Skyrim:Spirit of the Daedra")*** — A look into the Daedric mindset
- ***[There Be Dragons](/wiki/Skyrim:There_Be_Dragons "Skyrim:There Be Dragons")*** by [Torhal Bjorik](/wiki/Lore:Books_by_Author#Torhal_Bjorik "Lore:Books by Author") — A report on the nature of dragons
- ***[A Tragedy in Black](/wiki/Skyrim:A_Tragedy_in_Black "Skyrim:A Tragedy in Black")*** — The story of a youth summoning a Dremora
- ***[Varieties of Daedra](/wiki/Skyrim:Varieties_of_Daedra "Skyrim:Varieties of Daedra")*** by [Aranea Drethan](/wiki/Lore:Books_by_Author#Aranea_Drethan "Lore:Books by Author") — An analysis of Daedra forms, focusing primarily on the Dremora
